## UNDERGRADUATE

## CATALOG 2025-2026

ANDERSON UNIVERSITY

The Ĥateŋial coĥtaiĥed iĥ the Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Uĥdeŋgŋaduate Catalog is foŋ iĥfoŋĤatioĥ oĥlŽ aĥd does ĥot coĥstitute a coĥtŋact betŷeeĥ the studeĥt aĥd the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ. The catalog pŋoŶides aĥ oŶeŋŶieŷ of couŋse offeŋiĥgs aĥd coĥteĥt. It is ĥot the official list of offeŋiĥgs foŋ aĥŽ giŶeĥ teŋĤ. Studeĥts should coĥsult the couŋse schedule foŋ the specific teŋĤǜsǝ foŋ ŷhich theŽ ŷish to ŋegisteŋ. The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ aĥd its Ŷaŋious uĥits ŋeseŋŶe the ŋight to ŋeŶise, aĤeĥd, alteŋ, aĥd chaĥge fŋoĤ tiĤe to tiĤe its policies, ŋules, ŋegulatioĥs, aĥd fiĥaĥcial chaŋges, iĥcludiĥg those ŋelated to adĤissioĥ, iĥstŋuctioĥ, aĥd gŋaduatioĥ, ŷithout ĥotice to studeĥts. The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋeseŋŶes the ŋight to ŷithdŋaŷ cuŋŋicula aĥd specific couŋses, alteŋ couŋse coĥteĥt, chaĥge the caleĥdaŋ, aĥd ŷithdŋaŷ oŋ chaĥge pŋogŋaĤs aĥd Ĥajoŋs offeŋed bŽ the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷithout ĥotice to studeĥts.

Aĥdeŋsoĥ  UĥiŶeŋsitŽ  Ĥaiĥtaiĥs  coĤpliaĥce  ŷith  applicable  Fedeŋal  aĥd  State  statutes  ŋelated  to pŋiŶate iĥstitutioĥs of higheŋ educatioĥ iĥcludiĥg the FaĤilŽ Educatioĥal Rights aĥd PŋiŶacŽ Act ǜFERPAǝ, as aĤeĥdedǎ the Studeĥt Right to Kĥoŷ Act, as aĤeĥdedǎ aĥd the SoloĤoĥ AĤeĥdĤeĥt. Iĥ coĤpliaĥce ŷith the CiŶil Rights Act of ƐƘƕƓ aĥd ƐƘƘƐ, Title IX of the Educatioĥal AĤeĥdĤeĥts of ƐƘƖƑ, Sectioĥ ƔƏƓ of the Rehabilitatioĥ Act of ƐƘƖƒ aĥd the AĤeŋicaĥs ŷith Disabilities Act of ƐƘƘƏ as aĤeĥded, the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ does ĥot discŋiĤiĥate iĥ its educatioĥal pŋogŋaĤs  oŋ  adĤissioĥ  pŋoceduŋes.  Aĥdeŋsoĥ  UĥiŶeŋsitŽ  is  a  ĥot-foŋ-pŋofit  eżeĤpt  oŋgaĥizatioĥ  as  descŋibed  iĥ  Sectioĥ  ƔƏƐǜcǝǜƒǝ of the Iĥteŋĥal ReŶeĥue Code. The folloŷiĥg iĥdiŶiduals haŶe beeĥ desigĥated to haĥdle iĥŊuiŋies ŋegaŋdiĥg ĥoĥ-discŋiĤiĥatioĥ policiesǍ Diŋectoŋ of Woŋk Life EĥgageĤeĥt, ƐƐƏƏ East Fifth St., Aĥdeŋsoĥ, IN ƓƕƏƐƑ, telephoĥe ǜƖƕƔǝ ƕƓƐ-ƓƐƒƒǎ aĥd Diŋectoŋ foŋ Studeĥt AccessibilitŽ SeŋŶices, ƐƐƏƏ East Fifth St., Aĥdeŋsoĥ, IN ƓƕƏƐƑ, telephoĥe ǜƖƕƔǝ ƕƓƐ-ƓƑƑƒ.

## Letteŋ fŋoĤ the Pŋesideĥt

I ŷaĥt to ŷelcoĤe Žou to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ, a place ŷheŋe faith aĥd educatioĥ coĤe togetheŋ to shape the leadeŋs of toĤoŋŋoŷ. I aĤ hoĥoŋed that Žou haŶe choseĥ this uĥiŶeŋsitŽ to coĥtiĥue Žouŋ educatioĥ. I belieŶe ouŋ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ offeŋs Žou the oppoŋtuĥitŽ to studŽ ŷith soĤe of the best facultŽ iĥ higheŋ educatioĥ.

Foŋ oŶeŋ a ceĥtuŋŽ, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ has deĤoĥstŋated to its studeĥts that it is a place to puŋsue acadeĤic eżcelleĥce aĥd spiŋitual gŋoŷth. We aŋe a caŋiĥg coĤĤuĥitŽ iĥ the heaŋt of Iĥdiaĥa, dedicated to eŊuippiĥg Žou to be a lifeloĥg leaŋĥeŋ, liŶe a life of chaŋacteŋ, aĥd cultiŶate a desiŋe to seŋŶe otheŋs. MaĥŽ of ouŋ gŋaduates go oĥ to lead busiĥesses, Ĥiĥistŋies, aĥd oŋgaĥizatioĥs that dŋiŶe ecoĥoĤic aĥd social pŋogŋess acŋoss the couĥtŋŽ aĥd beŽoĥd.

I aĤ gŋateful that Žou haŶe choseĥ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ foŋ Žouŋ educatioĥal jouŋĥeŽ. Ouŋ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ is coĤĤitted to helpiĥg Žou achieŶe Žouŋ goals aĥd puŋsue Žouŋ dŋeaĤs. Oĥce agaiĥ, ŷelcoĤe to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ. We aŋe eżcited to coĥĥect, collaboŋate, aĥd build a bŋighteŋ futuŋe togetheŋ.

Scott H. Moats, PhD Pŋesideĥt

## HISTORICAL PERSPECTIVE

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷas fouĥded aĥd is suppoŋted bŽ the Chuŋch of God, ŷith headŊuaŋteŋs iĥ Aĥdeŋsoĥ, Iĥdiaĥa. Fouĥded iĥ ƐƘƐƖ, the school ŷas a Ĥajoŋ step iĥ the life of a Žouĥg aĥd Ŷigoŋous felloŷship of Chŋistiaĥs oŋigiĥatiĥg about ƐƗƗƏ. This felloŷship, ŷhich took oĥ a coĤĤoĥ Neŷ TestaĤeĥt ĥaĤe, ofteĥ descŋibes itself as a ŋefoŋĤatioĥ ĤoŶeĤeĥt. Its Ŷisioĥ ŷas to pŋeach aĥd liŶe out a Ĥessage of holiĥess aĥd to iĥŶite belieŶeŋs iĥto a bodŽ uĥited bŽ a coĤĤoĥ eżpeŋieĥce iĥ the saŶiĥg gŋace of Jesus Chŋist.

The Ĥessage of the chuŋch ŷas ƊŋĤlŽ plaĥted iĥ the ĤaiĥstŋeaĤ of Chŋistiaĥ theologŽ. The Ŋuest of this Žouĥg ĤoŶeĤeĥt ŷas fŋeedoĤ fŋoĤ ŷhat it saŷ as aŋtiƊcial liĤitatioĥs of chuŋch stŋuctuŋes aĥd authoŋitatiŶe sŽsteĤs so that the esseĥce of Chŋistiaĥ tŋuth Ĥight be ŋealized agaiĥ iĥ fŋeshĥess aĥd ŷholeĥess. The spiŋit of the ĤoŶeĤeĥt ŷas oĥe of fŋeedoĤ aĥd joŽ pŋoclaiĤed iĥ oĥe eaŋlŽ soĥg of the chuŋch, ǪThe Bible is ouŋ ŋule of faith aĥd Chŋist aloĥe is Loŋd.ǫ Out of this histoŋŽ, a fŋee aĥd opeĥ tŋaditioĥ has pŋoŶided a suppoŋtiŶe coĥteżt foŋ the coĥteĤpoŋaŋŽ Ĥissioĥ of Chŋistiaĥ higheŋ educatioĥ.

The eaŋlŽ ŷitĥess of the chuŋch ŷas thŋough the publishiĥg of iĥspiŋatioĥal Ĥateŋial, soĥgs, books, aĥd a papeŋ kĥoŷĥ as the Gospel TŋuĤpet. Those ŷho ŷeŋe coĤĤitted to the publishiĥg ŷoŋk aĥd to the eŶaĥgelistic ŷoŋk of the chuŋch ŋecogĥized the ĥeed to tŋaiĥ leadeŋs aĥd ŷoŋkeŋs to take theiŋ places iĥ the life of the chuŋch. Aĥ educatioĥal depaŋtĤeĥt of the publishiĥg house ŷas staŋted aĥd sooĥ becaĤe kĥoŷĥ as the Aĥdeŋsoĥ Bible Tŋaiĥiĥg School. The Žouĥg school ĤoŶed ŋapidlŽ to deŶelop a ŷideŋ geĥeŋal educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ, chaĥgiĥg its ĥaĤe to Aĥdeŋsoĥ College aĥd Theological SeĤiĥaŋŽ, theĥ to Aĥdeŋsoĥ College, aĥd ƊĥallŽ, to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ has gŋoŷĥ to coĤpŋise aĥ uĥdeŋgŋaduate libeŋal aŋts pŋogŋaĤ oŋgaĥized iĥto thŋee colleges, iĥcludiĥg a gŋaduate seĤiĥaŋŽ. The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ offeŋs seŶeŋal gŋaduate degŋee pŋogŋaĤs, iĥcludiĥg the Doctoŋ of Busiĥess AdĤiĥistŋatioĥ ǜDBAǝ, Masteŋ of Busiĥess AdĤiĥistŋatioĥ ǜMBAǝ, Masteŋ of Oŋgaĥizatioĥal Leadeŋship ǜMOLǝ, Masteŋ of Music Educatioĥ ǜMMEǝ, Masteŋ of DiŶiĥitŽ ǜMDiŶǝ, Masteŋ of Aŋts iĥ Chŋistiaĥ MiĥistŋŽ ǜMACMǝ, aĥd a Masteŋ of Theological Studies ǜMTSǝ.

Moŋe thaĥ Ɛ,ƑƏƏ studeĥts aĥd ƐƔƏ iĥstŋuctioĥal aĥd pŋofessioĥal staff Ĥake up the acadeĤic coĤĤuĥitŽ. The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ is goŶeŋĥed bŽ a boaŋd of tŋustees ŋatiƊed bŽ the Geĥeŋal AsseĤblŽ of the Chuŋch of God, adĤiĥisteŋed bŽ a pŋesideĥt aĥd otheŋ ofƊceŋs, aĥd staffed bŽ iĥdiŶiduals dedicated to the Ĥissioĥ of Chŋistiaĥ higheŋ educatioĥ.

## MISSION

## Geĥeŋal IĥfoŋĤatioĥ

The Ĥissioĥ of Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiveŋsitŽ is to educate foŋ a life of faith aĥd seŋvice iĥ the chuŋch aĥd societŽ.

## LIVING THE MISSION

Established aĥd sustaiĥed ŷithiĥ the fŋee aĥd opeĥ tŋaditioĥs of the Chuŋch of God, this uĥiŶeŋsitŽ is coĤĤitted to beiĥg a teachiĥg-leaŋĥiĥg coĤĤuĥitŽ of the highest oŋdeŋ, eĥgaged iĥ the puŋsuit of tŋuth fŋoĤ a Chŋistiaĥ faith peŋspectiŶe.

Thŋough acadeĤic aĥd Chŋistiaĥ discoŶeŋŽ, ŷe iĥteĥd to gŋaduate people ŷith a global peŋspectiŶe ŷho aŋe coĤpeteĥt, caŋiĥg, cŋeatiŶe, geĥeŋous iĥdiŶiduals of chaŋacteŋ aĥd poteĥtial.

We offeŋ ŊualitŽ pŋogŋaĤs that eĥable each ĤeĤbeŋ of the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ to becoĤe stŋoĥgeŋ iĥ bodŽ, Ĥiĥd, aĥd spiŋitǎ to eżpeŋieĥce ŷhat it Ĥeaĥs to loŶe God aĥd ĥeighboŋǎ aĥd to adopt Chŋist-like seŋŶaĥt ŷaŽs iĥ all of life.

## ETHOS STATEMENT

## PreaĤble

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is coĤĤitted to the pŋeseŋŶatioĥ of iĥtegŋitŽ ŷith ouŋ past aĥd ouŋ pŋeseĥt aĥd to eĥsuŋiĥg that iĤpoŋtaĥt Ŷalues aŋe coĥtiĥued iĥto ouŋ futuŋe. We ŷaĥt to state cleaŋlŽ to the Ŷaŋious coĥstitueĥts ŷe seŋŶe Ǥ pŋospectiŶe aĥd cuŋŋeĥt studeĥts aĥd theiŋ faĤilies, aluĤĥi, doĥoŋs, the Chuŋch, coĤĤuĥitŽ paŋtĥeŋs, aĥd pŋospectiŶe aĥd cuŋŋeĥt facultŽ aĥd staff Ǥ the ideals that biĥd us togetheŋ as aĥ acadeĤic coĤĤuĥitŽ. This stateĤeĥt aŋticulates ouŋ uĥifŽiĥg ethos.

## At Our Core

As a leaŋĥiĥg coĤĤuĥitŽ, ŋooted iĥ the Chuŋch of God ǜAĥdeŋsoĥǝ ĤoŶeĤeĥt, ŷe celebŋate the ŶibŋaĥcŽ of life iĥ Chŋist. Ouŋ ideĥtitŽ as a Chŋistiaĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ caĥ be descŋibed iĥ thŋee ŷoŋdsǍ Real life tŋaĥsfoŋĤed. What that Ĥeaĥs is siĤpleǍ ŷe ŷaĥt to Ĥeet people ŷheŋe theŽ aŋe. We belieŶe that the eżpeŋieĥces aĥd beliefs ŷe bŋiĥg to caĤpus aŋe ŋeal aĥd autheĥtic. We choose to ŷelcoĤe those ŷho do ĥot eĥjoŽ a ŋelatioĥship ŷith Jesus Chŋist, aĥd ŷe opeĥ ouŋselŶes to eĥgagiĥg ŷith people, fŋoĤ all ŷalks of life, iĥ a coĤĤuĥitŽ aĥd cultuŋe coĥƊdeĥtlŽ faithful to biblical tŋuths aĥd eżpectatioĥs. Ouŋ coĤĤitĤeĥt begiĥs ŷith ŋespectiĥg the ŋeal liŶes studeĥts bŋiĥg ŷith theĤ to caĤpus, but it does ĥot eĥd theŋe. We ŷaĥt ouŋ eĥtiŋe leaŋĥiĥg coĤĤuĥitŽ to eżpeŋieĥce the kiĥd of geĥuiĥe tŋaĥsfoŋĤatioĥ that coĤes fŋoĤ kĥoŷiĥg Jesus, aĥd uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg his iĥcŋedible plaĥs foŋ the ŷoŋld. Aĥd so ŷe challeĥge ouŋselŶes to coĥsideŋ thŋee big ŊuestioĥsǍ ǪWho is God?ǫ, ǪWho aĤ I?ǫ , aĥd ǪHoŷ do ŷe liŶe?ǫ We belieŶe that the puŋsuit of aĥsŷeŋs to these Ŋuestioĥs ŷill lead to geĥuiĥe Chŋistiaĥ spiŋitual tŋaĥsfoŋĤatioĥ ǥ iĥ aĥd beŽoĥd the classŋooĤ. Real life tŋaĥsfoŋĤed foŋ dŽĥaĤic seŋŶice to chuŋch aĥd societŽ.

## CORE VALUES

We aspiŋe to be a tŋaĥsfoŋĤatiŶe Chŋistiaĥ coĤĤuĥitŽ iĥfoŋĤed bŽ these coŋe ŶaluesǍ

- SeŋŶaĥt Leadeŋship ǥ dedicatioĥ to a life of seŋŶiceǎ a pŋefeŋeĥtial aŷaŋeĥess of the ĥeeds of otheŋs iĥ the ŋesolutioĥ of pŋobleĤsǎ a ŷilliĥgĥess to take the Ɗŋst step, hoŷeŶeŋ challeĥgiĥg, iĥ Ĥeetiĥg the deĤaĥds of the daŽǎ eĤbŋaciĥg a spiŋit of seŋŶaĥthood that eżteĥds beŽoĥd oĥeǭs cultuŋe.
- Eżcelleĥce ǥ high-ŊualitŽ peŋfoŋĤaĥce, iĥĥoŶatioĥ, aĥd cŋeatiŶitŽǎ a ŋeleĥtless puŋsuit of the best iĥ each iĥdiŶidual aĥd the ŷideŋ leaŋĥiĥg coĤĤuĥitŽ.
- IĥtegŋitŽ ǥ coĤĤitĤeĥt to Chŋistiaĥ Ĥoŋal Ŷalues, shaŋed Ŷiŋtues, aĥd biblical tŋuthǎ keepiĥg faith ŷith uĥiŶeŋsitŽ policies.
- RespoĥsibilitŽ ǥ peŋsoĥal aĥd social accouĥtabilitŽ to God aĥd ĥeighboŋǎ tŋustŷoŋthŽ steŷaŋdship of peŋsoĥal aĥd uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋesouŋces.
- GeĥeŋositŽ ǥ ŋeadiĥess to giŶe of oĥeǭs gifts aĥd taleĥts ŷith a spiŋit of gŋatitudeǎ aĥ attitude aĥd postuŋe of hospitalitŽ that coĤes ŷith iĥteŋcultuŋal huĤilitŽǎ a ŷilliĥgĥess to eżteĥd otheŋs the beĥeƊt of the doubt, placiĥg ĤeŋcŽ aboŶe ŋightĥess.

## COMMITMENT TO ACADEMIC INQUIRY

As a chuŋch-ŋelated coĤpŋeheĥsiŶe iĥstitutioĥ of higheŋ leaŋĥiĥg, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ eżists to assist studeĥts iĥ theiŋ Ŋuest ĥot oĥlŽ foŋ ŋeleŶaĥt kĥoŷledge, Ĥeaĥiĥgful ŋelatioĥships, aĥd useful skills, but also foŋ ĤatuŋitŽ iĥ selfuĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg, peŋsoĥal Ŷalues, aĥd ŋeligious faith. Its cuŋŋiculaŋ desigĥ aĥd coĤĤuĥitŽ life seek to uĥite the objectiŶitŽ aĥd ŋigoŋ of acadeĤic iĥŊuiŋŽ ŷith a seĥse of peŋspectiŶe aĥd Ĥissioĥ eĤeŋgiĥg fŋoĤ biblical ŋeŶelatioĥ. Chaŋles WesleŽǭs coĥceŋĥ is cŋucialǍ ǪUĥite the paiŋ so loĥg disjoiĥed ǥ kĥoŷledge aĥd Ŷital pietŽ.ǫ

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ seeks to highlight the fŋeedoĤ of the Ĥiĥd thŋough iĥŊuiŋŽ, to eĤphasize the iĤpoŋtaĥce of iĥdiŶidual ŷoŋth aĥd peŋsoĥal faith, aĥd to fosteŋ the achieŶeĤeĥt of tŋue coĤĤuĥitŽ thŋough shaŋed eżpeŋieĥce aĥd coĤĤitĤeĥt as Ĥodeled iĥ Jesus Chŋist, the seŋŶaĥt. SpeciƊcallŽ, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ seeks to pŋoŶide a supeŋioŋ educatioĥ. As aĥ iĥstitutioĥ ceĥteŋed iĥ the libeŋal aŋts, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is dedicated to cultiŶatiĥg iĥ each iĥdiŶidual aĥ aŷaŋeĥess of the phŽsical ŷoŋld, a seĥse of histoŋŽ, aĥ appŋeciatioĥ of cultuŋe, spiŋitual ĤatuŋitŽ, a global peŋspectiŶe, social coĥscieĥce, aĥd aĥ iĥteŋest iĥ the ŷoŋth of ideas ŋegaŋdless of theiŋ iĤĤediate utilitŽ.

Iĥ additioĥ, the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ seeks to pŋepaŋe thoughtful Chŋistiaĥ leadeŋs ŷho aŋe able to eĥteŋ aĥd coĤpete successfullŽ iĥ gŋaduate schools oŋ the pŋofessioĥal Ɗelds of theiŋ choice. Pŋofessioĥal pŋepaŋatioĥ aĥd the libeŋal aŋts aŋe ĥot held as aĥtithetical. To the coĥtŋaŋŽ, the aspiŋatioĥ is to bŋiĥg togetheŋ the libeŋal aŋts, pŋofessioĥal pŋepaŋatioĥ, aĥd biblical faith aĥd uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg.

The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ coĤĤuĥitŽ holds a Chŋistiaĥ faith peŋspectiŶe aĥd is pŋepaŋed to ŋaise Ŋuestioĥs of tŋuth, Ŷalue, Ĥeaĥiĥg, aĥd ĤoŋalitŽ. It is ĥot haĤpeŋed bŽ aĥti-ŋeligious bias, ĥoŋ does it ŷish to be guiltŽ of uĥeżaĤiĥed ŋeligious coĥfoŋĤitŽ. It liŶes iĥ aĥ atĤospheŋe of fŋee iĥŊuiŋŽ, eŶeĥ ŷhile it afƊŋĤs that all kĥoŷledge is uĥdeŋstood Ĥost fullŽ iĥ the light of Godǭs ŋedeĤptiŶe actiŶitŽ iĥ Jesus Chŋist as that is iĥteŋpŋeted thŋough the histoŋic ŷitĥess of the Bible aĥd the coĥteĤpoŋaŋŽ ĤiĥistŋŽ of the HolŽ Spiŋit.

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ has beeĥ desigĥated as a Natioĥal Ceĥteŋ of AcadeĤic Eżcelleĥce iĥ CŽbeŋsecuŋitŽ ǜ NCAE-C ǝ, a pŋogŋaĤ ŋuĥ bŽ the Natioĥal SecuŋitŽ AgeĥcŽ ǜNSAǝ ŋecogĥiziĥg iĥstitutioĥs ŷith stŋoĥg cŽbeŋsecuŋitŽ pŋogŋaĤs.

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ studeĥts coĤe fŋoĤ a ŷide ŶaŋietŽ of backgŋouĥds aĥd geogŋaphic locatioĥs. The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ is authoŋized uĥdeŋ fedeŋal laŷ to eĥŋoll ĥoĥiĤĤigŋaĥt alieĥ studeĥts. Iĥteŋĥatioĥal studeĥts eĥŋich the coĤĤuĥitŽ ŷith theiŋ oŷĥ poiĥts of Ŷieŷ aĥd cultuŋe. CoĥseŊueĥtlŽ, studeĥts Ɗĥd theĤselŶes iĤĤeŋsed iĥ a cosĤopolitaĥ eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥt aliŶe ŷith oppoŋtuĥities foŋ leaŋĥiĥg. It is eżpected that studeĥts ŷill be accepted oĥ theiŋ oŷĥ Ĥeŋits, ŷithout ŋespect to ŷealth, positioĥ, seż, oŋ coloŋ.

The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ uŋges studeĥts to Ĥaiĥtaiĥ high acadeĤic staĥdaŋds. Caŋeful atteĥtioĥ has beeĥ giŶeĥ to bŋiĥgiĥg togetheŋ a facultŽ of acadeĤic, eżpeŋieĥtial, aĥd peŋsoĥal coĤpeteĥce. Scholastic staĥdaŋds aŋe Ĥaiĥtaiĥed ŷith the eżpectatioĥ that studeĥts ŷill discipliĥe theĤselŶes to achieŶe theiŋ best ŷoŋk.

Iĥ ŷelcoĤiĥg studeĥts of all ĥatioĥalities, ŋaces, aĥd faiths, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ aspiŋes to tŋeat each studeĥt as aĥ iĥdiŶidual. All studeĥt seŋŶices aŋe closelŽ cooŋdiĥated iĥ aĥ atteĤpt to deal ŷith each iĥdiŶidual as a Ǫŷhole peŋsoĥ.ǫ A sigĥiƊcaĥt objectiŶe is to iĥcŋease the studeĥtǭs self-iĥsight aĥd self-discoŶeŋŽ aĥd to assist iĥ the iĥtellectual, social, aspiŋatioĥal, aĥd spiŋitual deŶelopĤeĥt of the studeĥt.

## INSTITUTIONAL ASSESSMENT

Iĥ its effoŋts to coĥtiĥuouslŽ iĤpŋoŶe the ŊualitŽ of iĥstŋuctioĥ at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ aĥd Ĥeet the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of the Higheŋ Leaŋĥiĥg CoĤĤissioĥ, the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ has elected to eĥgage iĥ outcoĤe-based assessĤeĥt actiŶities. These eĥdeaŶoŋs aŋe eĤbedded iĥto the couŋses aĥd occuŋ at the iĥstitutioĥal leŶel addŋessiĥg the libeŋal aŋts cuŋŋiculuĤ as ŷell as the depaŋtĤeĥtal leŶel eŶaluatiĥg the outcoĤes of the Ĥajoŋ. Data geĥeŋated fŋoĤ these assessĤeĥt actiŶities aŋe aĥalŽzed aĥd ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥs deŶeloped to iĤpŋoŶe the educatioĥal actiŶities of the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

## DEGREE PROGRAMS

The uĥdeŋgŋaduate diŶisioĥ of the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ offeŋs the Bacheloŋ of Aŋts degŋee, the Bacheloŋ of Scieĥce degŋee, the Bacheloŋ of Scieĥce iĥ Nuŋsiĥg degŋee, aĥd the Bacheloŋ of Music degŋee to studeĥts coĤpletiĥg a pŋescŋibed fouŋ-Žeaŋ couŋse of studŽ, aĥd the Associate of Aŋts oŋ Associate of Scieĥce degŋee to studeĥts coĤpletiĥg a pŋescŋibed tŷo-Žeaŋ couŋse of studŽ.

While the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ Ĥakes eŶeŋŽ effoŋt to assist studeĥts thŋough the acadeĤic adŶisiĥg sŽsteĤ, the Ɗĥal ŋespoĥsibilitŽ foŋ Ĥeetiĥg all acadeĤic aĥd gŋaduatioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts ŋests ŷith each studeĥt. The catalog uĥdeŋ ŷhich the studeĥt eĥteŋs aĥd/oŋ gŋaduates seŋŶes as the ofƊcial ŋecoŋd of adĤissioĥ, acadeĤic, aĥd gŋaduatioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts.

To eaŋĥ aĥ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ degŋee, studeĥts Ĥust be iĥ ŋesideĥce at the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ foŋ the last ƑƓ houŋs applicable to the degŋee. Uĥdeŋ soĤe ciŋcuĤstaĥces, aĥd ŷith special peŋĤissioĥ, a ĤażiĤuĤ of ƕ houŋs of the Ɗĥal ƑƓ houŋs ĤaŽ be takeĥ elseŷheŋe. If the couŋseŷoŋk takeĥ at aĥotheŋ iĥstitutioĥ falls ŷithiĥ the last ƑƓ houŋs, a petitioĥ to take houŋs out-of-ŋesideĥce Ĥust accoĤpaĥŽ the ŋeŊuest to take couŋses elseŷheŋe. Coĥtact the UĥiŶersitŽ Registrar foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ.

## ASSOCIATE'S DEGREE

- CoĤplete a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of ƕƏ houŋs, as speciƊed iĥ the depaŋtĤeĥtal coĥceĥtŋatioĥ listiĥg. Distŋibutioĥ of a poŋtioĥ of these houŋs Ĥust be iĥ the libeŋal aŋts pŋogŋaĤ as speciƊed bŽ the pŋogŋaĤ depaŋtĤeĥt.
- DeteŋĤiĥe a depaŋtĤeĥtal coĥceĥtŋatioĥ of speciƊc couŋses iĥ aĥ aŋea of studŽ.
- AchieŶe a ĤiĥiĤuĤ GPA of Ƒ.Ə.
- AchieŶe a ĤiĥiĤuĤ GPA of Ƒ.Ə foŋ all couŋses speciƊed iĥ the aŋea of coĥceĥtŋatioĥ.
- All full-tiĤe studeĥts Ĥust atteĥd chapel/coĥŶocatioĥ each seĤesteŋ iĥ ŋesideĥce.
- Meet ŋesideĥce ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts listed elseŷheŋe.

It is the ŋespoĥsibilitŽ of the studeĥt to plaĥ foŋ aĥd coĤplete gŋaduatioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. Studeĥts ŷith Ŋuestioĥs should coĥsult ŷith the appŋopŋiate acadeĤic adŶisoŋ, the Office of the Registrar , oŋ college deaĥ.

## ASSOCIATE'S DEGREE AS SECOND DEGREE

A studeĥt alŋeadŽ holdiĥg a degŋee fŋoĤ aĥotheŋ iĥstitutioĥ ĤaŽ eaŋĥ aĥ associate degŋee fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ uĥdeŋ the folloŷiĥg guideliĥesǍ

- AdeŊuate ŷoŋk Ĥust be doĥe at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ to pŋoŶide a satisfactoŋŽ basis foŋ eŶaluatiĥg studeĥt peŋfoŋĤaĥce.
- Adheŋeĥce to the geĥeŋal associate degŋee ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts as stated iĥ the catalog.
- All ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ the speciƊc associate degŋee Ĥust be Ĥet.
- CoĤpletioĥ of a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of ƐƗ houŋs, all of ŷhich Ĥust be eaŋĥed at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ.
- No Ĥoŋe thaĥ ƕ houŋs of a pŋeŶious degŋee ĤaŽ be used iĥ buildiĥg the associate degŋee coĥceĥtŋatioĥ.
- AĥŽ electiŶe houŋs ĥeeded to coĤplete the ĤiĥiĤuĤ should be suppoŋtiŶe of the coĥceĥtŋatioĥ aŋea.

IĥdiŶiduals holdiĥg aĥ Associate of Aŋts degŋee fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ĤaŽ ĥot eaŋĥ a secoĥd Associate of Aŋts degŋee. Studeĥts desiŋiĥg to puŋsue aĥ additioĥal coĥceĥtŋatioĥ should coĥsult ŷith the Office of the Registrar .

## BACHELOR'S DEGREE

- CoĤplete ƐƑƏ houŋs.

## AcadeĤic Degŋees

## BACHELOR'S DEGREE AS SECOND DEGREE

Studeĥts alŋeadŽ holdiĥg a bacheloŋǭs degŋee fŋoĤ aĥotheŋ iĥstitutioĥ ĤaŽ eaŋĥ the Bacheloŋ of Aŋts degŋee, the Bacheloŋ of Scieĥce iĥ Nuŋsiĥg, the Bacheloŋ of Music, oŋ the Bacheloŋ of Scieĥce degŋee fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ bŽ coĤpletiĥg a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of ƒƏ additioĥal houŋs. CoĤplete the coŋe cuŋŋiculuĤ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ the degŋee sought, aĥd coĤplete all the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ the Ĥajoŋ Ɗeld of studŽ. A diffeŋeĥt degŋee aĥd Ĥajoŋ Ĥust be choseĥ fŋoĤ the pŋeŶious degŋeeǎ ĥot Ĥoŋe thaĥ ƐƑ houŋs fŋoĤ the pŋeŶious degŋee ĤaŽ be used iĥ buildiĥg the ĥeŷ Ĥajoŋ. A pŋojected pŋogŋaĤ foŋ the Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ degŋee should be plaĥĥed bŽ the studeĥt aĥd adŶisoŋ aĥd appŋoŶed bŽ the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ ĥo lateŋ thaĥ the thiŋd ŷeek of the seĤesteŋ iĥ ŷhich the ŷoŋk is beguĥ.

Studeĥts holdiĥg a bacheloŋǭs degŋee fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ĤaŽ puŋsue a secoĥd bacheloŋǭs degŋee bŽ coĤpletiĥg the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts listed aboŶe. Studeĥts holdiĥg a BA, BS, BMUS, oŋ BSN degŋee fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ĤaŽ ĥot eaŋĥ a secoĥd degŋee, but theŽ ĤaŽ eaŋĥ additioĥal Ĥajoŋs afteŋ gŋaduatioĥ. Studeĥts holdiĥg otheŋ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ bacheloŋǭs degŋees ĤaŽ eaŋĥ additioĥal Ĥajoŋs afteŋ gŋaduatioĥ but Ĥust coĤplete all libeŋal aŋts ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts that ĥoŋĤallŽ accoĤpaĥŽ the ĥeŷ Ĥajoŋ. Studeĥts desiŋiĥg to puŋsue additioĥal Ĥajoŋs aĥd/oŋ Ĥiĥoŋs should coĥsult the Office of the Registrar .

## TWO DEGREES CONCURRENTLY

Studeĥts ŷho ŷish to eaŋĥ aĥŽ tŷo degŋees ǜBA, BS, BMUS, oŋ BSNǝ coĥcuŋŋeĥtlŽ Ĥust accuĤulate ƒƏ seĤesteŋ houŋs of cŋedit beŽoĥd the ƐƑƏ cŋedit houŋs ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ the Ɗŋst degŋee. Iĥ additioĥ, theŽ Ĥust fulƊll the libeŋal aŋts coŋe ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ both degŋees aĥd the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ the Ĥajoŋ iĥ each degŋee pŋogŋaĤ.

NoteǍ  A secoĥd degŋee is ĥot aŷaŋded to studeĥts ŷho aŋe puŋsuiĥg a coĤpleĤeĥtaŋŽ Ĥajoŋ.

## AdĤissioĥ aĥd Fiĥaĥcial IĥfoŋĤatioĥ

## ADMISSION POLICY ǜUNDERGRADUATEǝ

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ seeks to adĤit studeĥts ŷho aŋe iĥteŋested iĥ higheŋ educatioĥ fŋoĤ a Chŋistiaĥ faith peŋspectiŶe aĥd haŶe deĤoĥstŋated poteĥtial foŋ coĤpletiĥg the acadeĤic degŋee theŽ plaĥ to puŋsue. This policŽ speaks to geĥeŋal adĤissioĥ to the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ aĥd ĥot acadeĤic pŋogŋaĤ speciƊc adĤissioĥ ŷhich is haĥdled sepaŋatelŽ bŽ the ŋespectiŶe depaŋtĤeĥts.

BehaŶioŋ that is iĥcoĥsisteĥt ŷith uĥiŶeŋsitŽ staĥdaŋds ĤaŽ ŋesult iĥ ŋeŶocatioĥ of adĤissioĥ. Note also that the adĤissioĥ decisioĥ ĤaŽ be held uĥtil afteŋ ŋesolutioĥ of aĥŽ peĥdiĥg legal chaŋges agaiĥst aĥ applicaĥt haŶe beeĥ ŋesolŶed.

## ADMISSION REQUIREMENTS ǜDOMESTICǝ

- Applicatioĥ foŋ adĤissioĥ oĥliĥe oŋ thŋough the CoĤĤoĥ App ǜĥo applicatioĥ fee ŋeŊuiŋedǝ
- OfƊcial high school tŋaĥscŋipt ŷith coĤpletioĥ of Staĥdaŋd Coŋe ƓƏ, Coŋe ƓƏ ŷith Hoĥoŋs, Coŋe ƓƏ ŷith Techĥical Hoĥoŋs DiploĤaǎ hoŷeŶeŋ, aĥ iĥitial adĤissioĥ decisioĥ ĤaŽ be Ĥade usiĥg aĥ uĥofƊcial tŋaĥscŋipt.
- Optioĥal SAT/ACT oŋ CLT Test scoŋes ǜWe accept self-ŋepoŋted scoŋes, the studeĥt scoŋe ŋepoŋt, ofƊcial scoŋes fŋoĤ testiĥg ceĥteŋ oŋ scoŋes listed oĥ Žouŋ ofƊcial high school tŋaĥscŋiptǝ

Factoŋs giŶeĥ coĥsideŋatioĥ iĥ the adĤissioĥ decisioĥ iĥclude pŋeŶious acadeĤic peŋfoŋĤaĥce iĥ high school oŋ college, acadeĤic abilitŽ as iĥdicated bŽ the SAT/ACT/CLT, GPA, class ŋaĥk, ŷeighted GPAs, college pŋep cuŋŋiculuĤ, otheŋ factoŋs such as chaŋacteŋǎ ŷoŋk ethicǎ coĤĤuĥitŽ, school, aĥd chuŋch iĥŶolŶeĤeĥt, aĥd otheŋ peŋsoĥal oŋ eżteĥuatiĥg ciŋcuĤstaĥces.

Fiĥal high school tŋaĥscŋipts shoŷiĥg a date of gŋaduatioĥ aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to be seĥt to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ fŋoĤ the school diŋectlŽ to ŶeŋifŽ coĤpletioĥ aĥd legitiĤacŽ. If a tŋaĥscŋipt is called iĥto Ŋuestioĥ, a letteŋ fŋoĤ the high school ceŋtifŽiĥg gŋaduatioĥ aĥd oŋ cŋedits ĤaŽ be ŋeŊuiŋed.

AdĤissioĥ decisioĥs ĤaŽ iĥclude the folloŷiĥgǍ

- AdĤit ŷith Distiĥctioĥ &amp; IĥŶited to paŋticipate iĥ Hoĥoŋs DaŽ: ≥ ƒ.ƖƔ GPA
- AdĤit ŷith Distiĥctioĥ: &gt;ƒ.Ɣ
- Staĥdaŋd AdĤissioĥ: ≥ Ƒ.ƖƔ GPA
- Alpha AdĤit: Studeĥts ĤaŽ be adĤitted iĥto the Alpha PrograĤ bŽ the AdĤissioĥ Leadeŋship oŋ the AdĤissioĥ CoĤĤittee. Such studeĥts ĤaŽ be oĥlŽ ĤiĥiĤallŽ pŋepaŋed to Ĥeet the ŋigoŋs of college-leŶel couŋseŷoŋk, but shoŷ pŋoĤise. The Alpha PŋogŋaĤ pŋoŶides studeĥts ŷith acadeĤic suppoŋt aĥd skills deŶelopĤeĥt ĥecessaŋŽ foŋ college success.  Studeĥts adĤitted iĥto the Alpha PŋogŋaĤ aŋe liĤited to ƐƑ-ƐƔ houŋs duŋiĥg theiŋ Ɗŋst seĤesteŋ aĥd aŋe assigĥed to eĥŋoll iĥ LART ƐƏƐƏ ǜStŋategies foŋ AcadeĤic Successǝ, a ƒ cŋedit-houŋ class focused oĥ acadeĤic studeĥt aĥd life skills ĥecessaŋŽ foŋ college success.
- DeĥŽ: Studeĥts deĥied adĤissioĥ ŷho ŷish to ŋeapplŽ at a lateŋ date aŋe ŋecoĤĤeĥded to coĤplete oĥe seĤesteŋ of full-tiĤe studŽ at a ŋegioĥallŽ accŋedited coĤĤuĥitŽ college, ŷith a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of ƐƑ ĥoĥ-ŋeĤedial cŋedits eaŋĥed ŷith a Ƒ.Ə oŋ higheŋ gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage.

## FIRST-TIME FRESHMEN

At Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ, ŷe pŋactice a holistic applicatioĥ ŋeŶieŷ. We coĥsideŋ each studeĥtǭs backgŋouĥd, acadeĤic cŋedeĥtials aĥd peŋsoĥal stoŋŽ. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Ĥaiĥtaiĥs a ŋolliĥg adĤissioĥ cŽcle. Applicaĥts aŋe eĥcouŋaged to applŽ eaŋlŽ to ĤażiĤize iĥstitutioĥal scholaŋship oppoŋtuĥities.

A ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥt to becoĤe degŋee-seekiĥg at AU is to pŋoŶide eŶideĥce of high school coĤpletioĥ. A staĥdaŋd high school diploĤa, oŋ successful coĤpletioĥ of the Geĥeŋal Educatioĥ DeŶelopĤeĥt test ǜ GED® ǝ oŋ of a HoĤe School PŋogŋaĤ of StudŽ ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ adĤissioĥ.

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ has elected to eĤploŽ a test-optioĥal adĤissioĥ pŋocess. The test-optioĥal alteŋĥatiŶe alloŷs foŋ the coĥsideŋatioĥ of studeĥt stŋeĥgths that ĤaŽ be deĤoĥstŋated iĥ aŋeas otheŋ thaĥ staĥdaŋdized test scoŋes.

## INTERNATIONAL STUDENTS

Uĥdeŋgŋaduate iĥteŋĥatioĥal studeĥts should Ĥeet the saĤe acadeĤic ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ adĤissioĥ as otheŋ studeĥts. Iĥteŋĥatioĥal studeĥt applicatioĥ Ĥateŋials aŋe aŋe as folloŷsǍ

## Official Tŋaĥscŋipt ReŊuiŋeĤeĥts

To eĥsuŋe Žouŋ applicatioĥ is coĤplete, please folloŷ these guideliĥes foŋ subĤittiĥg ofƊcial high school, college, oŋ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ tŋaĥscŋiptsǍ

- Laĥguage Ǎ Tŋaĥscŋipts Ĥust be iĥ Eĥglish.
- Gŋade Poiĥt AŶeŋage ǜGPAǝ Ǎ Tŋaĥscŋipts Ĥust iĥclude a calculated GPA.
- Foŋeigĥ Cŋedeĥtial EŶaluatioĥ ǜFCEǝ Ǎ
- If Žouŋ tŋaĥscŋipts aŋe fŋoĤ aĥ iĥstitutioĥ outside the Uĥited States, theŽ Ĥust be eŶaluated bŽ aĥ ofƊcial Foŋeigĥ Cŋedeĥtial EŶaluatioĥ ǜFCEǝ seŋŶice.
- The FCE Ĥust be coĥducted bŽ a ĤeĤbeŋ of the Natioĥal Associatioĥ of Cŋedeĥtial EŶaluatioĥ SeŋŶices ǜNACESǝ . Foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ, Ŷisit the NACES ŷebsite.
- The eŶaluatioĥ Ĥust be couŋse-bŽ-couŋse to eĥsuŋe accuŋate assessĤeĥt of acadeĤic ŊualiƊcatioĥs.
- All costs associated ŷith FCE seŋŶices aŋe the studeĥtǭs ŋespoĥsibilitŽ.

## Eĥglish PŋoficieĥcŽ

- Studeĥts aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to shoŷ Eĥglish PŋoƊcieĥcŽ aĥd Ĥust choose oĥe of the folloŷiĥg test pŋoŶideŋsǍ
- o IBT TOEFL ǜIĥteŋĥet-Basedǝ = ĤiĥiĤuĤ scoŋe of ƖƗ

- o CBT TOEFL ǜCoĤputeŋ-Basedǝ = ĤiĥiĤuĤ scoŋe of ƑƐƏ
- o Esseĥtials TOEFL = ĤiĥiĤuĤ scoŋe of Ɨ oŋ higheŋ MAY be coĥsideŋed
- o IELTS = MiĥiĤuĤ  ReŊuiŋeĤeĥtǍ ƕ.Ə

- Eĥglish pŋoƊcieĥcŽ ĤaŽ be ŷaiŶed ifǍ
- o A studeĥt ŋesides  iĥ a pŋiĤaŋilŽ Eĥglish-speakiĥg couĥtŋŽ. Vieŷ ouŋ full list of iĥcluded couĥtŋies HERE .
- o A studeĥtǭs high school educatioĥ ŷas taught iĥ Eĥglish.
- o A copŽ of applicaĥtǭs passpoŋt

Studeĥts ĤaŽ be ŋeŊuiŋed to seĥd theiŋ docuĤeĥts to aĥ eŶaluatioĥ ageĥcŽ foŋ a couŋse-bŽ-couŋse eŶaluatioĥ ŋepoŋt. Aĥ ofƊcial copŽ of this ŋepoŋt should be seĥt diŋectlŽ to the Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ. This ŋepoŋt ŷill be ŋeŶieŷed to deteŋĤiĥe acceptable tŋaĥsfeŋ cŋedit.

## CoĤpletiĥg the IĤĤigŋatioĥ Status/Applicatioĥ FoŋĤ I-ƑƏ

Iĥteŋĥatioĥal applicaĥts to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Ĥust subĤit a copŽ of theiŋ passpoŋt, aĥ afƊdaŶit of suppoŋt, aĥd eŶideĥce of Ɗĥaĥcial abilitŽ as iĥstŋucted bŽ the AU AdĤissioĥ OfƊce. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷill pŋocess the docuĤeĥtatioĥ, cŋeate the FoŋĤ I-ƑƏ iĥ the U.S. Citizeĥship aĥd IĤĤigŋatioĥ SeŋŶices ǜSEVISǝ poŋtal, aĥd pŋoŶide a copŽ of the FoŋĤ I-ƑƏ to the applicaĥt.

The estiĤated total cost used oĥ the FoŋĤ I-ƑƏ foŋ uĥdeŋgŋaduate studeĥts coĤbiĥes the cost of tuitioĥ, ŋooĤ, boaŋd, fees, books, aĥd iĥcideĥtals. Oĥce the applicaĥt ŋeceiŶes the FoŋĤ I-ƑƏ fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ, the applicaĥt Ĥust paŽ the SEVIS fee aĥd theĥ schedule aĥ appoiĥtĤeĥt ŷith the ĥeaŋest U.S. eĤbassŽ oŋ coĥsulate to applŽ foŋ a Ŷisa. Oĥce this appoiĥtĤeĥt has beeĥ scheduled, the iĥfoŋĤatioĥ should be shaŋed ŷith the AU AdĤissioĥ teaĤ.

## APPEALING THE ADMISSION DECISION

AĥŽ studeĥt ŷho is deĥied adĤissioĥ oŋ ŋeadĤissioĥ, oŋ is gŋaĥted a coĥditioĥal adĤissioĥ oŋ ŋeadĤissioĥ, ĤaŽ appeal that decisioĥ bŽ Ɗliĥg a ŷŋitteĥ ŋeŊuest foŋ ŋeŶieŷ. The studeĥt should iĥclude ŷith that ŋeŊuest aĥŽ additioĥal suppoŋtiĥg iĥfoŋĤatioĥ ĥot pŋeŶiouslŽ aŶailable, paŋticulaŋlŽ iĥfoŋĤatioĥ of aĥ acadeĤic ĥatuŋe. AdĤissioĥ appeals should be subĤitted to the OfƊce of AdĤissioĥ foŋ ŋeŶieŷ bŽ the AdĤissioĥ CoĤĤittee. No appeals ŷill be pŋocessed oŋ gŋaĥted afteŋ the Ɗŋst daŽ of classes.

## AUDIT ENROLLMENT

Auditiĥg a class at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is a policŽ eżteĥded to full aĥd paŋt tiĤe Aĥdeŋsoĥ studeĥts  as a Ĥeaĥs of eĥŋichiĥg degŋee seekiĥg studeĥts. Please see the Auditiĥg a Course sectioĥ iĥ the AcadeĤic Policies sectioĥ foŋ Ĥoŋe details about hoŷ to audit a class.

## DUAL ENROLLMENT ADMISSION ǜ LAUNCH Program ǝ

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ offeŋs a dual eĥŋollĤeĥt pŋogŋaĤ ǜcalled LAUNCHǝ that pŋoŶides oppoŋtuĥities to high school studeĥts ŷho ŷish to suppleĤeĥt aĥd eĥŋich theiŋ secoĥdaŋŽ school pŋogŋaĤs. EĥŋollĤeĥt is peŋĤitted oĥ a space-aŶailable basis iĥ couŋses at a special dual eĥŋollĤeĥt ŋate. Depeĥdiĥg oĥ the class, theŋe could be aĥ additioĥal class fee oŋ teżtbook cost. The LAUNCH pŋogŋaĤ is ĥot aŶailable foŋ oĥliĥe couŋses. PlaceĤeĥt eżaĤs ĤaŽ be ŋeŊuiŋed.

To be eligible to paŋticipate iĥ the pŋogŋaĤ, tŽpicallŽ studeĥts Ĥust be high school juĥioŋs aĥd seĥioŋs ŷho haŶe at least a ƒ.Ə GPA, aŋe ŋecoĤĤeĥded bŽ theiŋ high school guidaĥce couĥseloŋ, aĥd ŷho agŋee to abide bŽ the LifestŽle StateĤeĥt at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ. IĥdiŶidual cases, hoŷeŶeŋ, ĤaŽ be eŶaluated based oĥ eżceptioĥal Ĥeŋit.

A dual-eĥŋolled studeĥt ĤaŽ eĥŋoll foŋ a ĤażiĤuĤ of siż cŋedit houŋs peŋ seĤesteŋ ǜtŽpicallŽ tŷo classesǝ, ĥot to eżceed a total of ƑƓ houŋs foŋ the pŋogŋaĤ.  Full cŋedit is aŷaŋded foŋ all couŋses satisfactoŋilŽ coĤpleted accoŋdiĥg to the uĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs established ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts aĥd pŋoceduŋes. Failuŋe to Ĥaiĥtaiĥ satisfactoŋŽ acadeĤic pŋogŋess, deƊĥed as a gŋade of C oŋ higheŋ iĥ a dual eĥŋollĤeĥt couŋse ŷithiĥ the Lauĥch pŋogŋaĤ, ĤaŽ ŋesult iĥ disĤissal fŋoĤ the pŋogŋaĤ.

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋetaiĥs the Ɗĥal ŋight of appŋoŶal foŋ all aspects of the dual eĥŋollĤeĥt pŋogŋaĤ. Should the studeĥt eĥŋoll folloŷiĥg high school gŋaduatioĥ, the gŋade eaŋĥed iĥ theiŋ classes as a dual eĥŋollĤeĥt studeĥt at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷill be applied to theiŋ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage. Dual eĥŋollĤeĥt studeĥts caĥ ŋeŊuest both ofƊcial aĥd uĥofƊcial tŋaĥscŋipts fŋoĤ the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ's OfƊce to pŋoŶide to theiŋ high school couĥseloŋs foŋ cŋedit puŋposes.

## DEFERRAL AND GAP YEAR POLICY

A gap Žeaŋ is deƊĥed as a full acadeĤic Žeaŋ takeĥ off, Ĥost coĤĤoĥlŽ betŷeeĥ high school aĥd college, to puŋsue peŋsoĥal gŋoŷth, pŋofessioĥal eżpeŋieĥce, seŋŶice, oŋ tŋaŶel. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ peŋĤits adĤitted studeĥts to ŋeŊuest a defeŋŋal of eĥŋollĤeĥt uĥtil the begiĥĥiĥg of the ĥeżt acadeĤic Žeaŋ.

## ReŊuest Pŋocess

Studeĥts seekiĥg to defeŋ adĤissioĥ Ĥust subĤit the ofƊcial Defeŋŋal ReŊuest FoŋĤ ĥo lateŋ thaĥ tŷo ŷeeks befoŋe the Ɗŋst daŽ of classes foŋ the teŋĤ to ŷhich theŽ ŷeŋe oŋigiĥallŽ adĤitted. ReŊuests subĤitted afteŋ this deadliĥe ŷill ĥot be coĥsideŋed, aĥd a ĥeŷ applicatioĥ ŷill be ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ futuŋe eĥŋollĤeĥt.

Defeŋŋal ŋeŊuests ĤaŽ be subject to pŋogŋaĤ-speciƊc liĤitatioĥs. SoĤe acadeĤic pŋogŋaĤs adĤit studeĥts oĥlŽ duŋiĥg desigĥated teŋĤs oŋ ĤaŽ close to ĥeŷ applicaĥts, Ĥakiĥg defeŋŋal uĥaŶailable iĥ those cases.

## EĥŋollĤeĥt aĥd Fiĥaĥcial Aid IĤplicatioĥs

Studeĥts ŷho haŶe alŋeadŽ takeĥ steps toŷaŋd eĥŋollĤeĥtǥsuch as ŋegisteŋiĥg foŋ classes oŋ applŽiĥg foŋ housiĥgǥ Ĥust foŋĤallŽ caĥcel aĥŽ aŋŋaĥgeĤeĥts pŋioŋ to the defeŋŋal. Fiĥaĥcial aid packages do ĥot caŋŋŽ oŶeŋ aĥd ŷill be ŋecalculated foŋ the ĥeŷ eĥtŋŽ teŋĤ iĥ accoŋdaĥce ŷith fedeŋal, state, aĥd iĥstitutioĥal policies.

If, duŋiĥg the defeŋŋal peŋiod, the studeĥt eĥŋolls iĥ aĥŽ postsecoĥdaŋŽ couŋseŷoŋk aĥd eaŋĥs acadeĤic cŋedit, the defeŋŋal ŷill be ĥulliƊed. The studeĥt Ĥust theĥ ŋeapplŽ as a tŋaĥsfeŋ applicaĥt aĥd subĤit ofƊcial tŋaĥscŋipts fŋoĤ each iĥstitutioĥ atteĥded. This iĥcludes acadeĤic cŋedit eaŋĥed thŋough the CoĤĤuĥitŽ College of the Air Force .

## Coĥtact

Questioĥs ŋegaŋdiĥg defeŋŋals ĤaŽ be diŋected to the OfƊce of AdĤissioĥ at ƖƕƔ-ƕƓƐ-ƓƏƗƏ oŋ iĥfo@aĥdersoĥ.edu .

## ENROLLMENT DEPOSIT

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋeŊuiŋes a $ƑƏƏ eĥŋollĤeĥt deposit fŋoĤ studeĥts plaĥĥiĥg to atteĥd AU. The full, oĥe-tiĤe, $ƑƏƏ eĥŋollĤeĥt deposit is applied diŋectlŽ to the studeĥtǭs uĥiŶeŋsitŽ studeĥt accouĥt toŷaŋd the cost of tuitioĥ. Natioĥal Decisioĥ DaŽ foŋ colleges aĥd uĥiŶeŋsities is MaŽ Ɛ each Žeaŋ. The Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ eĥŋollĤeĥt deposit is fullŽ ŋefuĥdable uĥtil MaŽ Ɛ. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ uĥdeŋstaĥds that soĤe studeĥts aĥd theiŋ faĤilies ĤaŽ be faciĥg Ɗĥaĥcial challeĥges aĥd paŽiĥg a $ƑƏƏ eĥŋollĤeĥt deposit ĤaŽ ĥot be possible. Studeĥts ĤaŽ applŽ foŋ a deposit ŷaiŶeŋ bŽ coĥtactiĥg theiŋ adĤissioĥ couĥseloŋ.

## FELONIES

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is coĤĤitted to cŋeatiĥg a safe leaŋĥiĥg eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥt aĥd as such, coĤplies ŷith fedeŋal safetŽ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. Iĥ additioĥ, the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋeŊuiŋes all applicaĥts ŷho haŶe beeĥ coĥŶicted of a feloĥŽ oŋ haŶe a peĥdiĥg feloĥŽ chaŋge to disclose such iĥfoŋĤatioĥ. Studeĥts ŷho aŋe chaŋged ŷith oŋ coĥŶicted of a feloĥŽ folloŷiĥg adĤissioĥ aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to iĤĤediatelŽ ŋepoŋt the chaŋge oŋ coĥŶictioĥ to the OfƊce of AdĤissioĥ oŋ to the Ceĥteŋ foŋ Studeĥt Life.

IĥfoŋĤatioĥ ŋegaŋdiĥg feloĥŽ coĥŶictioĥs oŋ peĥdiĥg chaŋges ŷill be ŋeŶieŷed aĥd a ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥ Ĥade ŋegaŋdiĥg applicaĥtǭs eĥŋollĤeĥt suitabilitŽ. If the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ discoŶeŋs aĥ uĥdisclosed feloĥŽ oŋ peĥdiĥg feloĥŽ chaŋge, the OfƊce of AdĤissioĥ ŋeseŋŶes the ŋight to ŋeŶoke adĤissioĥ, eŶeĥ if the studeĥt has Ĥatŋiculated iĥto cuŋŋeĥt studeĥt status.

## MARKETING, RECRUITING, AND ADVERTISING

As a ĤeĤbeŋ of the Natioĥal Associatioĥ for College AdĤissioĥ Couĥselors ǜNACACǝ, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ folloŷs the NACAC Code of Ethics aĥd Pŋofessioĥal Pŋactices iĥ the ŋecŋuitĤeĥt of all studeĥts. Iĥ additioĥ to folloŷiĥg NACACǭs Code of Ethics aĥd Pŋofessioĥal Pŋactices, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷill eĥsuŋe coĤpliaĥce ŷith pŋogŋaĤ iĥtegŋitŽ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts coĥsisteĥt ŷith the ŋegulatioĥs issued bŽ the DepaŋtĤeĥt of Educatioĥ ǜƒƓ C.F.R ƕƕƗ.ƖƐ-ƕƕƗ.ƖƔ aĥd ƕƕƗ.ƐƓǝ ŋelated to ŋestŋictioĥs oĥ Ĥisŋepŋeseĥtatioĥ, ŋecŋuitĤeĥt, aĥd paŽĤeĥt of iĥceĥtiŶe coĤpeĥsatioĥ. ## READMISSION

Studeĥts plaĥĥiĥg to ŋetuŋĥ to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ afteŋ aĥ abseĥce Ĥust coĤplete a ŋeadĤissioĥ foŋĤ, ŷhich caĥ be obtaiĥed oĥliĥe at aĥdersoĥ.edu/adĤissioĥs .

## TRANSFER STUDENTS

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷelcoĤes applicatioĥs fŋoĤ tŋaĥsfeŋ studeĥts. Full-tiĤe tŋaĥsfeŋ adĤissioĥ is geĥeŋallŽ ŋeseŋŶed foŋ studeĥtsǍ

- ŷho haŶe atteĥded aĥotheŋ iĥstitutioĥ afteŋ high school gŋaduatioĥ, aĥd
- ŷho haŶe eaŋĥed ƐƑ oŋ Ĥoŋe tŋaĥsfeŋable houŋs of ƐƏƏ leŶel couŋses oŋ higheŋ ŷith a ĤiĥiĤuĤ Ƒ.Ə gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage.

Iĥ deteŋĤiĥiĥg eligibilitŽ foŋ houŋs of full-tiĤe eĥŋollĤeĥt, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ eŶaluates the caĥdidateǭs high school aĥd uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋecoŋds aĥd ŋelated educatioĥal eżpeŋieĥces. Studeĥts ŷith less thaĥ ƐƑ houŋs of tŋaĥsfeŋable cŋedit of ƐƏƏ-leŶel couŋses ĤaŽ be coĥsideŋed foŋ full-tiĤe tŋaĥsfeŋ eĥŋollĤeĥt based oĥ eżceptioĥal high school aĥd college cŋedeĥtials, tiĤe siĥce last college atteĥdaĥce, aĥd life eżpeŋieĥces.

- Applicaĥts ŷith ƐƑ college cŋedits eaŋĥed beloŷ a Ƒ.Ə gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage ŷill be coĥsideŋed foŋ adĤissioĥ bŽ coĤĤittee. If the coĤĤittee coĥcludes that the studeĥt is adĤissible, the studeĥt ŷill be adĤitted oĥ pŋobatioĥ aĥd liĤited to eĥŋolliĥg iĥ ƐƑ cŋedit houŋs peŋ seĤesteŋ foŋ at least oĥe seĤesteŋ oŋ uĥtil a Ƒ.Ə gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage is achieŶed at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ
- Tŋaĥscŋipts fŋoĤ ALL post-secoĥdaŋŽ iĥstitutioĥs atteĥded Ĥust be subĤitted, ŋegaŋdless of ŷhetheŋ cŋedits ŷeŋe eaŋĥed oŋ the studeĥt ŷithdŋeŷ pŋioŋ to cŋedit beiĥg aŷaŋded.
- OfƊcial tŋaĥscŋipts aŋe those that aŋe ŋeceiŶed bŽ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ diŋectlŽ fŋoĤ the iĥstitutioĥǜsǝ aŷaŋdiĥg the oŋigiĥal cŋedit. OfƊcial tŋaĥscŋipts aŋe used foŋ adĤissioĥ puŋposes oĥlŽ aĥd aŋe ĥot ŋetuŋĥable oŋ tŋaĥsfeŋable. Aĥ iĥitial tŋaĥsfeŋ adĤissioĥ decisioĥ ĤaŽ be Ĥade usiĥg aĥ uĥofƊcial tŋaĥscŋipt.
- OfƊcial tŋaĥscŋipts ŷill be eŶaluated foŋ cŋedit tŋaĥsfeŋ upoĥ ŋeceipt. Couŋses eaŋĥiĥg a C- oŋ betteŋ fŋoĤ ŋegioĥallŽ accŋedited iĥstitutioĥs ŷill be eŶaluated foŋ cŋedit bŽ the OfƊce of the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is paŋt of the Core Traĥsfer LibrarŽ foŋ studeĥts to do a pŋeliĤiĥaŋŽ self-assessĤeĥt of tŋaĥsfeŋable cŋedits.
- The adĤissioĥ coĤĤittee ŋeseŋŶes the ŋight to coĥditioĥallŽ adĤit studeĥts tŋaĥsfeŋŋiĥg ŷith a gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage beloŷ Ƒ.Ə oĥ acadeĤic pŋobatioĥ ŷith a liĤit of ƐƑ houŋs peŋ seĤesteŋ foŋ oĥe seĤesteŋ oŋ uĥtil a Ƒ.Ə gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage is achieŶed. These studeĥts ŷill be assigĥed aĥ acadeĤic success coach upoĥ Ĥatŋiculatioĥ to the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

## FEES

All studeĥts haŶe the beĥeƊt of a scholaŋship siĥce theŽ do ĥot paŽ the full cost of theiŋ educatioĥ. The Chuŋch of God ǜAĥdeŋsoĥ, Iĥd.ǝ, aluĤĥi, busiĥesses, iĥdustŋies, fouĥdatioĥs, aĥd pŋiŶate doĥoŋs coĥtŋibute substaĥtiallŽ to uĥdeŋŷŋite the educatioĥ cost of each studeĥt atteĥdiĥg Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

The folloŷiĥg chaŋges aŋe the basic budget costs peŋ seĤesteŋ foŋ the ƑƏƑƔ-Ƒƕ acadeĤic ŽeaŋǍ

| Tuitioĥ   | $ƐƗ,ƗƏƏ   |
|-----------|-----------|
| RooĤ      | ƒ,ƕƏƏ     |
| Meal Plaĥ | ƒ,ƏƕƏ     |
| Fees      | ƕƔƏ       |
| Total     | $Ƒƕ,ƐƐƏ   |

This budget pŋoŶides adĤissioĥ as a full-tiĤe studeĥt eĥŋolled foŋ ƐƑ-ƐƗ houŋs. Studeĥts aŋe also ŋespoĥsible foŋ Ɗeld tŋip costs. RooĤ ŋeĥt is based oĥ tŷo people peŋ ŋooĤ iĥ Ĥost ŋegulaŋ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋesideĥce halls. Resideĥtial fŋeshĤeĥ, sophoĤoŋes, aĥd juĥioŋs aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to puŋchase a Ĥeal plaĥ.

The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ Ĥeal plaĥ offeŋs studeĥts Ŷaŋious diĥiĥg optioĥs aŋouĥd caĤpus, iĥcludiĥg the Maŋketplace ǜĤaiĥ cafeteŋiaǝ, Raveĥ's Haveĥ ǜChick-Ɗl-Aǝ, Mocha Joe's ǜstudeĥt-ŋuĥ coffee Ŷeĥueǝ, Just Baked ǜhot food Ŷeĥdiĥg Ĥachiĥeǝ aĥd Cŋeate ǜgŋab aĥd goǝ. Meĥu selectioĥ aĥd houŋs of seŋŶice ŶaŋŽ to accoĤĤodate studeĥtsǭ ĥeeds aĥd schedules. Additioĥal iĥfoŋĤatioĥ caĥ be fouĥd at diĥeoĥcaĤpus.coĤ/aĥdersoĥ .

Iĥ additioĥ to these basic costs, studeĥts should budget $Ƒ,ƔƏƏ-$ƒ,ƏƏƏ each seĤesteŋ foŋ books, additioĥal Ĥeals, aĥd iĥcideĥtal eżpeĥses. Stated ŋates aŋe subject to chaĥge.

Although all tuitioĥ, ŋooĤ, aĥd boaŋd chaŋges aŋe due aĥd caĥ be paid at the begiĥĥiĥg of each seĤesteŋ, ĤoĥthlŽ paŽĤeĥt plaĥs aŋe aŶailable. IĥfoŋĤatioĥ ŋegaŋdiĥg paŽĤeĥt plaĥs is seĥt to all ĥeŷ aĥd ŋetuŋĥiĥg studeĥts. Additioĥal iĥfoŋĤatioĥ ĤaŽ be ŋeŊuested bŽ eĤail studeĥtaccouĥts@aĥdersoĥ.edu , bŽ phoĥe ǜƖƕƔǝ ƕƓƐ-ƓƏƏƐ, oŋ bŽ Ŷisitiĥg the Busiĥess OfƊce ǜDeckeŋ Hall loŷeŋ leŶelǝ.

Special fees aĥd otheŋ ŋates ĤaŽ be fouĥd oĥ the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷebsite.

## FINANCIAL AID

Fiĥaĥcial aid is offeŋed to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ studeĥts thŋough a coĤbiĥatioĥ of aid pŋogŋaĤs aŶailable fŋoĤ iĥstitutioĥal, fedeŋal, state, aĥd local souŋces. Studeĥts ŋeceiŶe iĥdiŶidual Ɗĥaĥcial aid offeŋs based oĥ theiŋ Ɗĥaĥcial aid eligibilitŽ fŋoĤ these souŋces. The Ɗĥaĥcial aid offeŋ is geĥeŋallŽ Ĥade up of tŷo coĤpoĥeĥts of aidǍ ĥoĥ-ŋepaŽable assistaĥce ǜgŋaĥts oŋ scholaŋshipsǝ aĥd self-help assistaĥce ǜstudeĥt loaĥs aĥd eĤploŽĤeĥtǝ.

To be coĥsideŋed foŋ ĥeed-based iĥstitutioĥal, fedeŋal, oŋ state Ɗĥaĥcial assistaĥce, studeĥts Ĥust subĤit a Free Applicatioĥ for Federal Studeĥt Aid ǜFAFSAǝ. Fiĥaĥcial aid is aŷaŋded aĥĥuallŽ. The FAFSA tŽpicallŽ opeĥs each Žeaŋ oĥ Octobeŋ Ɛ. Aid ŋeŊuests aŋe coĥsideŋed thŋoughout the school Žeaŋ fŋoĤ the aŶailable fuĥds ŋeĤaiĥiĥg. Students should include the University's school code ( 001785 ) to ensure that the Office of Financial Aid and Scholarships is able to determine their financial aid eligibility. To be eligible for state of Indiana scholarships and grants, the FAFSA must be submitted by the state of Indiana deadline (typically April 15) prior to the beginning of the fall semester. Additional documentation may be requested in order to process a student financial aid.

OccasioĥallŽ, studeĥts ĤaŽ Ɗĥd it ĥecessaŋŽ to ŶaŋŽ theiŋ eĥŋollĤeĥt status ǜi.e., chaĥgiĥg fŋoĤ full tiĤe to paŋt tiĤeǝ. Because eligibilitŽ of Ɗĥaĥcial aid pŋogŋaĤs is ŋelated diŋectlŽ to eĥŋollĤeĥt status, studeĥts should coĥsult ŷith the Office of Fiĥaĥcial Aid aĥd Scholarships to leaŋĥ ŷhat effect, if aĥŽ, theiŋ coĥteĤplated chaĥge ŷill haŶe oĥ theiŋ Ɗĥaĥcial aid.

Fedeŋal ŋegulatioĥs Ĥaĥdate that colleges aĥd uĥiŶeŋsities establish staĥdaŋds of SatisfactoŋŽ AcadeĤic Pŋogŋess ǜSAPǝ foŋ studeĥts ŷho ŋeceiŶe fedeŋal Ɗĥaĥcial aid. Iĥ oŋdeŋ to Ĥaiĥtaiĥ a coĥsisteĥt policŽ foŋ all studeĥts ŋeceiŶiĥg Ɗĥaĥcial assistaĥce, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ has adopted these saĤe staĥdaŋds iĥ the adĤiĥistŋatioĥ of all iĥstitutioĥallŽ aŷaŋded fuĥds as ŷell. A ŋeŶieŷ of a studeĥtǭs SAP status ŷill be Ĥade at the eĥd of each seĤesteŋ, iĥcludiĥg a suĤĤeŋ teŋĤ if the studeĥt is eĥŋolled iĥ a  suĤĤeŋ teŋĤ.

- MażiĤuĤ NuĤbeŋ of AtteĤpted Houŋs. Studeĥts aŋe eligible to ŋeceiŶe Ɗĥaĥcial aid, pŋoŶided all otheŋ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of the SAP PolicŽ haŶe beeĥ Ĥet, so loĥg as the ĥuĤbeŋ of atteĤpted houŋs does ĥot eżceed ƐƔƏ% of the ĥuĤbeŋ of houŋs ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ theiŋ degŋee. Tŋaĥsfeŋ houŋs that applŽ toŷaŋds the degŋee ŷill be coĥsideŋed as atteĤpted houŋs. Oĥce a studeĥtǭs ĥuĤbeŋ of atteĤpted houŋs eżceeds ƐƔƏ% of the ĥuĤbeŋ of houŋs ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ theiŋ degŋee, oŋ if it is ĥo loĥgeŋ ĤatheĤaticallŽ possible foŋ the studeĥt to coĤplete theiŋ degŋee ŷithiĥ the ĤażiĤuĤ ĥuĤbeŋ of atteĤpted houŋs alloŷed, the studeĥt ŷill be deĥied eligibilitŽ foŋ Ɗĥaĥcial aid.
- MiĥiĤuĤ CuĤulatiŶe Gŋade Poiĥt AŶeŋage ǜGPAǝ ReŊuiŋed. Studeĥts aŋe eligible to ŋeceiŶe Ɗĥaĥcial aid, pŋoŶided all otheŋ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of the SAP PolicŽ haŶe beeĥ Ĥet, so loĥg as theŽ Ĥaiĥtaiĥ the ĤiĥiĤuĤ cuĤulatiŶe GPA as listed beloŷ. Studeĥts ŷho fall beloŷ the ĤiĥiĤuĤ cuĤulatiŶe GPA ŷill be placed oĥ a ǪWaŋĥiĥgǫ status foŋ Ɗĥaĥcial aid.

Studeĥts oĥ a Waŋĥiĥg status Ĥust iĥcŋease theiŋ cuĤulatiŶe GPA to Ĥeet SAP eligibilitŽ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts bŽ the eĥd of the folloŷiĥg seĤesteŋ. If SAP eligibilitŽ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts aŋe ĥot Ĥet at the eĥd of the folloŷiĥg seĤesteŋ, the studeĥt ŷill be deĥied theiŋ eligibilitŽ foŋ Ɗĥaĥcial aid. ǜSee Fiĥaĥcial Aid Appeals beloŷǝ.  Withdŋaŷĥ classes aĥd tŋaĥsfeŋ cŋedits aŋe ĥot used iĥ the deteŋĤiĥatioĥ of the studeĥtǭs gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage. Repeated classes ŷill be used iĥ the deteŋĤiĥatioĥ of the gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage. AĥŽ IĥcoĤplete ǜIǝ that is chaĥged to aĥotheŋ gŋade ŷill be ŋeŶieŷed at the ĥeżt seĤesteŋ ŋeŶieŷ.

## Houŋs Eaŋĥed MiĥiĤuĤ CuĤulatiŶe GPA:

Ɛ-ƑƘ coĤpleted cŋedit houŋs = Ɛ.ƕƏ ĤiĥiĤuĤ GPA ƒƏ-ƔƘ houŋs coĤpleted cŋedit houŋs = Ɛ.ƗƏ ĤiĥiĤuĤ GPA ƕƏ oŋ Ĥoŋe coĤpleted cŋedit houŋs = Ƒ.ƏƏ ĤiĥiĤuĤ GPA

- MiĥiĤuĤ NuĤbeŋ of Eaŋĥed Houŋs ReŊuiŋed. Studeĥts aŋe eligible to ŋeceiŶe Ɗĥaĥcial aid, pŋoŶided all otheŋ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of the SAP PolicŽ haŶe beeĥ Ĥet, so loĥg as theŽ eaŋĥ at least ƕƖ% of atteĤpted houŋs. Studeĥts ŷho do ĥot eaŋĥ at least ƕƖ% of theiŋ atteĤpted houŋs ŷill be placed oĥ a ǪWaŋĥiĥgǫ status foŋ Ɗĥaĥcial aid. Studeĥts oĥ a Waŋĥiĥg status Ĥust Ĥeet SAP eligibilitŽ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts bŽ the eĥd of the folloŷiĥg seĤesteŋ. If SAP eligibilitŽ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts aŋe ĥot Ĥet at the eĥd of the folloŷiĥg seĤesteŋ, the studeĥt ŷill be deĥied theiŋ eligibilitŽ foŋ Ɗĥaĥcial aid. ǜSee Fiĥaĥcial Aid Appeals beloŷǝ. Withdŋaŷĥ classes iĥ ŷhich studeĥts ŋeceiŶe a gŋade of ǪWǫ ǜŷithdŋaŷǝ, ŋepeated classes, classes iĥ ŷhich theŽ haŶe IĥcoĤpletes ǜIǝ, aĥd tŋaĥsfeŋ cŋedits aŋe all coĥsideŋed atteĤpted houŋs. AĥŽ IĥcoĤplete ǜIǝ that is chaĥged to aĥotheŋ gŋade ŷill be ŋeŶieŷed at the ĥeżt seĤesteŋ ŋeŶieŷ.

Studeĥts ŷho fail to Ĥeet SAP aŋe ĥot eligible to ŋeceiŶe Ɗĥaĥcial aid but aŋe eligible foŋ ŋeiĥstateĤeĥt of theiŋ Ɗĥaĥcial aid folloŷiĥg the coĤpletioĥ of at least tŷelŶe ǜƐƑǝ cŋedit houŋs aĥd bŽ eaŋĥiĥg at least a Ƒ.Ə GPA foŋ those houŋs. Such couŋseŷoŋk caĥ be coĤpleted at aĥŽ accŋedited college oŋ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ. To ŋeŊuest ŋeiĥstateĤeĥt of eligibilitŽ studeĥts ŷill be ŋeŊuiŋed to subĤit a copŽ of theiŋ Ĥost ŋeceĥt tŋaĥscŋipt ŷhich shoŷs the coĤpletioĥ of at least tŷelŶe ǜƐƑǝ cŋedit houŋs ŷith at least a Ƒ.Ə GPA aloĥg ŷith aĥ appŋoŶed acadeĤic plaĥ.

A studeĥt ĤaŽ appeal uĥdeŋ aĥŽ coĥditioĥ that coĥstitutes aĥ eżteĥuatiĥg aĥd/oŋ Ĥitigatiĥg ciŋcuĤstaĥce aĥd ŷheŋe such ciŋcuĤstaĥces coĥtŋibuted to theiŋ failuŋe to Ĥeet the uĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs staĥdaŋd of SAP.

Additioĥal policies aĥd pŋoceduŋes aŋe aŶailable fŋoĤ the OfƊce of Fiĥaĥcial Aid aĥd Scholaŋships oŋ oĥliĥe at https://aĥdersoĥ.edu/adĤissioĥs/fiĥaĥcial-aid/resources/ .

## REFUND POLICY

Studeĥts ŷithdŋaŷiĥg fŋoĤ all classes afteŋ classes haŶe beguĥ oŋ ŋeduciĥg the ĥuĤbeŋ of houŋs caŋŋied ĤaŽ be eĥtitled to a ŋeductioĥ iĥ chaŋges foŋ tuitioĥ, housiĥg aĥd Ĥeals. Reductioĥs foŋ ŷithdŋaŷals oŋ schedule ŋeŶisioĥs occuŋŋiĥg oĥ oŋ befoŋe the eĥd ofǍ

- Ɗŋst ŷeek of classes ǥ ƘƏ% ŋeductioĥ
- secoĥd ŷeek of classes ǥ ƘƏ% ŋeductioĥ
- thiŋd ŷeek of classes ǥ ƖƔ% ŋeductioĥ
- fouŋth ŷeek of classes ǥ ĥo ŋeductioĥ

AdjustĤeĥts aŋe based upoĥ the date of ofƊcial ŷithdŋaŷal. OfƊcial ŷithdŋaŷal fŋoĤ all classes Ĥust be ŋeŊuested bŽ coĤpletiĥg aĥd subĤittiĥg a Withdŋaŷal/Not Retuŋĥiĥg foŋĤ.

Reductioĥs aŋe based oĥ chaŋges Ĥade to studeĥts aĥd ĥot the aĤouĥt paid oĥ the studeĥtsǭ accouĥts. Theŋe is ĥo ŋeductioĥ of aĥŽ chaŋges foŋ studeĥts ŷho haŶe beeĥ disĤissed oŋ suspeĥded foŋ discipliĥaŋŽ ŋeasoĥs. Pŋopoŋtioĥal adjustĤeĥts ĤaŽ be Ĥade foŋ suĤĤeŋ sessioĥs aĥd those classes ŷheŋe the staŋt dates aŋe ĥot paŋt of the staĥdaŋd teŋĤ dates.

Questioĥs coĥceŋĥiĥg the policŽ foŋ coĤplete ŷithdŋaŷal should be diŋected to the Deaĥ of Studeĥt Life. Questioĥs of adjustĤeĥt foŋ ŋeduciĥg the ĥuĤbeŋ of houŋs should be diŋected to the OfƊce of the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ.

## VETERANS BENEFITS

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ atteĤpts to Ĥake a good-faith effoŋt to coĤplŽ ŷith EżecutiŶe Oŋdeŋ ƐƒƕƏƖǍ establishiĥg pŋiĥciples of eżcelleĥce foŋ educatioĥal iĥstitutioĥs seŋŶiĥg seŋŶice ĤeĤbeŋs, Ŷeteŋaĥs, spouses, aĥd otheŋ faĤilŽ ĤeĤbeŋs. These pŋiĥciples ŷeŋe established to stŋeĥgtheĥ oŶeŋsight, eĥfoŋceĤeĥt, aĥd accouĥtabilitŽ of educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤs aĥd to eĥsuŋe all seŋŶice ĤeĤbeŋs, Ŷeteŋaĥs, aĥd theiŋ faĤilies haŶe the ĥecessaŋŽ iĥfoŋĤatioĥ theŽ ĥeed to Ĥake iĥfoŋĤed decisioĥs coĥceŋĥiĥg theiŋ educatioĥal goals. Iĥ additioĥ, ŷe adŶise seŋŶice ĤeĤbeŋs to speak ŷith aĥ educatioĥ seŋŶices ofƊceŋ oŋ couĥseloŋ ŷithiĥ theiŋ ĤilitaŋŽ seŋŶice pŋioŋ to eĥŋolliĥg at the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ coĤplies ŷith ŋegulatioĥs of the State of Iĥdiaĥa DepaŋtĤeĥt of Veteŋaĥs Affaiŋs, Veteŋaĥs Educatioĥal Uĥit, iĥcludiĥg appŋoŶal of the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ caleĥdaŋ, tuitioĥ aĥd fees schedule, aĥd the acadeĤic policies of the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ. The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ is authoŋized to eĥŋoll ŋecipieĥts of the Veteŋaĥs AdĤiĥistŋatioĥ Educatioĥal beĥeƊts iĥ ŋegulaŋlŽ scheduled cŋedit couŋses leadiĥg to staĥdaŋd college degŋees.

IĥŊuiŋies coĥceŋĥiĥg eligibilitŽ should be diŋected to the DepaŋtĤeĥt of Veteŋaĥs Affaiŋs. IĥdiŶiduals plaĥĥiĥg to studŽ uĥdeŋ oĥe of the educatioĥ chapteŋs should ŋeceiŶe appŋoŶal befoŋe eĥŋolliĥg. Moŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ is aŶailable oĥliĥe at aĥdersoĥ.edu/registrar/Ŷeteraĥs .

## VA Chapteŋ ƒƐ aĥd Chapteŋ ƒƒ Post Ƙ/ƐƐ GI Bill®Ǥ AssessĤeĥt of Late Fees .

Iĥ accoŋdaĥce ŷith Title ƒƗ US Code ƒƕƖƘ ǜeǝ, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ adopts the folloŷiĥg pŋoŶisioĥs foŋ aĥŽ studeĥts usiĥg U.S. DepaŋtĤeĥt of Veteŋaĥs Affaiŋs ǜVAǝ Post Ƙ/ƐƐ GI Bill® ǜCh. ƒƒǝ oŋ Vocatioĥal Rehabilitatioĥ &amp; EĤploŽĤeĥt ǜCh. ƒƐǝ beĥeƊts, ŷhile paŽĤeĥt to the iĥstitutioĥ is peĥdiĥg fŋoĤ the VA. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷill ĥotǍ

- PŋeŶeĥt the studeĥtǭs eĥŋollĤeĥtǎ
- Assess a late peĥaltŽ fee to the studeĥtǎ
- ReŊuiŋe the studeĥt to secuŋe alteŋĥatiŶe oŋ additioĥal fuĥdiĥgǎ

- DeĥŽ the studeĥt access to aĥŽ ŋesouŋces ǜaccess to classes, libŋaŋies, oŋ otheŋ iĥstitutioĥal facilitiesǝ aŶailable to otheŋ studeĥts ŷho haŶe satisƊed theiŋ tuitioĥ aĥd fee bills to the iĥstitutioĥ.

HoŷeŶeŋ, to ŊualifŽ foŋ this pŋoŶisioĥ, such studeĥts aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed toǍ

- Pŋoduce the VA CeŋtiƊcate of EligibilitŽ ǜCOEǝ oŋ Chaĥge of PŋogŋaĤ oŋ Place of Tŋaiĥiĥg FoŋĤ ƑƑ-ƐƘƏƔ.
- All studeĥts Ĥust subĤit a VA Educatioĥ BeĥeƊt ReŊuest FoŋĤ foŋ each seĤesteŋ theŽ iĥteĥd to ŋeceiŶe VA paŽĤeĥts. Studeĥtsǭ classes ŷoĥǭt be ceŋtiƊed to the VA uĥless theŽ aŋe eĥŋolled iĥ the classes.

Cuŋŋeĥt aĥd adĤitted studeĥts ŷho haŶe Ŋuestioĥs about VA beĥeƊts ĤaŽ also addŋess iĥŊuiŋies to the OfƊce of the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ oŋ to the OfƊce of Fiĥaĥcial Aid aĥd Scholaŋships.

GI Bill® is a ŋegisteŋed tŋadeĤaŋk of the U.S. DepaŋtĤeĥt of Veteŋaĥs Affaiŋs ǜVAǝ. Moŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ about educatioĥ beĥeƊts offeŋed bŽ VA is aŶailable at the ofƊcial U.S. goŶeŋĥĤeĥt ŷebsite at https://ŷŷŷ.beĥefits.Ŷa.goŶ/gibill .

## AcadeĤic Policies
