## ACADEMIC FORGIVENESS

The AcadeĤic FoŋgiŶeĥess PolicŽ eżteĥds to a studeĥt ŷho has beeĥ aŷaŽ fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ foŋ a peŋiod of at least ƊŶe Žeaŋs aĥd ŷas ĥot Ĥakiĥg satisfactoŋŽ acadeĤic pŋogŋess, Ĥeaĥiĥg aĥ oŶeŋall GPA of less thaĥ Ƒ.Ə. This is a oĥe-tiĤe oppoŋtuĥitŽ to establish a ĥeŷ GPA.

The policŽ ŷill ĥot applŽ if a studeĥt has eaŋĥed a degŋee, diploĤa, oŋ ceŋtiƊcate fŋoĤ aĥotheŋ college oŋ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ. A studeĥt ŋeceiŶiĥg acadeĤic foŋgiŶeĥess is ĥot eligible foŋ gŋaduatioĥ hoĥoŋs. The studeĥt Ĥust ĥot haŶe beeĥ eĥŋolled iĥ aĥŽ couŋseŷoŋk foŋ cŋedit at Aĥdeŋsoĥ foŋ a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of ƊŶe coĥsecutiŶe Žeaŋs pŋioŋ to the poiĥt of ŋeŊuestiĥg acadeĤic foŋgiŶeĥess. Studeĥts ŷho eaŋĥ gŋades of C-, D, F, oŋ WF ĤaŽ ŋeŊuest up to ƐƔ-seĤesteŋ cŋedits.

Upoĥ ŋeadĤissioĥ to AU, the studeĥt Ĥust deĤoĥstŋate acadeĤic abilitŽ bŽ successfullŽ coĤpletiĥg ƐƑ seĤesteŋ cŋedits at the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ, ŷith ĥo gŋades beloŷ a C. Studeĥts ŷho Ĥeet these tŷo coĥditioĥs ĤaŽ petitioĥ iĥ ŷŋitiĥg to the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋegistŋaŋ bŽ coĤpletiĥg aĥ acadeĤic foŋgiŶeĥess applicatioĥ to haŶe theiŋ gŋades foŋgiŶeĥ aĥd ĥot coĤputed iĥ the gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage aĥd haŶe the ŷoŋds ǪacadeĤic foŋgiŶeĥessǫ aĥĥotated oĥ theiŋ ŋecoŋd.

Oĥce the applicatioĥ foŋ acadeĤic foŋgiŶeĥess has beeĥ appŋoŶed aĥd afteŋ coĥsultatioĥ ŷith the studeĥt, the OfƊce of the Registŋaŋ ŷill Ĥake the folloŷiĥg adjustĤeĥts to the studeĥtǭs tŋaĥscŋiptǍ Up to ƐƔ seĤesteŋ cŋedits of couŋseŷoŋk, to be selected bŽ the studeĥt, ŷill be ŋesciĥded pŋioŋ to the poiĥt of acadeĤic foŋgiŶeĥessǎ hoŷeŶeŋ, couŋse titles aĥd gŋades fŋoĤ these couŋses ŷill ŋeĤaiĥ oĥ the tŋaĥscŋipt. Calculatioĥ of the studeĥtǭs GPA ŷill ĥot iĥclude gŋades foŋ classes appŋoŶed foŋ foŋgiŶeĥess. Foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ, coĥtact the Office of the Registrar .

## ACADEMIC INTEGRITY

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ seeks to suppoŋt aĥd pŋoĤote Ŋualities of acadeĤic hoĥestŽ aĥd peŋsoĥal iĥtegŋitŽ aĥd ŋegaŋds cheatiĥg, plagiaŋisĤ aĥd all otheŋ foŋĤs of acadeĤic dishoĥestŽ as seŋious offeĥses agaiĥst the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ coĤĤuĥitŽ. Such offeĥses ŷill be dealt ŷith iĥ aĥ appŋopŋiate Ĥaĥĥeŋ.

Cheatiĥg oŋ acadeĤic dishoĥestŽ is deƊĥed as the deceptioĥ of otheŋs about oĥe's oŷĥ ŷoŋk oŋ about the ŷoŋk of aĥotheŋ. EżaĤples of cheatiĥg iĥclude but aŋe ĥot liĤited toǍ

- Ɛ. SubĤittiĥg aĥotheŋ's ŷoŋk as oĥe's oŷĥ oŋ alloŷiĥg aĥotheŋ to subĤit oĥe's ŷoŋk as though it ŷeŋe his oŋ heŋs.
- Ƒ. Failuŋe to ackĥoŷledge pŋopeŋlŽ authoŋities Ŋuoted, cited, oŋ coĥsulted iĥ the pŋepaŋatioĥ of ŷŋitteĥ ŷoŋk ǜplagiaŋisĤǝ.
- ƒ. The use of aĥŽ ŋesouŋces duŋiĥg aĥ eżaĤiĥatioĥ ŷithout peŋĤissioĥ of the iĥstŋuctoŋ.
- Ɠ. The gettiĥg oŋ giŶiĥg of uĥauthoŋized help oĥ assigĥĤeĥts.
- Ɣ. TaĤpeŋiĥg ŷith eżpeŋiĤeĥtal data to obtaiĥ a "desiŋed" ŋesult oŋ cŋeatiĥg ŋesults foŋ eżpeŋiĤeĥts ĥot doĥe ǜdŋŽ labbiĥgǝ.
- ƕ. TaĤpeŋiĥg ŷith oŋ destŋoŽiĥg the acadeĤic ŷoŋk of otheŋs.
- Ɩ. SubĤittiĥg substaĥtial poŋtioĥs of the saĤe acadeĤic ŷoŋk foŋ cŋedit oŋ hoĥoŋs Ĥoŋe thaĥ oĥce ŷithout peŋĤissioĥ of the pŋeseĥt iĥstŋuctoŋ.
- Ɨ. LŽiĥg about these oŋ otheŋ acadeĤic Ĥatteŋs.

Studeĥts ŷho aŋe guiltŽ of such acadeĤic Ŷiolatioĥs caĥ eżpect to be peĥalized. Aĥ iĥstŋuctoŋ ŷhose deƊĥitioĥ of cheatiĥg ĤaŽ diffeŋ fŋoĤ that stated aboŶe has the ŋespoĥsibilitŽ aĥd obligatioĥ to iĥfoŋĤ studeĥts, iĥ ŷŋitiĥg, at the begiĥĥiĥg of the couŋse. Those iĥstŋuctoŋs ŷho fail to do so haŶe ĥo basis foŋ discipliĥaŋŽ actioĥ iĥ iĥstaĥces of puŋpoŋted studeĥt dishoĥestŽ outside of the pŋoŶisioĥs stated aboŶe.

The couŋse iĥstŋuctoŋ shall haŶe the authoŋitŽ to deal ŷith iĥstaĥces of acadeĤic dishoĥestŽ ŷithiĥ the fŋaĤeŷoŋk of the folloŷiĥg guideliĥes.

- Ɛ. FacultŽ ĤeĤbeŋs Ĥust ŋepoŋt aĥŽ studeĥt ŷho has sigĥiƊcaĥtlŽ Ŷiolated the policŽ oĥ acadeĤic iĥtegŋitŽ to the OfƊce of the PŋoŶost usiĥg the AcadeĤic IĥtegŋitŽ Violatioĥ ŋepoŋt foŋĤ. Folloŷiĥg tŷo ŋepoŋts agaiĥst a paŋticulaŋ studeĥt, actioĥ ŷill be iĥitiated uĥdeŋ pŋoŶisioĥs of the judicial code aĥd ĤaŽ lead to disĤissal of the studeĥt fŋoĤ the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ.
- Ƒ. The ĤażiĤuĤ assessable peĥaltŽ foŋ a Ɗŋst offeĥse shall ĥot eżceed double the oŋigiĥal Ŷalue of the assigĥĤeĥt plus ĥo optioĥ to Ĥake up the ŷoŋk iĥ Ŋuestioĥ.
- ƒ. Alteŋĥate couŋses of actioĥ ĤaŽ iĥclude, but aŋe ĥot liĤited to, the folloŷiĥgǍ
- a. Woŋk ĤaŽ be ŋedoĥe foŋ full oŋ paŋtial cŋedit.
- b. Alteŋĥate assigĥĤeĥts ĤaŽ be giŶeĥ foŋ full oŋ paŋtial cŋedit.
- c. Woŋk ĤaŽ ĥot be ŋedoĥe aĥd ĥo cŋedit ŷill be giŶeĥ foŋ that paŋticulaŋ assigĥĤeĥt.

The studeĥt has the ŋight to appeal actioĥs uĥdeŋ this policŽ thŋough the ŋegulaŋ chaĥĥels as established bŽ the gŋade appeal pŋocess.

Gŋouĥds foŋ appeal aŋeǍ

- Ɛ. iĥsufƊcieĥt eŶideĥce of dishoĥestŽǎ
- Ƒ. peĥalties assessed iĥ eżcess of those alloŷed uĥdeŋ the aboŶe guideliĥesǎ oŋ
- ƒ. pŋoŶisioĥs of gŋade appeal cited iĥ the Studeĥt Haĥdbook.

Iĥ all iĥstaĥces of acadeĤic dishoĥestŽ, iĥstŋuctoŋs aŋe uŋged to couĥsel offeĥdeŋs aĥd, if ĥecessaŋŽ, ŋefeŋ theĤ to the PŋoŶost foŋ Ĥoŋe eżteĥsiŶe coĥŶeŋsatioĥs.

## ACADEMIC LEAVE OF ABSENCE

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ offeŋs uĥdeŋgŋaduate studeĥts ŷho aŋe iĥ good staĥdiĥg, as deƊĥed bŽ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs acadeĤic policŽ, aĥd ŷho aŋe ĥot subject to discipliĥaŋŽ actioĥ the oppoŋtuĥitŽ to ŋeŊuest aĥ acadeĤic leaŶe of abseĥce.

The LeaŶe of Abseĥce PolicŽ applies toǍ

- studeĥts ŷho aŋe puŋsuiĥg a degŋee fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ but leaŶe the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ foŋ a seĤesteŋ to paŋticipate iĥ a studŽ-abŋoad pŋogŋaĤ, iĥteŋĥship, oŋ pŋacticuĤ, ŷhich is ĥot doĥe ŷith aĥ AU Ĥatŋiculatioĥ
- studeĥts ŷho, due to ciŋcuĤstaĥces beŽoĥd theiŋ coĥtŋol ǜsuch as the ĥeed to caŋe foŋ ill paŋeĥts oŋ the oĥset of a peŋsoĥal illĥess oŋ ĤilitaŋŽ tŋaiĥiĥgǝ, Ĥust suspeĥd theiŋ eĥŋollĤeĥt iĥ classes foŋ a seĤesteŋ

A leaŶe of abseĥce ĤaŽ be gŋaĥted foŋ oĥe seĤesteŋ but, depeĥdiĥg oĥ the speciƊc ciŋcuĤstaĥces, ĤaŽ be gŋaĥted foŋ a full acadeĤic Žeaŋ if the studeĥt iĥteĥds to ŋetuŋĥ to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ foŋ the coĤpletioĥ of theiŋ degŋee. To ŊualifŽ, studeĥts Ĥust be iĥ good acadeĤic aĥd Ɗĥaĥcial staĥdiĥg aĥd Ĥust coĤplete the ŋeŊuiŋed applicatioĥ foŋĤs.

The acadeĤic ŋecoŋds of studeĥts gŋaĥted a leaŶe of abseĥce ŋeĤaiĥ iĥ aĥ actiŶe status. While oĥ acadeĤic leaŶe of abseĥce, the studeĥt ŋetaiĥs the ŋight to use soĤe caĤpus facilities such as the AU libŋaŋŽ, studeĥt couĥseliĥg seŋŶices, aĥd caŋeeŋ seŋŶices.

Due to Visa ŋestŋictioĥs, iĥteŋĥatioĥal studeĥts aŋe ĥot eligible foŋ acadeĤic leaŶe aĥd should coĥsult ŷith theiŋ Desigĥated School OfƊcial ǜDSOǝ. Foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ, coĥtact the Ceĥteŋ foŋ Studeĥt Life.

## ACADEMIC LOAD

A full-tiĤe acadeĤic load is ƐƑ-ƐƗ houŋs. Upoĥ appŋoŶal fŋoĤ theiŋ college deaĥ, studeĥts ŷith ŋecoŋds of aboŶe-aŶeŋage acadeĤic peŋfoŋĤaĥce ĤaŽ ŋegisteŋ at additioĥal cost foŋ additioĥal houŋs. SuĤĤeŋ school teŋĤs, iĥteŋĥatioĥal oppoŋtuĥitŽ, oŋ tŋaĥsfeŋ ŷoŋk ĤaŽ ĥot be used to establish a seĤesteŋ GPA.

The ĥuĤbeŋ of houŋs takeĥ each seĤesteŋ is depeĥdeĥt upoĥ a studeĥtǭs GPAǍ

- Studeĥts ŷith a ƒ.ƑƔ GPA ĤaŽ ŋegisteŋ foŋ ƐƘ houŋs
- Studeĥts ŷith a ƒ.Ɣ GPA ĤaŽ ŋegisteŋ foŋ ƑƏ houŋs
- Studeĥts ŷith a ƒ.ƖƔ GPA ĤaŽ ŋegisteŋ foŋ ƑƐ houŋs

These guideliĥes also applŽ to studeĥts ŷho haŶe eaŋĥed ƔƑ oŋ Ĥoŋe houŋs aĥd ŷhose cuĤulatiŶe GPAs at the tiĤe of ŋegistŋatioĥ Ĥeet the stated staĥdaŋds. The factoŋs of pŋeŶious acadeĤic achieŶeĤeĥt, tŽpes of couŋses to be takeĥ, aĥd deĤaĥds of eĤploŽĤeĥt Ĥust also be ŋecogĥized.

## ACADEMIC NOTICE

Studeĥts ĤaŽ be dŋopped fŋoĤ the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ at aĥŽ tiĤe ŷheĥ eżcessiŶe class abseĥces oŋ acadeĤic peŋfoŋĤaĥce iĥdicates aĥ iĥabilitŽ oŋ uĥŷilliĥgĥess to achieŶe ĥoŋĤal pŋogŋess toŷaŋd a degŋee. TŽpicallŽ, hoŷeŶeŋ, studeĥts ĥot iĥ good acadeĤic staĥdiĥg aŋe placed oĥ acadeĤic ĥotice foŋ a ĤażiĤuĤ of tŷo coĥsecutiŶe seĤesteŋs.

Iĥ geĥeŋal, studeĥts oĥ acadeĤic ĥotice ĤaŽ ĥot paŋticipate iĥ aĥŽ eżtŋacuŋŋiculaŋ actiŶities. The pŋoŶost has the Ɗĥal authoŋitŽ oŶeŋ the coĥditioĥs placed upoĥ studeĥts oĥ acadeĤic ĥotice.

Befoŋe atteĥdiĥg classes, studeĥts oĥ acadeĤic ĥotice aŋe eżpected to sigĥ aĥ acadeĤic suppoŋt coĥtŋact ŷith the diŋectoŋ of educatioĥal suppoŋt seŋŶices. The coĥtŋact ĤaŽ iĥclude, but is ĥot liĤited to, such iteĤs as studŽ assistaĥceǎ ŋestŋictioĥs oĥ ŷoŋk coĤĤitĤeĥts, housiĥg, couŋse loadǎ beiĥg assigĥed to LART ƐƏƏƏ ǎ aĥd class atteĥdaĥce.

## ACADEMIC PROGRESSION

AĥŽ studeĥt ĥot achieŶiĥg acceptable staĥdaŋds ĤaŽ be baŋŋed fŋoĤ ŋetuŋĥiĥg to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ foŋ a peŋiod of at least oĥe seĤesteŋ. Studeĥts ŷho aŋe ŋeadĤitted afteŋ haŶiĥg beeĥ baŋŋed oĥce aŋe eżpected to attaiĥ a Ƒ.Ə cuŋŋeĥt GPA iĥ theiŋ ĥeżt ƐƑ houŋs aĥd Ĥust coĥtiĥue to achieŶe oŋ Ĥake substaĥtial pŋogŋess toŷaŋd the stated ĤiĥiĤuĤ staĥdaŋds iĥ oŋdeŋ to coĥtiĥue. ReadĤitted studeĥts coĤe iĥ uĥdeŋ acadeĤic ĥotice status.  If the studeĥt is baŋŋed a secoĥd tiĤe, it ŷill be foŋ at least tŷo Žeaŋs. AĥŽ subseŊueĥt ŋeadĤissioĥ ŷill be ŋegaŋded as a Ɗĥal oppoŋtuĥitŽ to coĥtiĥue studies at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

The pŋoŶost ĤaŽ ŋeŊuest the AcadeĤic ReŶieŷ CoĤĤittee to ŋeŶieŷ aĥd Ĥake ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥs ŋegaŋdiĥg cases ŷheĥ ĥecessaŋŽ. Eżteĥuatiĥg ciŋcuĤstaĥces ĤaŽ justifŽ the coĥtiĥuatioĥ of studeĥts ŷhose cuĤulatiŶe GPA falls beloŷ the stated staĥdaŋds.

## ACADEMIC STANDING

To ŋeĤaiĥ iĥ good acadeĤic staĥdiĥg, studeĥts Ĥust Ĥaiĥtaiĥ the folloŷiĥg staĥdaŋdsǍ

| Hours Earĥed   | GPA   |
|----------------|-------|
| Ɛ-ƑƘ           | Ɛ.ƕ   |
| ƒƏ-ƔƘ          | Ɛ.Ɨ   |
| ƕƏ oŋ Ĥoŋe     | Ƒ.Ə   |

## ADVANCED PLACEMENT

AdŶaĥced placeĤeĥt aĥd/oŋ cŋedit ĤaŽ be eaŋĥed thŋough placeĤeĥt eżaĤiĥatioĥ foŋ a ĤażiĤuĤ of ƒƏ cŋedits. The fouŋ eżaĤiĥatioĥs Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋecogĥizes, subject to appŋoŶal bŽ the acadeĤic depaŋtĤeĥts, aŋeǍ

- the College Board AdŶaĥced PlaceĤeĥt ǜAPǝ PrograĤ
- the College LeŶel EżaĤiĥatioĥ PrograĤ ǜCLEPǝ
- the CaĤbridge Iĥterĥatioĥal EżaĤiĥatioĥs ǜGCE A leŶelǝ
- the Iĥterĥatioĥal Baccalaureate ǜIBǝ PrograĤ

Cŋedit ŋeceiŶed bŽ eżaĤiĥatioĥ is tuitioĥ- fŋee aĥd applies toŷaŋd gŋaduatioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. Coĥtact the Office of the Registrar foŋ additioĥal iĥfoŋĤatioĥ.

## AUDITING A COURSE

As a Ĥeaĥs of eĥŋichĤeĥt to the degŋee-seekiĥg studeĥt, Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋecogĥizes the folloŷiĥg ŷaŽs of auditiĥg a couŋseǍ

- Ɛ. Occasioĥal class Ŷisitatioĥ Ǎ A studeĥt ĤaŽ ŷish to Ŷisit a class to heaŋ a lectuŋe aĥd/oŋ a discussioĥ oĥ a giŶeĥ topic. The iĥstŋuctoŋǭs coĥseĥt is the oĥlŽ ĥecessaŋŽ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥt.
- Ƒ. Auditiĥg oĥe couŋse ŷithout a fee Ǎ AĥŽ studeĥt ŋegisteŋed foŋ ƐƑ-ƐƗ houŋs ŷho is Ĥakiĥg satisfactoŋŽ acadeĤic pŋogŋess ĤaŽ eĥŋoll iĥ aĥ additioĥal class oĥ aĥ iĥfoŋĤal audit oŋ ŋecoŋded audit basis.
- A. IĥfoŋĤal Audit Ǎ IĥfŋeŊueĥt atteĥdaĥce of a class ŷith ĥo couŋse obligatioĥ. Although foŋĤal ŋegistŋatioĥ is ĥot ŋeŊuiŋed, the studeĥt Ĥust haŶe the ŷŋitteĥ coĥseĥt of the iĥstŋuctoŋ. PeŋĤissioĥ foŋĤs aŋe aŶailable iĥ the Office of the Registrar . No ŋecoŋd is Ĥade of the audit oĥ the studeĥtǭs peŋĤaĥeĥt ŋecoŋd.
- B. Recoŋded Audit Ǎ Regulaŋ atteĥdaĥce ŷith ĥoŋĤal couŋse obligatioĥs foŋ the puŋpose of haŶiĥg the audit ŋecoŋded oĥ the studeĥtǭs peŋĤaĥeĥt ŋecoŋd. Iĥ this situatioĥ, the studeĥt should folloŷ these pŋoceduŋesǍ
- i. Registeŋ as aĥ audit usiĥg the schedule of classes foŋĤ oŋ chaĥge of schedule foŋĤ, sigĥed bŽ the adŶisoŋ.
- ii. Adheŋe to the iĥstŋuctoŋǭs stated atteĥdaĥce policies.
- iii. CoĤplete sufƊcieĥt ŷoŋk of C- ŊualitŽ oŋ betteŋ iĥ oŋdeŋ to haŶe the audit ŋecoŋded.
- iŶ. Chaĥges of schedules to oŋ fŋoĤ aĥ audit Ĥust be doĥe ĥo lateŋ thaĥ the eĥd of the Ɣth ŷeek of the seĤesteŋ.

The couŋse ŷill be ŋecoŋded oĥ the studeĥtǭs peŋĤaĥeĥt ŋecoŋd as aĥ audit if the aboŶe coĥditioĥs aŋe Ĥet aĥd the studeĥt does satisfactoŋŽ ŷoŋk iĥ the couŋse. If the aboŶe coĥditioĥs aŋe ĥot Ĥet, the iĥstŋuctoŋ ŷill ĥotifŽ the OfƊce of the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ aĥd ĥo ŋecoŋd of the audit ŷill be Ĥade.

- ƒ. Auditiĥg ŷith paŽĤeĥt of a fee Ǎ A studeĥt ŷho does ĥot Ĥeet the speciƊc ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts as outliĥed aboŶe ĤaŽ, upoĥ paŽĤeĥt of the audit fee, audit a couŋse as outliĥed uĥdeŋ ǪAǫ oŋ ǪBǫ aboŶe. Full-tiĤe studeĥts aŋe eĥtitled to audit oĥe couŋse peŋ seĤesteŋ at ĥo additioĥal chaŋge. Otheŋ studeĥts ŷill be chaŋged the cuŋŋeĥt fee.

The couŋses ŷill appeaŋ oĥ the tŋaĥscŋipt ŷith a gŋade of "AU" aĥd ŷill ĥot couĥt toŷaŋd acadeĤic cŋedit. Auditiĥg is a policŽ pŋiŶilege eżteĥded to full- aĥd paŋt-tiĤe AU studeĥts oĥlŽ.

## CLASS ATTENDANCE

EffectiŶe leaŋĥiĥg iĥ a uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋeŊuiŋes the actiŶe iĥŶolŶeĤeĥt of both studeĥts aĥd facultŽ. Studeĥts aŋe eżpected to atteĥd all classes uĥless pŋeŶeĥted bŽ eżteĥuatiĥg ciŋcuĤstaĥces. IĥasĤuch as studeĥts aŋe ŋespoĥsible foŋ the leaŋĥiĥg that ĤaŽ deŶelop fŋoĤ both iĥ-class aĥd out-of-class eżpeŋieĥces, theŽ should aĥticipate abseĥces foŋ a good cause ǜsuch as ŶaŋsitŽ athletic tŋips, Ɗeld tŋips, Ĥusic, dŋaĤa, aĥd debate tŋipsǝ aĥd adŶise theiŋ iĥstŋuctoŋs of such abseĥces as faŋ iĥ adŶaĥce as possible.

AĥŽ abseĥce fŋoĤ a class ŋesults iĥ a loss of leaŋĥiĥg foŋ the studeĥt. It is the studeĥtǭs obligatioĥ to peŋsoĥallŽ ĥotifŽ the iĥdiŶidual couŋse iĥstŋuctoŋǜsǝ about aĥŽ abseĥce, iĥ adŶaĥce if possible. Studeĥts ĤaŽ be diŋectlŽ peĥalized oĥlŽ afteŋ the ĥuĤbeŋ of abseĥces eżceeds the ĥuĤbeŋ of class Ĥeetiĥg houŋs peŋ ŷeek. Wheŋe a studeĥt Ĥisses Ĥoŋe thaĥ the ĥuĤbeŋ of classes stated aboŶe, the couŋse iĥstŋuctoŋ has the discŋetioĥ to alloŷ foŋ the coĤpletioĥ of Ĥissed ŷoŋk aĥd to deteŋĤiĥe hoŷ such ŷoŋk ŷill be eŶaluated, iĥcludiĥg possible peĥalties.

## CLASS LEVEL IDENTIFICATION

Class ideĥtiƊcatioĥ at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is deteŋĤiĥed as folloŷsǍ

- FŋeshĤaĥ Ǎ A studeĥt ŷho has coĤpleted feŷeŋ thaĥ ƑƓ houŋs of college cŋedit.
- SophoĤoŋe Ǎ A studeĥt ŷho has coĤpleted ƑƓ-ƔƐ houŋs of college cŋedit.
- Juĥioŋ Ǎ A studeĥt ŷho has coĤpleted ƔƑ-ƗƖ houŋs of college cŋedit.
- Seĥioŋ Ǎ A studeĥt ŷho has coĤpleted ƗƗ oŋ Ĥoŋe houŋs of college cŋedit.
- Loŷeŋ-DiŶisioĥ Ǎ FŋeshĤaĥ aĥd sophoĤoŋe studeĥts.
- Uppeŋ-DiŶisioĥ Ǎ Juĥioŋ aĥd seĥioŋ studeĥts.
- Paŋt-tiĤe Ǎ A studeĥt caŋŋŽiĥg Ɛ-ƐƐ houŋs.
- Special Ǎ Audit, guest studeĥt, oŋ high school studeĥt. Also iĥcludes childŋeĥ oŋ adults ŷho aŋe takiĥg Ĥusic lessoĥs but aŋe ĥot eĥŋolled iĥ acadeĤic ŷoŋk at the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ leŶel.

## COURSE REPETITION

Studeĥts ĤaŽ ŋepeat couŋses foŋ ŷhich theŽ ŋeceiŶed a C- oŋ loŷeŋ bŽ siĤplŽ ŋe-eĥŋolliĥg iĥ the saĤe iĥstitutioĥal couŋses. If studeĥts ŷish to ŋepeat couŋses foŋ ŷhich the depaŋtĤeĥtal captioĥs oŋ ĥuĤbeŋs haŶe chaĥged, theŽ Ĥust petitioĥ the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋegistŋaŋ. FuŋtheŋĤoŋe, studeĥts ĤaŽ ŋepeat couŋses foŋ ŷhich theŽ ŋeceiŶed a C oŋ aboŶe bŽ petitioĥiĥg the deaĥ of the college iĥ ŷhich each couŋse is offeŋed to be gŋaĥted aĥ eżceptioĥ. The folloŷiĥg ŋules applŽ iĥ all casesǍ

- Studeĥts ĤaŽ ŋepeat aĥŽ giŶeĥ couŋse a total of oĥlŽ tŷo tiĤes duŋiĥg theiŋ acadeĤic caŋeeŋ.
- Withdŋaŷal ǜW, WF, oŋ AWǝ gŋade couĥts as aĥ atteĤpt, but it does ĥot chaĥge the pŋeŶious gŋade.
- All pŋeŶious gŋades ŋeceiŶed ŷill ŋeĤaiĥ oĥ studeĥtsǭ acadeĤic ŋecoŋds.
- OĥlŽ the Ĥost ŋeceĥt gŋade ŋeceiŶed ŷill be used iĥ calculatiĥg GPA.
- Cŋedit houŋs eaŋĥed toŷaŋd gŋaduatioĥ ŷill be couĥted foŋ oĥlŽ the Ĥost ŋeceĥt couŋse takeĥ.

This policŽ does ĥot applŽ to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ cŋedit bŽ eżaĤiĥatioĥ oŋ tŋaĥsfeŋ cŋedit. The couŋse ŋepetitioĥ policŽ does ĥot applŽ to couŋses takeĥ at otheŋ colleges oŋ uĥiŶeŋsities aĥd tŋaĥsfeŋŋed to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

## CREDIT HOUR POLICY

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs deƊĥitioĥ of a cŋedit houŋ foŋĤalizes coĤpliaĥce ŷith fedeŋal aĥd accŋeditatioĥ eżpectatioĥs aĥd helps to pŋoŶide coĥsisteĥcŽ thŋoughout the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ. Iĥ geĥeŋal, acadeĤic couŋses coĥstitute betŷeeĥ ƒƔ-ƓƔ houŋs of leaŋĥiĥg eĥgageĤeĥt foŋ each cŋedit houŋ eaŋĥed. Foŋ eżaĤple, oĥe cŋedit is eŊuiŶaleĥt to ƔƏ Ĥiĥutes ǜĤiĥiĤuĤǝ of class tiĤe ǜdiŋect iĥstŋuctioĥǝ aĥd a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of tŷo houŋs of out of class studeĥt ŷoŋk peŋ ŷeek. Theŋefoŋe, a thŋee-cŋedit couŋse ŷill tŽpicallŽ Ĥeet ƐƔƏ Ĥiĥutes peŋ ŷeek foŋ ƐƔ ŷeeks ǜƒƖ.ƔƏ houŋs, diŋect facultŽ iĥstŋuctioĥǝ. Cŋedit houŋ guideliĥes foŋ Ŷaŋious Ĥodalities aŋe as folloŷsǍ

## ClassŋooĤ Iĥstŋuctioĥ ǜFace-to-Faceǝ

- Lectuŋe/SeĤiĥaŋ: Couŋses focus oĥ pŋiĥciples, coĥcepts oŋ ideas, lectuŋe, discussioĥ aĥd deĤoĥstŋatioĥ. A seĤesteŋ cŋedit houŋ is eaŋĥed acŋoss ƐƔ ŷeeks foŋ thŋee ƔƏ-Ĥiĥute sessioĥs peŋ ŷeek oŋ tŷo ƖƔ-Ĥiĥute sessioĥs peŋ ŷeek of diŋect facultŽ iĥstŋuctioĥ ŷith a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of tŷo houŋs of studeĥt leaŋĥiĥg eĥgageĤeĥt outside of class peŋ ŷeek thŋoughout the seĤesteŋ. Foŋ eżaĤple, a tŽpical thŋee-cŋedit houŋ couŋse Ĥeets foŋ thŋee, ƔƏ-Ĥiĥute sessioĥs oŋ tŷo, ƖƔ-Ĥiĥute sessioĥs a ŷeek foŋ Ɗfteeĥ ŷeeks. Most lectuŋe aĥd seĤiĥaŋ couŋses aŋe aŷaŋded ƒ cŋedits.

- Acceleŋated: Couŋses offeŋed ŷithiĥ the staĥdaŋd ƐƔ-ŷeek teŋĤ but iĥ aĥ acceleŋated foŋĤat ǜe.g. Ɩ oŋ Ɨ ŷeeksǝ. The coĥteĥt aĥd substaĥtiŶe leaŋĥiĥg outcoĤes aŋe the saĤe. These couŋses Ĥust Ĥeet the deƊĥitioĥ of staĥdaŋd lectuŋe coĥtact tiĤe aĥd out of class eĥgaged leaŋĥiĥg ŷithiĥ the tiĤe fŋaĤe the acceleŋated Ŷeŋsioĥ is offeŋed.

## Pŋactical Applicatioĥ

- LaboŋatoŋŽ: Couŋses ŷheŋe the Ĥajoŋ focus is oĥ Ǫhaĥds oĥǫ eżpeŋieĥce to suppoŋt studeĥt leaŋĥiĥg ǜuse of eŊuipĤeĥt, actiŶities, tools, Ĥachiĥes geĥeŋallŽ fouĥd iĥ a laboŋatoŋŽǝ. Oĥe to tŷo LaboŋatoŋŽ cŋedits ŋepŋeseĥts a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of Ɛ houŋ peŋ ŷeek of lectuŋe oŋ discussioĥ plus a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of Ƒ-Ɠ houŋs of scheduled supeŋŶised oŋ iĥdepeĥdeĥt laboŋatoŋŽ ŷoŋk.
- Studio: Couŋses taught as applied studŽ oĥ a pŋiŶate oŋ seĤi-pŋiŶate basis. Studeĥts ŋeceiŶe aĥŽŷheŋe fŋoĤ oĥe to tŷo cŋedits foŋ applied Ĥusic couŋses. PŋiŶate iĥstŋuctioĥ ŋaĥges fŋoĤ ƒƏ to ƕƏ Ĥiĥutes ŷith iĥdepeĥdeĥt pŋactice as pŋescŋibed bŽ the iĥstŋuctoŋ.
- Iĥteŋĥship/Field Eżpeŋieĥce: Couŋses deŶeloped foŋ iĥdepeĥdeĥt leaŋĥiĥg aĥd the deŶelopĤeĥt aĥd applicatioĥ of job ŋelated oŋ pŋactical skills iĥ a paŋticulaŋ discipliĥe. These couŋses alloŷ foŋ obseŋŶatioĥ, paŋticipatioĥ, aĥd Ɗeldŷoŋk, aĥd aŋe geĥeŋallŽ offeŋed off caĤpus. Iĥteŋĥship tiĤe iĥcludes a coĤbiĥatioĥ of supeŋŶised tiĤe bŽ appŋoŶed eżpeŋts outside the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ, studeĥt assigĥĤeĥts, aĥd tiĤe supeŋŶised bŽ a uĥiŶeŋsitŽ iĥstŋuctoŋ.
- PŋacticuĤ/Studeĥt Teachiĥg: Couŋses deŶeloped foŋ iĥdepeĥdeĥt leaŋĥiĥg aĥd the deŶelopĤeĥt aĥd applicatioĥ of job-ŋelated oŋ pŋactical skills iĥ a paŋticulaŋ discipliĥe. These couŋses alloŷ foŋ obseŋŶatioĥ, paŋticipatioĥ, clieĥt eŶaluatioĥ, Ɗeldŷoŋk, aĥd aŋe offeŋed off caĤpus. Iĥteŋĥship tiĤe iĥcludes a coĤbiĥatioĥ of supeŋŶised tiĤe bŽ appŋoŶed eżpeŋts outside the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ, studeĥt assigĥĤeĥts, aĥd tiĤe supeŋŶised bŽ a uĥiŶeŋsitŽ iĥstŋuctoŋ ǜsee aboŶeǝ.
- Cliĥical PlaceĤeĥt: SupeŋŶised eżpeŋieĥces ŷheŋe studeĥts aŋe affoŋded aĥ oppoŋtuĥitŽ to applŽ skills aĥd techĥiŊues acŊuiŋed fŋoĤ assessĤeĥt aĥd iĥteŋŶeĥtioĥ-oŋieĥted couŋse Ĥateŋial. NuĤbeŋ of houŋs Ŷaŋies bŽ acadeĤic pŋogŋaĤ based oĥ cliĥical placeĤeĥt site houŋ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts aĥd studeĥt assigĥĤeĥts ǜsee aboŶeǝ.

Aĥ eŊuiŶaleĥt aĤouĥt of ŷoŋk is ŋeŊuiŋed iĥ couŋses aĥd acadeĤic actiŶities ŷheŋe diŋect iĥstŋuctioĥ is ĥot the pŋiĤaŋŽ Ĥode of leaŋĥiĥg, such as iĥdepeĥdeĥt studŽ, aĥd diŋected studŽ, oĥliĥe, aĥd hŽbŋid couŋses. Cŋedits ŷill be aŷaŋded oĥ the basis of docuĤeĥted leaŋĥiĥg objectiŶes, eżpected leaŋĥiĥg outcoĤes, aĥd studeĥt ŷoŋkload eżpectatioĥs ŷithiĥ a speciƊed peŋiod of acadeĤicallŽ eĥgaged tiĤe.

- Iĥdepeĥdeĥt StudŽ: Couŋses that peŋĤit a studeĥt to studŽ a subject oŋ topic iĥ coĥsideŋable depth beŽoĥd the scope of a ŋegulaŋ couŋse. Studeĥts Ĥeet peŋiodicallŽ, as agŋeed upoĥ ŷith the facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋ, foŋ the duŋatioĥ of the couŋse. UĥiŶeŋsitŽ facultŽ pŋoŶides guidaĥce, cŋitiŊue, aĥd ŋeŶieŷ of the studeĥtǭs ŷoŋk. Studeĥts deĤoĥstŋate coĤpeteĥcŽ thŋough the coĤpletioĥ of a Ɗĥal assessĤeĥt eitheŋ bŽ subĤittiĥg a Ɗĥal papeŋ, pŋoject oŋ poŋtfolio, etc. as ŋeŊuiŋed bŽ the facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋ. Cŋedit houŋs aŋe assigĥed based oĥ appŋożiĤatelŽ ƒƔ-ƓƔ houŋs of leaŋĥiĥg eĥgageĤeĥt peŋ cŋedit houŋ foŋ the aĤouĥt of actiŶitŽ associated ŷith the couŋse, facultŽ supeŋŶisioĥ, aĥd aĤouĥt of studeĥt outside ŷoŋk.
- Diŋected StudŽ: Couŋses that aŋe ŋegulaŋ couŋses, ĥot aŶailable iĥ the seĤesteŋ aĥd that the studeĥt has ĥot beeĥ able to schedule iĥ the ŋegulaŋ seŊueĥce. Scope, assigĥĤeĥts, aĥd ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ a diŋected studŽ couŋse aŋe the saĤe as foŋ the ŋegulaŋ couŋse ŷith the saĤe couŋse ĥuĤbeŋ, title, aĥd descŋiptioĥ. Studeĥts Ĥeet ŷith the iĥstŋuctoŋ as aŋŋaĥged, coĤpletiĥg appŋożiĤatelŽ ƒƔ-ƓƔ houŋs of leaŋĥiĥg eĥgageĤeĥt peŋ cŋedit houŋ ŷhich ĤaŽ iĥclude face-to-face iĥstŋuctioĥ, iĥdepeĥdeĥt ŷoŋk, oĥliĥe discussioĥ, aĥd ŷŋitteĥ assigĥĤeĥts oŋ tests.
- HŽbŋid: A couŋse is coĥsideŋed hŽbŋid ǜoŋ bleĥdedǝ ŷheĥ it is coĤposed of both oĥliĥe leaŋĥiĥg aĥd classŋooĤ leaŋĥiĥg aĥd iĥcoŋpoŋates the best featuŋes of both eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥts to Ĥeet the leaŋĥiĥg objectiŶes of the couŋse. No less thaĥ ƔƐ% of the couŋse is to be scheduled as face-to-face, aĥd ĥo Ĥoŋe thaĥ ƓƘ% of the couŋse is to be scheduled as oĥliĥe. Foŋ a thŋee-cŋedit couŋse, ĥo less thaĥ Ɩƕ.ƔƏ Ĥiĥutes ǜƐ.ƑƖƔ houŋsǝ a ŷeek caĥ be scheduled face-to-face aĥd ĥo Ĥoŋe thaĥ Ɩƒ.ƔƏ Ĥiĥutes ǜƐ.ƑƑƔ houŋsǝ peŋ a ŷeek caĥ be scheduled oĥliĥe eŊualiĥg a total of ƐƔƏ Ĥiĥutes of iĥstŋuctioĥ peŋ ŷeek.
- Oĥliĥe ǜAsŽĥchŋoĥousǝ: Couŋses ŷheŋe Ǫiĥstŋuctoŋs aĥd studeĥts do ĥot Ĥeet iĥ the saĤe spaceǫ. Regaŋdless of Ĥode of iĥstŋuctioĥ, couŋses should be coĥsisteĥt iĥ teŋĤs of ŊualitŽ, assessĤeĥt, leaŋĥiĥg outcoĤes, ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts, etc. as couŋses offeŋed face-to-face ŷith the saĤe depaŋtĤeĥt pŋeƊż, ĥuĤbeŋ, aĥd couŋse title. FacultŽ Ĥust deĤoĥstŋate actiŶe acadeĤic eĥgageĤeĥt thŋough iĥteŋactiŶe Ĥethods, iĥcludiĥg but ĥot liĤited to, iĥteŋactiŶe tutoŋials, gŋoup discussioĥs, Ŷiŋtual studŽ/pŋoject gŋoups, discussioĥ boaŋds, chat ŋooĤs, etc. SiĤplŽ loggiĥg oĥ, eitheŋ bŽ facultŽ oŋ studeĥts, does ĥot coĥstitute actiŶe studeĥt leaŋĥiĥg. Cŋedit houŋs assigĥed to a couŋse deliŶeŋed oĥliĥe Ĥust eŊual the ĥuĤbeŋ of cŋedit houŋs foŋ the saĤe couŋse deliŶeŋed face-to-face.

ReŶised Eżpaĥded PolicŽǍ Maŋch ƐƗ, ƑƏƐƘ

## DEAN'S LIST

Full-tiĤe studeĥts ǜeĥŋolled iĥ ƐƑ oŋ Ĥoŋe graded houŋsǝ ŷho eaŋĥ a seĤesteŋ GPA of ƒ.Ɣ to ƒ.ƘƘ ŊualifŽ foŋ the Deaĥǭs List. Full-tiĤe studeĥts ŷho eaŋĥ a peŋfect Ɠ.Ə seĤesteŋ GPA ŊualifŽ foŋ the Deaĥǭs List ŷith the additioĥal hoĥoŋ of ǪSpecial Distiĥctioĥ.ǫ

## GRADING

## Gŋades, Houŋs, aĥd Cŋedit Poiĥts:

Aĥ Ǫhouŋǫ is couŋseŷoŋk eŊuiŶaleĥt to oĥe class houŋ peŋ ŷeek foŋ a seĤesteŋ. A Ǫcŋedit poiĥtǫ is a Ĥeasuŋe of the ŊualitŽ of ŷoŋk peŋfoŋĤed. Cŋedit poiĥts aŋe Ɗguŋed oĥlŽ oĥ ŷoŋk coĤpleted at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

Gŋade ŋepoŋts aŋe issued bŽ the Office of the Registrar iĥ the folloŷiĥg teŋĤsǍ

| A, A-     | AchieŶeĤeĥt of supeŋioŋ ŊualitŽ iĥ couŋse objectiŶes                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|-----------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| B+, B, B- | AchieŶeĤeĥt of eżcelleĥt ŊualitŽ iĥ couŋse objectiŶes                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| C+, C, C- | AchieŶeĤeĥt of aŶeŋage oŋ soĤeŷhat aboŶe aŶeŋage ŊualitŽ iĥ couŋse objectiŶes                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| D+, D     | BasicallŽ uĥsatisfactoŋŽ achieŶeĤeĥt but of sufƊcieĥt ŊualitŽ to Ĥeet ĤiĥiĤuĤ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts                                                                                                                                                                     |
| F         | CleaŋlŽ uĥsatisfactoŋŽ oŋ beloŷ ĤiĥiĤal achieŶeĤeĥt of couŋse objectiŶes                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| I         | IĥcoĤplete. Alloŷs coĤpletioĥ of delaŽed ŷoŋk bŽ ŷŋitteĥ agŋeeĤeĥt betŷeeĥ iĥstŋuctoŋ aĥd studeĥt. Must be oĥ Ɗle ŷith the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋegistŋaŋ befoŋe gŋades aŋe pŋocessedǎ becoĤes F at the eĥd of the Ɗfth ŷeek of the folloŷiĥg seĤesteŋ if ĥot coĤpleted. |
| IP        | Iĥ pŋogŋess                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| NR        | FacultŽ did ĥot ŋecoŋd a gŋade.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| W         | Withdŋeŷ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| WF        | Withdŋaŷĥ failiĥg                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| AW        | AdĤiĥistŋatiŶe Withdŋaŷal                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| S         | Woŋk coĤpleted at C- leŶel oŋ aboŶe                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| U         | Woŋk coĤpleted at D+ leŶel oŋ beloŷ                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| CR        | Woŋk coĤpleted at a satisfactoŋŽ leŶel                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| NC        | Woŋk coĤpleted at aĥ uĥsatisfactoŋŽ leŶel                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |

Studeĥts ĤaŽ ŷithdŋaŷ fŋoĤ couŋses duŋiĥg the Ɗŋst ƊŶe ŷeeks ŷithout haŶiĥg a ĥotatioĥ oĥ theiŋ tŋaĥscŋiptsǎ theŽ ĤaŽ ŷithdŋaŷ ŷith a ŋecoŋded W afteŋ the Ɗfth ŷeek but ĥo lateŋ thaĥ the eĥd of the ƐƏth ŷeek. Studeĥts ĤaŽ chaĥge theiŋ ŋegistŋatioĥ to oŋ fŋoĤ S/U duŋiĥg the Ɗŋst ƊŶe ŷeeks of the seĤesteŋ. No ŷithdŋaŷals oŋ chaĥges iĥ ŋegistŋatioĥ aŋe peŋĤitted afteŋ the ƐƏth ŷeek.

| Credit poiĥts per hourǍ   | A   | =   | Ɠ.Ə   |
|---------------------------|-----|-----|-------|
|                           | A-  | =   | ƒ.ƕƖ  |
|                           | B+  | =   | ƒ.ƒƒ  |
|                           | B   | =   | ƒ.Ə   |
|                           | B-  | =   | Ƒ.ƕƖ  |
|                           | C+  | =   | Ƒ.ƒƒ  |
|                           | C   | =   | Ƒ.Ə   |
|                           | C-  | =   | Ɛ.ƕƖ  |
|                           | D+  | =   | Ɛ.ƒƒ  |
|                           | D   | =   | Ɛ.Ə   |

No cŋedit poiĥts aŋe giŶeĥ foŋ couŋses beaŋiĥg gŋades of CR, NC, S, U, F, I, W, WF, oŋ AW. The cŋedit poiĥt iĥdeż is the ŋatio of the ĥuĤbeŋ of cŋedit poiĥts eaŋĥed to the ĥuĤbeŋ of houŋs atteĤpted ǜeżcludiĥg CR, NC, S, U, aĥd Wǝ. No cŋedit poiĥts aŋe issued foŋ tŋaĥsfeŋ couŋses.

Mid-seĤesteŋ gŋades aŋe aŶailable to all studeĥts oĥliĥe. Fiĥal seĤesteŋ gŋades aŋe based oĥ the ŷoŋk of the eĥtiŋe seĤesteŋ, ŷhich iĥcludes eżaĤiĥatioĥs aĥd eŶaluatioĥs thŋoughout the couŋse.

## Gŋade Poiĥt AŶeŋage:

Gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage ǜGPAǝ is coĤputed bŽ diŶidiĥg the total ĥuĤbeŋ of cŋedit poiĥts accuĤulated iĥ couŋses foŋ ŷhich a gŋade of A, A-, B+, B, B-, C+, C, C-, D+, D, F, oŋ WF ŷas assigĥed bŽ the total ĥuĤbeŋ of houŋs atteĤpted iĥ those couŋses. Couŋses foŋ ŷhich a gŋade of IP, S, U, CR, NC, W, AW, oŋ NR ŷas assigĥed aŋe ĥot iĥcluded iĥ coĤputiĥg the GPA.

Wheĥ the couŋse is ŋepeated, oĥlŽ the houŋs aĥd cŋedit poiĥts foŋ the latest gŋade assigĥed foŋ that couŋse aŋe couĥted iĥ the total houŋs atteĤpted aĥd total cŋedit poiĥts. The folloŷiĥg eżaĤple shoŷs hoŷ seĤesteŋ GPA aĥd cuĤulatiŶe GPA aŋe calculatedǍ

| Couŋse         | Houŋs AtteĤpted   | Gŋade   | Cŋedit Poiĥts   |
|----------------|-------------------|---------|-----------------|
| ENGL ƐƐƐƏ      | ƒ                 | C       | ƕ.Ə             |
| SOCI ƑƏƐƏ      | ƒ                 | B       | Ƙ.Ə             |
| BIOL ƑƑƐƏ      | Ɠ                 | A-      | ƐƓ.ƕƗ           |
| PSYC ƑƏƏƏ      | ƒ                 | D       | ƒ.Ə             |
| HIST ƑƏƒƏ      | ƒ                 | F       | Ə.Ə             |
| SeĤesteŋ Total | Ɛƕ                |         | ƒƑ.ƕƗ           |

| PŋeŶious SeĤesteŋs      | ƑƖ    |                           | ƖƓ.Ə   |
|-------------------------|-------|---------------------------|--------|
| CuĤulatiŶe Total        | Ɠƒ    |                           | ƐƏƕ.ƕƗ |
| SeĤesteŋ Cŋedit PoiĥtsǍ | ƒƑ.ƕƗ | CuĤulatiŶe Cŋedit PoiĥtsǍ | ƐƏƕ.ƕƗ |
| ÷ Houŋs AtteĤptedǍ      | Ɛƕ    | ÷ Houŋs AtteĤptedǍ        | Ɠƒ     |
| = SeĤesteŋ GPAǍ         | Ƒ.ƏƓ  | = CuĤulatiŶe GPAǍ         | Ƒ.ƓƗ   |

The GPA is tŋuĥcated ǜĥot ŋouĥdedǝ. Foŋ eżaĤple, a Ƒ.ƘƘƘ GPA is still a Ƒ.ƘƘ, NOT a ƒ.Ə.

## Gŋade Appeal:

At tiĤes, studeĥts Ĥight belieŶe theŋe is adeŊuate ŋeasoĥ foŋ gŋade ŋecoĥsideŋatioĥ. Studeĥts ŷith such gŋieŶaĥces haŶe the ŋight to Ĥake aĥ appeal aĥd ŋeceiŶe a faiŋ heaŋiĥg. The folloŷiĥg aŋe the oĥlŽ gŋouĥds foŋ ŷhich a couŋse gŋade ĤaŽ be appealedǍ

- Aĥ obŶious eŋŋoŋ iĥ the calculatioĥ of the gŋade
- The assigĥĤeĥt of a couŋse gŋade to a paŋticulaŋ studeĥt bŽ applicatioĥ of Ĥoŋe eżactiĥg oŋ deĤaĥdiĥg staĥdaŋds thaĥ ŷeŋe applied to otheŋ studeĥts iĥ the couŋse
- The assigĥĤeĥt of a couŋse gŋade to a paŋticulaŋ studeĥt oĥ soĤe basis otheŋ thaĥ peŋfoŋĤaĥce iĥ the couŋse
- The assigĥĤeĥt of a couŋse gŋade bŽ a substaĥtial depaŋtuŋe fŋoĤ the iĥstŋuctoŋǭs pŋeŶiouslŽ aĥĥouĥced staĥdaŋds.

The folloŷiĥg pŋoceduŋe outliĥes the steps iĥ the gŋade-appeal pŋocessǍ

- STEP Ɛ Ǎ  Studeĥts aŋe eżpected to atteĤpt to ŋesolŶe the issue thŋough coĥsultatioĥ ŷith the iĥstŋuctoŋ. The gŋade appeal pŋocess Ĥust be iĥitiated bŽ the studeĥt bŽ eĤail as sooĥ as possible, but ĥo lateŋ thaĥ ƐƔ caleĥdaŋ daŽs afteŋ gŋades haŶe beeĥ posted bŽ the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ. Eżteĥuatiĥg ciŋcuĤstaĥces aŋe possible iĥ ŷhich it ŷould ĥot be feasible oŋ adŶisable to ŋegisteŋ aĥ appeal ŷith the iĥstŋuctoŋ. Iĥ such uĥusual ciŋcuĤstaĥces, studeĥts ĤaŽ pŋeseĥt theiŋ appeal diŋectlŽ to the chaiŋ of the depaŋtĤeĥt iĥ ŷhich the couŋse ŷas offeŋed.
- STEP Ƒ Ǎ  Studeĥts ŷho aŋe uĥable to ŋeach a satisfactoŋŽ agŋeeĤeĥt ŷith the iĥstŋuctoŋ oŋ ŷho, foŋ ŋeasoĥs stated pŋeŶiouslŽ, haŶe ĥot coĥfeŋŋed ŷith the iĥstŋuctoŋ, ĤaŽ Ɗle a ŷŋitteĥ petitioĥ bŽ coĥtactiĥg the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ. The UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ ŷill diŋect the ŷŋitteĥ petitioĥ to the appŋopŋiate depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ oŋ pŋogŋaĤ diŋectoŋ, ŋeŊuestiĥg the chaiŋ oŋ diŋectoŋ ŋeŶieŷ the appeal. If the depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ is the iĥstŋuctoŋ ŷho issued the gŋade beiĥg appealed, theĥ the ŷŋitteĥ petitioĥ ŷill be seĥt bŽ the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ to the appŋopŋiate college deaĥ.  Such a petitioĥ is to be Ɗled ŷithiĥ ƊŶe caleĥdaŋ daŽs afteŋ the discussioĥ ŷith the iĥstŋuctoŋ, oŋ if the coĥtact has beeĥ bŽ eĤail, ŷithiĥ ƊŶe caleĥdaŋ daŽs folloŷiĥg the ŋeceipt of the iĥstŋuctoŋǭs ŋeplŽ. Iĥ Ɗliĥg appeals, studeĥts Ĥust state theiŋ appeal cleaŋlŽ, iĥdicate the dateǜsǝ oĥ ŷhich theŽ coĥsulted ŷith the iĥstŋuctoŋ, aĥd state bŋieƋŽ theiŋ iĥteŋpŋetatioĥ of the outcoĤe of the discussioĥ.
- STEP ƒ Ǎ  Upoĥ ŋeceiŶiĥg a petitioĥ foŋ a gŋade appeal, the depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ oŋ pŋogŋaĤ diŋectoŋ Ĥight seek additioĥal iĥfoŋĤatioĥ fŋoĤ the studeĥt ǜthŋough iĥteŋŶieŷ oŋ bŽ eĤailǝ iĥ aĥ atteĤpt to uĥdeŋstaĥd as fullŽ as possible, the ĥatuŋe of aĥd the justiƊcatioĥ foŋ the appeal. The depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ oŋ pŋogŋaĤ diŋectoŋ ŷill theĥ coĥfeŋ ŷith the facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋ aĥd, at his oŋ heŋ discŋetioĥ, ĤaŽ talk ŷith the iĥstŋuctoŋ aĥd studeĥt togetheŋ.
- STEP Ɠ Ǎ  If the depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ oŋ pŋogŋaĤ diŋectoŋ is uĥable to ŋesolŶe the issue to the studeĥtǭs satisfactioĥ, he oŋ she ŷill ask the chaiŋpeŋsoĥ of the AcadeĤic Policies &amp; Appeals CoĤĤittee to call a special Ĥeetiĥg of the coĤĤittee to ŋeŶieŷ all the iĥfoŋĤatioĥ aŶailable, to giŶe a heaŋiĥg to the studeĥt ǜthŋough iĥteŋŶieŷ oŋ bŽ eĤailǝ at the discŋetioĥ of the coĤĤittee, aĥd also to the iĥstŋuctoŋ. The coĤĤittee ĤaŽ coĥsult ŷith otheŋ studeĥts ŷho ŷeŋe iĥ the saĤe couŋse aĥd also ŷith otheŋ facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋǜsǝ iĥ the iĥstŋuctoŋǭs depaŋtĤeĥt.
- STEP Ɣ Ǎ  Wheĥ the AcadeĤic Policies &amp; Appeals CoĤĤittee has Ĥade a thoŋough ŋeŶieŷ of the case aĥd has ŋeached a decisioĥ about the appeal pŋeseĥted, it shall Ĥake its decisioĥ aĥd ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥs kĥoŷĥ, iĥ ŷŋitiĥg, to the studeĥt, to the iĥstŋuctoŋ of the couŋse, to the college deaĥ, aĥd to the depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ oŋ pŋogŋaĤ diŋectoŋ.

The coĤĤittee ĤaŽ Ĥake appŋopŋiate ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥs ŋegaŋdiĥg pŋoceduŋes to the iĥstŋuctoŋ. If a seĤesteŋ gŋade is iĥ Ŋuestioĥ, the coĤĤittee ĤaŽ ŋecoĤĤeĥd to the iĥstŋuctoŋ that a chaĥge of gŋade be coĥsideŋed. Iĥ uĥusual ciŋcuĤstaĥces, the pŋoŶost aĥd college deaĥ ĤaŽ iĥitiate such a chaĥge if the iĥstŋuctoŋ ŷill ĥot do so aĥd theŋe appeaŋs to be coĤpelliĥg ŋeasoĥs foŋ such actioĥ. The decisioĥ of the coĤĤittee is Ɗĥal.

## Cŋedit/Noĥ-Cŋedit Gŋadiĥg:

SoĤe couŋses aŋe offeŋed oĥlŽ as cŋedit oŋ ĥoĥ-cŋedit. As such, theŽ appeaŋ iĥ the Ĥasteŋ schedule of classes ŷith a CR/NC ŋegistŋatioĥ. The houŋs takeĥ aŋe cŋedited toŷaŋd gŋaduatioĥ but ŷill ĥot be coĥsideŋed iĥ deteŋĤiĥiĥg the gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage ǜoŋ iĥcluded iĥ coĥsideŋiĥg eligibilitŽ foŋ the Deaĥǭs Listǝ.

## SatisfactoŋŽ/UĥsatisfactoŋŽ Gŋadiĥg:

Iĥ additioĥ to ŋegisteŋiĥg foŋ couŋses oĥ a ŋegulaŋ-gŋade basis, studeĥts also haŶe the optioĥ of ŋegisteŋiĥg oĥ a satisfactoŋŽ/uĥsatisfactoŋŽ ǜS/Uǝ basis.

The S/U optioĥ seeks to facilitate iĥtellectual eżploŋatioĥ iĥ seaŋch of a Ĥajoŋ, iĥ suppoŋt of a Ĥajoŋ, oŋ iĥ puŋsuit of a peŋsoĥal iĥteŋestǎ to offeŋ the ƋeżibilitŽ of a gŋadiĥg pŋocess ŷhich Ĥost appŋopŋiatelŽ ŋelates to the objectiŶes of a

paŋticulaŋ couŋseǎ aĥd to pŋoŶide aĥ oppoŋtuĥitŽ, ŷithout gŋade-poiĥt coĥsideŋatioĥ, foŋ studeĥts to assess theiŋ oŷĥ iĥteŋests aĥd abilities. This eĥcouŋages gŋeateŋ coĤĤuĥicatioĥ betŷeeĥ studeĥts aĥd facultŽ coĥceŋĥiĥg the Ĥeaĥiĥg of eŶaluatioĥ. Coĥditioĥs foŋ takiĥg classes satisfactoŋŽ/uĥsatisfactoŋŽ aŋe as folloŷsǍ

- Choosiĥg the S/U optioĥ is alŷaŽs at the studeĥtǭs discŋetioĥ.
- S/U optioĥs aŋe liĤited to ƐƑ houŋs foŋ the studeĥtǭs eĥtiŋe college caŋeeŋ aĥd a ĤażiĤuĤ of Ɠ houŋs takeĥ S/U iĥ aĥŽ oĥe seĤesteŋ.
- Libeŋal aŋts couŋses takeĥ to Ĥeet libeŋal aŋts ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts ĤaŽ ĥot be takeĥ S/U.
- Couŋses iĥ the acadeĤic Ĥajoŋ oŋ Ĥiĥoŋ oŋ teacheŋ ceŋtiƊcatioĥ pŋogŋaĤs ĤaŽ ĥot be takeĥ S/U oĥce the Ĥajoŋ oŋ Ĥiĥoŋ oŋ pŋogŋaĤ has beeĥ declaŋed.
- If a studeĥt subseŊueĥtlŽ elects to Ĥajoŋ iĥ a discipliĥe iĥ ŷhich a couŋse had beeĥ gŋaded satisfactoŋŽ, that couŋse, but ĥo otheŋ such couŋses ĤaŽ be couĥted toŷaŋd the Ĥajoŋ oŋ Ĥiĥoŋ.
- Aĥ S sigĥiƊes a gŋade of C- oŋ betteŋ aĥd U a gŋade loŷeŋ thaĥ C-.
- Couŋses takeĥ oĥ the S/U basis ŷill ĥot be coĥsideŋed iĥ deteŋĤiĥiĥg GPA.

Studeĥts should coĥsult theiŋ adŶisoŋs oŋ the chaiŋ of the depaŋtĤeĥt iĥ ŷhich theŽ Ĥajoŋ ŋegaŋdiĥg the desiŋabilitŽ of takiĥg couŋses S/U. The eĥd of the Ɗfth ŷeek is the last daŽ foŋ Ĥakiĥg a chaĥge iĥ ŋegistŋatioĥ to oŋ fŋoĤ S/U.

## GRADUATION PROCEDURES

A studeĥtǭs catalog eżpiŋes ƐƏ Žeaŋs afteŋ Ĥatŋiculatioĥ. If a catalog has eżpiŋed, the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of the gŋaduatioĥ catalog Ĥust be Ĥet. Iĥ Ĥatteŋs of couŋse staĥdaŋds, pŋeŋeŊuisites, eligibilitŽ to coĥtiĥue, aĥd otheŋ acadeĤic policies, studeĥts aŋe subject to the ŋegulatioĥs aĥd pŋoceduŋes of the cuŋŋeĥt acadeĤic Žeaŋ.

To gŋaduate, studeĥts Ĥust be iĥ good staĥdiĥg ŷith the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ aĥd Ĥust haŶe Ɗĥaĥcial aŋŋaĥgeĤeĥts satisfactoŋilŽ Ĥade ŷith the OfƊce of Fiĥaĥcial Aid &amp; Scholaŋships. All iĥcoĤplete gŋades Ĥust be ŋeĤoŶed, all iĥstitutioĥal eżaĤiĥatioĥ ŋesults Ĥust be ŋecoŋded, aĥd all tŋaĥsfeŋ cŋedits fŋoĤ otheŋ iĥstitutioĥs Ĥust be oĥ Ɗle iĥ the OfƊce of the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ. The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋeseŋŶes the ŋight to ŋeĤoŶe studeĥts fŋoĤ paŋticipatioĥ iĥ coĤĤeĥceĤeĥt based oĥ acadeĤic deƊcieĥcies aĥd/oŋ discipliĥaŋŽ actioĥs as deƊĥed bŽ the deaĥ of studeĥt life at aĥŽ tiĤe. Petitioĥs to gŋaduate iĥ abseĥtia Ĥust be Ɗled ŷith the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋegistŋaŋ at least thŋee ŷeeks pŋioŋ to coĤĤeĥceĤeĥt.

Aĥ Applicatioĥ foŋ Gŋaduatioĥ Ĥust be Ɗled ŷith the Office of the Registrar bŽ the folloŷiĥg deadliĥes to alloŷ sufƊcieĥt tiĤe foŋ pŋocessiĥgǍ

- DeceĤbeŋ aĥd MaŽ gŋaduatesǍ bŽ the last FŋidaŽ iĥ Apŋil
- August gŋaduatesǍ bŽ the Ɗŋst MoĥdaŽ iĥ Octobeŋ

## DIRECTED OR INDEPENDENT STUDY

Oĥ occasioĥ a studeĥt ĤaŽ ĥeed oŋ desiŋe to take a couŋse out of schedule ǜi.e. Diŋected StudŽǝ oŋ to do iĥdiŶidual ŷoŋk oĥ a pŋoject oŋ topic ǜi.e. Iĥdepeĥdeĥt StudŽǝ uĥdeŋ the supeŋŶisioĥ of a facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋ.

Diŋected StudŽ Ǎ Wheĥ a studeĥt is uĥable to take a ŋeŊuiŋed catalog couŋse as ŋegulaŋlŽ scheduled the studeĥt ĤaŽ petitioĥ to the facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋ to take the couŋse as a Diŋected StudŽ. The saĤe couŋse objectiŶes aŋe used ŷith the oĥlŽ diffeŋeĥce beiĥg that the studeĥt coĤpletes the couŋse iĥdepeĥdeĥtlŽ uĥdeŋ the diŋectioĥ of the facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋ.

Iĥdepeĥdeĥt StudŽ Ǎ Studeĥts iĥteŋested iĥ puŋsuiĥg acadeĤic cŋedit foŋ aĥ iĥdiŶiduallŽ coĥstŋucted couŋse uĥdeŋ the supeŋŶisioĥ of a facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋ ĤaŽ ŋeŊuest to deŶelop aĥ Iĥdepeĥdeĥt StudŽ sŽllabus. Aĥ Iĥdepeĥdeĥt StudŽ ŋeŊuiŋes a sŽllabus/leaŋĥiĥg coĥtŋact, ĤutuallŽ coĥstŋucted bŽ the studeĥt aĥd facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋ, aĥd Ĥust haŶe peŋĤissioĥ fŋoĤ the facultŽ ĤeĤbeŋ, depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ, acadeĤic adŶisoŋ, aĥd deaĥ. Studeĥts ĤaŽ schedule a ĤażiĤuĤ of Ɨ houŋs of iĥdepeĥdeĥt studŽ applicable to a Ĥajoŋ, Ɠ houŋs to a Ĥiĥoŋ, aĥd ĥo Ĥoŋe thaĥ Ɠ houŋs iĥ a giŶeĥ seĤesteŋ.

## INSTITUTIONAL EXAM

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋecogĥizes the ĥeed foŋ studeĥt adŶaĥceĤeĥt accoŋdiĥg to abilitŽ aĥd achieŶeĤeĥt. Theŋefoŋe, studeĥts ŷho aŋe coĤpeteĥt iĥ a giŶeĥ subject bŽ ŋeasoĥ of theiŋ paŋticulaŋ backgŋouĥd oŋ eżpeŋieĥce outside the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ classŋooĤ ĤaŽ choose to ŋeceiŶe cŋedit bŽ iĥstitutioĥal eżaĤiĥatioĥ. EżaĤiĥatioĥs aŋe to be takeĥ pŋioŋ to eĥŋollĤeĥt iĥ the ĥeżt leŶel couŋse. Not all couŋses, hoŷeŶeŋ, aŋe appŋopŋiate foŋ cŋedit bŽ iĥstitutioĥal eżaĤiĥatioĥ.

Results fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ iĥstitutioĥal eżaĤiĥatioĥs aŋe coĥsideŋed foŋ puŋposes of adŶaĥced staĥdiĥg oŋ adŶaĥced placeĤeĥt.

Studeĥts Ĥust eaŋĥ a gŋade of C- oŋ aboŶe iĥ the Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ iĥstitutioĥal eżaĤiĥatioĥs to ŋeceiŶe cŋedit foŋ the couŋses. SatisfactoŋŽ-uĥsatisfactoŋŽ ǜS/Uǝ gŋadiĥg optioĥ is aŶailable as ŷell as ŋegulaŋ letteŋ gŋades. Gŋaduatiĥg seĥioŋs Ĥust haŶe eżaĤiĥatioĥ ŋesults oĥ Ɗle iĥ the Office of the Registrar bŽ Apŋil Ɛ of theiŋ gŋaduatioĥ Žeaŋ.

## INTERNSHIPS

So as to coĤplŽ ŷith fedeŋal aĥd state ŋegulatioĥs aĥd to addŋess coĥceŋĥs foŋ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ liabilitŽ, the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋeŊuiŋes studeĥts to ŋegisteŋ foŋ aĥ iĥteŋĥship pŋioŋ to the staŋt of the iĥteŋĥship aĥd ŷithiĥ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ deadliĥes. Gŋaĥtiĥg cŋedit foŋ iĥteŋĥships ŋeŊuiŋes eĥŋollĤeĥt iĥ the class duŋiĥg the seĤesteŋ/teŋĤ iĥ ŷhich paŋticipatioĥ iĥ the iĥteŋĥship occuŋs. If aĥ iĥteŋĥship eżteĥds to Ĥoŋe thaĥ oĥe seĤesteŋ oŋ teŋĤ, the studeĥtǭs ŋegistŋatioĥ Ĥust ŋeƋect the cŋedit houŋs eaŋĥed each seĤesteŋ oŋ teŋĤ. This policŽ satisƊes the ĥeed to liĤit uĥiŶeŋsitŽ liabilitŽ aĥd to coĤplŽ ŷith goŶeŋĥĤeĥtal ŋegulatioĥs coĥceŋĥiĥg Ɗĥaĥcial aid.

## LATIN HONORS

Studeĥts eaŋĥiĥg a cuĤulatiŶe GPA of ƒ.Ɩ oŋ aboŶe ŷill gŋaduate cuĤ laude ǎ ƒ.Ɨ aĥd aboŶe, Ĥagĥa cuĤ laude ǎ aĥd ƒ.Ƙ aĥd aboŶe, suĤĤa cuĤ laude . Such hoĥoŋs aŋe opeĥ oĥlŽ to studeĥts ŷho haŶe eaŋĥed the ŊualifŽiĥg GPA ŷith a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of ƕƏ houŋs at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

## PROGRAM AND POLICY CHANGES

The schedule of classes foŋ each acadeĤic Žeaŋ is published the pŋecediĥg FebŋuaŋŽ. Both the Ĥasteŋ class schedule aĥd this catalog aŋe ŋegaŋded as ofƊcial stateĤeĥts of aĥticipated couŋse offeŋiĥgs. The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋeseŋŶes the ŋight to chaĥge oŋ caĥcel aĥŽ couŋse foŋ ŷhich eĥŋollĤeĥt is less thaĥ siż studeĥts oŋ foŋ ŷhich satisfactoŋŽ aŋŋaĥgeĤeĥts caĥĥot be Ĥade.

Iĥ additioĥ to couŋses listed iĥ the catalog, depaŋtĤeĥts ĤaŽ offeŋ special seĤiĥaŋs oŋ otheŋ couŋses, as the ĥeed aŋises, uĥdeŋ the ĥuĤbeŋs ƐƕƏƏ, ƑƕƏƏ, ƒƕƏƏ, aĥd ƓƕƏƏ.

## RESIDENCY REQUIREMENT

To eaŋĥ a degŋee fŋoĤ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ, studeĥts Ĥust be iĥ ŋesideĥce at the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ foŋ the last ƑƓ houŋs applicable to the degŋee. Uĥdeŋ soĤe ciŋcuĤstaĥces, aĥd ŷith special peŋĤissioĥ, a ĤażiĤuĤ of siż houŋs of the Ɗĥal ƑƓ houŋs ĤaŽ be takeĥ elseŷheŋe. Coĥtact the Office of the Registrar foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ.

## TRANSCRIPTS

Studeĥts ŷaĥtiĥg tŋaĥscŋipts of theiŋ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷoŋk Ĥust subĤit a ŷŋitteĥ ŋeŊuest to the Office of the Registrar , giŶiĥg at least oĥe ŷeekǭs ĥotice. The appŋopŋiate fee is to be iĥcluded ŷith the ŋeŊuest. All Ɗĥaĥcial obligatioĥs to the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ Ĥust be aŋŋaĥged to the satisfactioĥ of the Busiĥess OfƊce befoŋe tŋaĥscŋipts ŷill be ŋeleased diŋectlŽ to aĥ iĥdiŶidual. Tŋaĥscŋipts ĤaŽ be seĥt diŋectlŽ to aĥ eĤploŽeŋ,  poteĥtial eĤploŽeŋ, oŋ aĥ educatioĥal iĥstitutioĥ ŷithout Ɗĥaĥcial obligatioĥs beiĥg Ĥet. Tŋaĥscŋipts ĤaŽ be oŋdeŋed oĥliĥe at getĤŽtraĥscript.org .

## TRANSFER OF CREDIT FROM OTHER INSTITUTIONS

The Office of the Registrar ŷill eŶaluate aĥd deteŋĤiĥe the applicabilitŽ of all college cŋedits beiĥg tŋaĥsfeŋŋed fŋoĤ otheŋ iĥstitutioĥs. Studeĥts ŷho tŋaĥsfeŋ a substaĥtial ĥuĤbeŋ of houŋs fŋoĤ otheŋ iĥstitutioĥs aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to coĤplete at least ƔƏ% of theiŋ Ĥajoŋs, Ĥiĥoŋs, oŋ pŋofessioĥal Ɗelds at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ. GeĥeŋallŽ, cŋedit is accepted ŷithout coĥditioĥ foŋ couŋses ŷith a gŋade of C- oŋ aboŶe fŋoĤ tŋaditioĥal iĥstitutioĥs holdiĥg eitheŋ a ŋegioĥal oŋ Couĥcil foŋ Higheŋ Educatioĥ Accŋeditatioĥ ǜCHEAǝ. Studeĥts should coĥsult ŷith the OfƊce of the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ coĥceŋĥiĥg policŽ oĥ acceptaĥce of cŋedit fŋoĤ ĥoĥ-tŋaditioĥal iĥstitutioĥs aĥd iĥstitutioĥs ĥot holdiĥg ŋegioĥal accŋeditatioĥ.

GPA is Ɗguŋed oĥlŽ oĥ ŷoŋk coĤpleted at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ. Gŋades foŋ couŋses fŋoĤ otheŋ iĥstitutioĥs do ĥot tŋaĥsfeŋ iĥ.

All iĥteŋĥatioĥal studeĥts seekiĥg to tŋaĥsfeŋ cŋedit to the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ fŋoĤ outside the Uĥited States aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to pŋoŶide aĥ ofƊcial foŋeigĥ cŋedit eŶaluatioĥ ǜFCEǝ iĥ Eĥglish, iĥcludiĥg the cuĤulatiŶe gŋade poiĥt aŶeŋage. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷill accept couŋse-bŽ-couŋse foŋeigĥ cŋedeĥtial eŶaluatioĥs ǜFCEǝ fŋoĤ aĥŽ Natioĥal Associatioĥ of Cŋedeĥtial EŶaluatioĥ SeŋŶices ǜNACESǝ ĤeĤbeŋ. The iĥteŋĥatioĥal iĥstitutioĥ Ĥust be ŋecogĥized bŽ the couĥtŋŽǭs MiĥistŋŽ of Higheŋ Educatioĥ oŋ eŊuiŶaleĥt goŶeŋĥĤeĥt ageĥcŽ.  NoteǍ All eżpeĥses associated ŷith foŋeigĥ tŋaĥscŋipt eŶaluatioĥs aŋe the studeĥtǭs ŋespoĥsibilitŽ.

Tŋaĥsfeŋ couŋses ĤaŽ be coĥsideŋed applicable to the libeŋal aŋts ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥt foŋ adŶaĥced ŷŋitiĥg oŋ speech coĤpeteĥcŽ ǜŷŋitiĥg/speakiĥg-iĥteĥsiŶeǝ if eitheŋ the tŋaĥscŋipt iĥdicates that the couŋseǜsǝ ŷeŋe couĥted toŷaŋd the otheŋ iĥstitutioĥǭs adŶaĥced ŷŋitiĥg oŋ speakiĥg-iĥteĥsiŶe ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts ŷhich Ĥeet oŋ eżceed Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts ǜsee ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts iĥ the Libeŋal Aŋts PŋogŋaĤ sectioĥ iĥ this catalogǝ, oŋ the studeĥt caĥ pŋoduce a sŽllabus that cleaŋlŽ shoŷs hoŷ the couŋseǜsǝ satisƊes Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. No Ĥoŋe thaĥ ƕƓ seĤesteŋ cŋedit houŋs eaŋĥed fŋoĤ aĥ Associate Degŋee ĤaŽ be applied to aĥŽ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ baccalauŋeate degŋee. The tŋaĥsfeŋ cŋedit pŋocess caĥ oĥlŽ be iĥitiated foŋ studeĥts ŷho haŶe applied to AU.

Associate of Arts aĥd Associate of Scieĥce Degree Traĥsfer PolicŽǍ

AĥŽ studeĥt tŋaĥsfeŋŋiĥg to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ fŋoĤ a ŋegioĥallŽ-accŋedited oŋ CHEA-ŋecogĥized college/ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷith aĥ Associate of Aŋts oŋ Associate of Scieĥce degŋee aĥd has coĤpleted at least ƑƓ cŋedits iĥ the Libeŋal Aŋts ŷill haŶe satisƊed the Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Libeŋal Aŋts Coŋe ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts ŷith the ĥoted eżceptioĥs of the ŋeligioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts ǜBiblical LiteŋacŽ aĥd Chŋistiaĥ WaŽs of Kĥoŷiĥgǝ aĥd the libeŋal aŋts ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts that aŋe eĤbedded iĥ the Ĥajoŋs ǜWŋitiĥg-IĥteĥsiŶe, Speakiĥg-IĥteĥsiŶe, aĥd Eżpeŋieĥtial ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥtsǝ. Associate degŋee tŋaĥsfeŋ studeĥts Ĥust coĤplete at least ƕƏ houŋs at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ aĥd ŋeach ƐƑƏ cŋedits to gŋaduate. This policŽ oĥlŽ applies to studeĥts ŷho hold aĥ Associate Degŋee pŋioŋ to Ĥatŋiculatiĥg to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ. Foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ, coĥtact the Office of the Registrar .

## Traĥsfer of Credit - Curreĥt StudeĥtsǍ

Studeĥts cuŋŋeĥtlŽ eĥŋolled at AU should obtaiĥ peŋĤissioĥ fŋoĤ the UĥiŶersitŽ Registrar to take couŋses elseŷheŋe if theŽ iĥteĥd to tŋaĥsfeŋ that couŋseŷoŋk to AU. Couŋses ĥeed to be takeĥ at a ŋegioĥallŽ accŋedited college oŋ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

A sŽllabus oŋ catalog descŋiptioĥ fŋoĤ the otheŋ iĥstitutioĥ is ŋeŊuiŋed to deteŋĤiĥe the applicabilitŽ of the iĥteĥded couŋseŷoŋk toŷaŋd the libeŋal aŋts oŋ pŋogŋaĤ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. Studeĥts ŷho haŶe a declaŋed Ĥajoŋ ĥeed depaŋtĤeĥtal appŋoŶal as ŷell as appŋoŶal fŋoĤ the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ foŋ a couŋse to applŽ to the Ĥajoŋ oŋ Ĥiĥoŋ.

A Ɗĥal gŋade of C- oŋ aboŶe Ĥust be eaŋĥed iĥ oŋdeŋ foŋ tŋaĥsfeŋ cŋedit to be ŋeceiŶed. Gŋades foŋ couŋses takeĥ at otheŋ iĥstitutioĥs ŷill ĥot appeaŋ oĥ Žouŋ AU tŋaĥscŋipt, but cŋedit houŋs ĤaŽ couĥt toŷaŋd gŋaduatioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. The Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Couŋse Repetitioĥ PolicŽ ŋeŊuiŋes that the saĤe couŋse Ĥust be takeĥ at AU to adjust the GPA.

## WITHDRAWAL FROM COURSES

## Studeĥt-Iĥitiated WithdraŷalǍ

OfƊcial ŷithdŋaŷal fŋoĤ all couŋses Ĥust be coĤpleted bŽ subĤissioĥ of the appŋopŋiate foŋĤ. The ofƊcial ŷithdŋaŷal date ŷill be the date that the foŋĤ is subĤitted. Iĥ eżteĥuatiĥg ciŋcuĤstaĥces, a studeĥt ĤaŽ iĥitiate coĤplete ŷithdŋaŷal fŋoĤ all couŋses bŽ phoĥe oŋ bŽ letteŋ to the Office of the Registrar . Questioĥs about the policŽ foŋ coĤplete ŷithdŋaŷal should be diŋected to the Office of the Registrar .

Studeĥts desiŋiĥg to dŋop aĥ iĥdiŶidual couŋse ĤaŽ do so bŽ Ɗlliĥg out the appŋopŋiate EtŋieŶe foŋĤ. Deadliĥes aĥd dŋop fees should be ĥoted. Questioĥs ŋegaŋdiĥg dŋoppiĥg a couŋse should be diŋected to the studeĥtǭs acadeĤic adŶisoŋ oŋ ĤaŽ be diŋected to the ŋegistŋaŋǭs ofƊce.

## UĥiŶersitŽ-Iĥitiated WithdraŷalǍ

The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ has the authoŋitŽ to ŷithdŋaŷ a studeĥt fŋoĤ the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ aĥd to ŋeŶoke the studeĥtǭs ŋegistŋatioĥ at aĥŽ tiĤe duŋiĥg the acadeĤic Žeaŋ. Theŋe aŋe tŷo tŽpes of uĥiŶeŋsitŽ-iĥitiated ŷithdŋaŷalsǍ

- WF ǜŷithdŋaŷĥ failiĥgǝ Ǎ  A gŋade of WF is assigĥed bŽ the facultŽ at aĥŽ tiĤe befoŋe the teĥth ŷeek of the seĤesteŋ oŋ bŽ the deaĥ of studeĥt life ŷheĥeŶeŋ it is deeĤed appŋopŋiate. The WF gŋade is assigĥed eitheŋ ŷheĥ a studeĥt has stopped atteĥdiĥg classes ŷithout ofƊciallŽ ŷithdŋaŷiĥg oŋ ŷheĥ a studeĥt is ŷithdŋaŷĥ foŋ discipliĥaŋŽ ŋeasoĥs. Foŋ puŋposes of GPA calculatioĥ, a WF is eŊuiŶaleĥt to aĥ F.
- AW ǜadĤiĥistŋatiŶe ŷithdŋaŷalǝ Ǎ A gŋade of AW is assigĥed bŽ the adĤiĥistŋatioĥ oŋ bŽ the deaĥ of studeĥt life ŷheĥ ciŋcuĤstaĥces do ĥot ŷaŋŋaĥt a failiĥg gŋade oŋ ŷheĥeŶeŋ it is deeĤed appŋopŋiate. The AW gŋade is ĥot coĤputed iĥ the studeĥtǭs GPA aĥd theŋefoŋe iĥŶolŶes ĥo acadeĤic peĥaltŽ. The ŋecoŋdiĥg of this gŋade Ĥust be authoŋized bŽ the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ.

## MAJORS AND MINORS

Majoŋs pŋoŶide the oppoŋtuĥitŽ to take a gŋoupiĥg of couŋses, usuallŽ coĥceĥtŋated iĥ oĥe depaŋtĤeĥt, foŋ puŋposes of specializatioĥ oŋ pŋofessioĥal ceŋtiƊcatioĥ. Iĥ additioĥ to the Ĥajoŋ, a Ĥiĥoŋ oŋ cogĥate of ƐƔ-ƐƗ houŋs ĤaŽ be selected but is ĥot ŋeŊuiŋed.

Studeĥts aŋe ŋespoĥsible foŋ plaĥĥiĥg aĥd coĤpletiĥg the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of theiŋ Ĥajoŋs, Ĥiĥoŋs, aĥd cogĥates. A GPA of at least Ƒ.Ə is ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ all couŋses applied to the Ĥajoŋ oŋ aŋea of coĥceĥtŋatioĥ.

Studeĥts coĤpletiĥg tŷo oŋ Ĥoŋe Ĥajoŋs ǜiĥcludiĥg coĤpleĤeĥtaŋŽ Ĥajoŋsǝ Ĥust eaŋĥ a ĤiĥiĤuĤ of ƐƔ houŋs that aŋe uĥiŊue to each Ĥajoŋ. To be aŷaŋded a Ĥajoŋ, studeĥts Ĥust coĤplete at least ƔƏ% of all couŋseŷoŋk iĥ ŋesideĥce at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

## DECLARATION OF MAJOR AND MINOR

Studeĥts should Ɗle a declaŋatioĥ of Ĥajoŋ aĥd Ĥiĥoŋ oŋ cogĥate utiliziĥg the appŋopŋiate EtŋieŶe foŋĤ. Foŋ plaĥĥiĥg the pŋopeŋ seŊueĥce of couŋses, studeĥts should declaŋe a Ĥajoŋ as sooĥ as possible.

This applicatioĥ aĥd the pŋoceduŋes iĥŶolŶed iĥ its appŋoŶal affoŋd studeĥts aĥ oppoŋtuĥitŽ foŋ eŶaluatioĥ of theiŋ objectiŶes iĥ college aĥd life. Studeĥts foŋĤallŽ state theiŋ pŋoposed Ĥajoŋs, Ĥiĥoŋs, aĥd/oŋ pŋofessioĥal oŋ pŋepŋofessioĥal pŋogŋaĤs aĥd coĥfeŋ ŷith the Ĥajoŋ adŶisoŋ of the depaŋtĤeĥt oŋ pŋogŋaĤ ŋegaŋdiĥg ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. This pŋoceduŋe coĥstitutes studeĥtsǭ ofƊcial declaŋatioĥs of Ĥajoŋs oŋ Ĥiĥoŋs.

To chaĥge Ĥajoŋs oŋ Ĥiĥoŋs, studeĥts Ĥust Ɗle the appŋopŋiate EtŋieŶe foŋĤ at the eaŋliest possible date.

## ADMISSION TO A PARTICULAR MAJOR

AdĤissioĥ to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ does ĥot autoĤaticallŽ iĥclude adĤissioĥ to specialized pŋogŋaĤs ŷithiĥ the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ, such as busiĥess, Ĥusic, ĥuŋsiĥg, social ŷoŋk, aĥd teacheŋ educatioĥ. The cŋiteŋia foŋ adĤissioĥ aĥd acceptaĥce to specialized pŋogŋaĤs aŋe deteŋĤiĥed bŽ the facultŽ of those pŋogŋaĤs. IĥfoŋĤatioĥ ŋegaŋdiĥg applicatioĥ deadliĥes aĥd adĤissioĥ cŋiteŋia ĤaŽ be obtaiĥed fŋoĤ the depaŋtĤeĥts offeŋiĥg the pŋogŋaĤs to ŷhich studeĥts ŷish to applŽ.

## TEACHING MAJORS

A coĤpleĤeĥtaŋŽ Ĥajoŋ is a gŋoup of ŋelated couŋses ǜƑƕ-ƔƓ houŋsǝ that Ĥust be takeĥ aloĥg ŷith oĥe of the Ĥajoŋs listed iĥ the pŋecediĥg Majors sectioĥ. ## PHYSICAL THERAPY

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ offeŋs a pŋogŋaĤ that pŋepaŋes studeĥts foŋ eĥtŋŽ iĥto phŽsical theŋapŽ pŋogŋaĤs. Most studeĥts seekiĥg to eĥteŋ the pŋofessioĥ obtaiĥ a bacheloŋǭs degŋee iĥ eżeŋcise scieĥce oŋ biologŽ. Because of the sĤall ĥuĤbeŋ of schools offeŋiĥg gŋaduate degŋees iĥ phŽsical theŋapŽ aĥd the laŋge ĥuĤbeŋ of studeĥts ŷho applŽ, adĤissioĥ to those pŋogŋaĤs is ŶeŋŽ coĤpetitiŶe. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ has deŶeloped aĥ aŋticulatioĥ agŋeeĤeĥt ŷith Southŷest Baptist UĥiŶeŋsitŽ iĥ BoliŶaŋ, Missouŋi, to facilitate adĤissioĥ foŋ AU gŋaduates to a doctoŋate degŋee pŋogŋaĤ iĥ phŽsical theŋapŽ. Iĥteŋested studeĥts should coĥtact the DepartĤeĥt of Natural Scieĥces foŋ Ĥoŋe details aĥd adŶisiĥg.

## PRE-HEALTH PROFESSIONAL PROGRAMS

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ offeŋs pŋe-health pŋofessioĥal pŋogŋaĤs foŋ studeĥts desiŋiĥg caŋeeŋs iĥ Ĥediciĥe, athletic tŋaiĥiĥg, phŽsical aĥd occupatioĥal theŋapŽ, deĥtistŋŽ, phŽsiciaĥ assistaĥt, phaŋĤacŽ, chiŋopŋactic, optoĤetŋŽ, podiatŋŽ, aĥd ŶeteŋiĥaŋŽ Ĥediciĥe. IĥdiŶidualized pŋogŋaĤs aŋe deŶeloped foŋ studeĥts ŷishiĥg to eĥteŋ otheŋ health pŋofessioĥs ĥot listed aboŶe.

Although Ĥost pŋe-health pŋofessioĥ studeĥts Ĥajoŋ iĥ biologŽ, biocheĤistŋŽ, oŋ eżeŋcise scieĥce, iĥ Ĥost cases aĥŽ Ĥajoŋ ĤaŽ be choseĥ as loĥg as the paŋticulaŋ health pŋofessioĥ pŋogŋaĤ aĥd couŋse ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts aŋe Ĥet. The leĥgth aĥd speciƊc couŋseŷoŋk foŋ each pŋogŋaĤ Ŷaŋies depeĥdiĥg oĥ the Ɗeld aĥd the iĥdiŶidual pŋofessioĥal school selected.

Each pŋe-health pŋofessioĥal pŋogŋaĤ is desigĥed to giŶe studeĥts a bŋoad, Chŋistiaĥ, libeŋal aŋts pŋepaŋatioĥ foŋ seŋŶice iĥ the health Ɗeld of choice. The pŋogŋaĤ usuallŽ coĥsists of the folloŷiĥg coĤpoĥeĥtsǍ

- A staĥdaŋd pŋe-health pŋofessioĥ coŋe of couŋses ǜoĥe Žeaŋ each of laboŋatoŋŽ-based, college-leŶel geĥeŋal biologŽ, geĥeŋal cheĤistŋŽ, aĥd phŽsicsǝ.
- Additioĥal couŋses iĥ the scieĥces to iĥcŋease studŽ skills aĥd kĥoŷledge base iĥ the ĤedicallŽ ŋelated subjects.
- A ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥt to iĥclude couŋses iĥ psŽchologŽ, sociologŽ, biblical studies, aĥd coĤĤuĥicatioĥ as paŋt of the libeŋal aŋts coĤpoĥeĥt.
- Pŋepaŋatioĥ foŋ the paŋticulaŋ health pŋofessioĥ staĥdaŋdized eżaĤ.
- Beiĥg aĥ actiŶe ĤeĤbeŋ iĥ the Pŋe-Pŋofessioĥal Health SocietŽ.
- A coĤĤittee eŶaluatioĥ aĥd ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥ pŋocess foŋ the pŋofessioĥal school applicatioĥ pŋoceduŋe.

Studeĥts iĥteŋested iĥ a paŋticulaŋ pŋe-health pŋofessioĥal pŋogŋaĤ should coĥtact the diŋectoŋ of pŋe-health pŋofessioĥal pŋogŋaĤs foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ aĥd/oŋ ŋefeŋŋal to the appŋopŋiate adŶisoŋ iĥ that pŋofessioĥ.

The success of Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs pŋe-health pŋofessioĥ pŋogŋaĤs caĥ be Ĥeasuŋed iĥ a ŶaŋietŽ of ŷaŽs. AU has aĥ eżcelleĥt placeĤeĥt ŋecoŋd duŋiĥg the past ƑƏ Žeaŋs. Of those studeĥts ŋeceiŶiĥg stŋoĥg coĤĤittee ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥs, ĥeaŋlŽ all haŶe beeĥ accepted.

## PRE-LAW

Studeĥts plaĥĥiĥg to atteĥd laŷ school aŋe ĥot ŋestŋicted to aĥŽ oĥe Ĥajoŋ. The top Ĥajoŋs foŋ studeĥts ŷho applŽ to laŷ school aŋe political scieĥce, Eĥglish, histoŋŽ, psŽchologŽ, aĥd busiĥess. Studeĥts aŋe eĥcouŋaged to ŷoŋk ŷith theiŋ Ĥajoŋ adŶisoŋ aĥd AUǭs pŋe-laŷ adŶisoŋ to select couŋses fŋoĤ acŋoss the cuŋŋiculuĤ that pŋepaŋe theĤ foŋ adĤissioĥ to laŷ school aĥd the pŋactice of laŷ.

Takiĥg classes acŋoss the cuŋŋiculuĤ helps studeĥts deŶelop the aĥalŽtical, ŷŋitiĥg, ŋeseaŋch, aĥd oŋal coĤĤuĥicatioĥ skills ĥecessaŋŽ to succeed iĥ laŷ school aĥd beŽoĥd. These classes also help studeĥts acŊuiŋe the kĥoŷledge of histoŋŽ, politics, societies, cultuŋes, ecoĥoĤies, aĥd philosophies that Ĥake success iĥ laŷ school Ĥoŋe likelŽ.

Iĥteŋested studeĥts should coĥsideŋ the Ĥiĥoŋ iĥ legal studies aĥd coĥsult ŷith AUǭs pŋe-laŷ adŶisoŋ as eaŋlŽ as possible.

## PRE-SEMINARY STUDIES

The uĥiŶeŋsitŽ seeks to seŋŶe studeĥts pŋepaŋiĥg foŋ seĤiĥaŋŽ adĤissioĥ thŋough a ŋaĥge of couŋses coĥsideŋed basic to such gŋaduate pŋofessioĥal studŽ. Theŋe is ĥo siĥgle ĥoŋĤatiŶe patteŋĥ foŋ pŋe-seĤiĥaŋŽ educatioĥ because of ŷidelŽ ŶaŋŽiĥg eĤphases aĥd settiĥgs foŋ ĤiĥistŋŽ. The Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ School of TheologŽ &amp; Chŋistiaĥ MiĥistŋŽ folloŷs cuŋŋeĥt adĤissioĥ ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥs of the Associatioĥ of Theological Schools ŷheĥ it suggests the folloŷiĥg categoŋies of leaŋĥiĥg as fouĥdatioĥal foŋ gŋaduate seĤiĥaŋŽ studŽǍ

## Pŋe-Pŋofessioĥal PŋogŋaĤs

- The abilitŽ to ŋead, ŷŋite, aĥd speak cleaŋ aĥd coŋŋect Eĥglish is Ŷital foŋ iĥteŋpŋetiĥg aĥd coĤĤuĥicatiĥg the faith of the chuŋch. It is highlŽ desiŋable that a ŋeadiĥg kĥoŷledge of Hebŋeŷ aĥd/oŋ Gŋeek be deŶeloped as a basic tool. Additioĥal laĥguage skills Ĥight be esseĥtial, depeĥdiĥg oĥ Ŷocatioĥal iĥteĥt.
- Geĥeŋal uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of huĤaĥ selfhood, Ĥodeŋĥ social iĥstitutioĥs, cultuŋe aĥd ŋeligioĥ, scieĥce aĥd techĥologŽ. Studeĥts aŋe eżpected to haŶe soĤe acadeĤic uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of the Ɗelds of philosophŽ, sociologŽ, psŽchologŽ, aĥd histoŋŽ, aĥd iĥ soĤe iĥstaĥces, ĤaŽ Ĥajoŋ iĥ oĥe of these aŋeas.
- Theological uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of Ĥajoŋ ŋeligious tŋaditioĥs aĥd the coĥteĤpoŋaŋŽ uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of Ŷalues aĥd faith. A kĥoŷledge of the ĥatuŋe aĥd coĥteĥt of biblical Ĥateŋials is of paŋticulaŋ sigĥiƊcaĥce.

Details of adĤissioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ the Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ School of TheologŽ &amp; Chŋistiaĥ MiĥistŋŽ should be coĥsideŋed iĥ the plaĥĥiĥg of uĥdeŋgŋaduate juĥioŋ aĥd seĥioŋ Žeaŋs.

## LEVEL

Loŷeŋ DiŶisioĥ ǜƐƏƏƏ/ƑƏƏƏ-LeŶelǝ Couŋses Ǎ Iĥ geĥeŋal, couŋses iĥ the ƐƏƏƏ oŋ ƑƏƏƏ seŋies couĥt toŷaŋd the libeŋal aŋts ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts aĥd aŋe to be takeĥ duŋiĥg the fŋeshĤaĥ oŋ sophoĤoŋe Žeaŋs. SoĤe couŋses iĥ the ƑƏƏƏ seŋies aŋe Ɗŋst-leŶel couŋses applicable to a giŶeĥ Ĥajoŋ oŋ specializatioĥ.

Uppeŋ-DiŶisioĥ ǜƒƏƏƏ/ƓƏƏƏ-LeŶelǝ Couŋses Ǎ Couŋses listed iĥ the ƒƏƏƏ aĥd ƓƏƏƏ seŋies aŋe coĥsideŋed uppeŋ-diŶisioĥ couŋses aĥd aŋe pŋiĤaŋilŽ iĥteĥded foŋ juĥioŋs aĥd seĥioŋs. HoŷeŶeŋ, fŋeshĤeĥ oŋ sophoĤoŋes iĥ good staĥdiĥg ĤaŽ be alloŷed to take uppeŋ-diŶisioĥ couŋses if theŽ haŶe Ĥet the pŋeŋeŊuisites aĥd haŶe the appŋoŶal of theiŋ adŶisoŋs.

## TITLE

Desigĥates the couŋse ĥuĤbeŋ aĥd title foŋ the couŋse ǜe.g., ƒƏƖƏ Geĥetics, listed uĥdeŋ the BIOL captioĥ headiĥgǝ.

## CREDIT HOURS

Iĥdicates the ĥuĤbeŋ of cŋedit houŋs that ĤaŽ be eaŋĥed bŽ takiĥg the couŋse. Withiĥ paŋeĥtheses, the ĥuĤbeŋ to the left iĥdicates the ĥuĤbeŋ of classŋooĤ houŋs associated ŷith the couŋse, aĥd the ĥuĤbeŋ to the ŋight iĥdicates the ĥuĤbeŋ of laboŋatoŋŽ oŋ studio houŋs. ## ADDITIONAL INFORMATION

The couŋse descŋiptioĥ , listed diŋectlŽ beĥeath the couŋse title, pŋoŶides details about theĤes, topics, aĥd issues coŶeŋed bŽ the couŋse, as ŷell as additioĥal iĥfoŋĤatioĥǍ

- EXPECTATION : Iĥdicates skills oŋ eżpeŋieĥces ŷhich studeĥts aŋe eżpected to haŶe achieŶed oŋ deĤoĥstŋated befoŋe takiĥg the couŋse. Also iĥdicates ŋestŋictioĥs ŋegaŋdiĥg ŷho ĤaŽ take the couŋse ǜi.e. depaŋtĤeĥtal eżaĤs, ĤiĥiĤuĤ gŋade iĥ a pŋeŋeŊuisite couŋse, etc.ǝ.
- CONSENT: Iĥdicates ŷhetheŋ studeĥts Ĥust obtaiĥ coĥseĥt to take the couŋse. If ĥo desigĥatioĥ is listed, ĥo special coĥseĥt is ŋeŊuiŋed.
- PREREQUISITE Ǎ Iĥdicates ŋeŊuiŋed class staĥdiĥg, ŋeŊuiŋed Ĥajoŋ, oŋ couŋseǜsǝ ŷhich Ĥust be coĤpleted befoŋe the couŋse ĤaŽ be takeĥ.
- COREQUISITE Ǎ Iĥdicates ŋeŊuiŋed class staĥdiĥg, ŋeŊuiŋed Ĥajoŋ, oŋ otheŋ couŋseǜsǝ ŷhich Ĥust be takeĥ iĥ the saĤe seĤesteŋ as the couŋse.
- REPEAT: Iĥdicates ŷheĥ a couŋse ĤaŽ be ŋepeated foŋ cŋedit. MaŽ also iĥclude liĤitatioĥs oĥ the ĥuĤbeŋ of tiĤes the couŋse ĤaŽ be ŋepeated oŋ ĤażiĤuĤ total cŋedits that ĤaŽ be couĥted.
- GRADE: Iĥdicates ŷheĥ CR/NC gŋadiĥg is iĥ effect. No listiĥg iĥdicates staĥdaŋd A-F gŋadiĥg.
- SAME AS: Iĥdicates ŷheĥ the couŋse shaŋes the saĤe descŋiptioĥ aĥd ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts as aĥotheŋ couŋse iĥ the catalog.

## Adult Leaŋĥiĥg

Adult educatioĥ at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ pŋoŶides Ĥeaĥiĥgful leaŋĥiĥg eżpeŋieĥces foŋ studeĥts age Ƒƒ aĥd oldeŋ bŽ offeŋiĥg ŊualitŽ pŋogŋaĤs desigĥed ŷith the adult leaŋĥeŋ iĥ Ĥiĥd. Adult studeĥts ĤaŽ select fŋoĤ daŽtiĤe, eŶeĥiĥg, oŋ oĥliĥe couŋses. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is coĤĤitted to offeŋiĥg accessible aĥd affoŋdable pŋogŋaĤs that aŋe ŋeleŶaĥt iĥ the cuŋŋeĥt ŷoŋkfoŋce aĥd ecoĥoĤŽ. Adult leaŋĥeŋs aŋe suppoŋted ŷith dedicated adŶisoŋs aĥd success coaches.

## DEGREE PROGRAMS

Adult studeĥts ĤaŽ puŋsue aĥŽ tŋaditioĥal degŋee pŋogŋaĤs offeŋed bŽ the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ.  Iĥ additioĥ, the folloŷiĥg oĥliĥe pŋogŋaĤs aŋe desigĥed speciƊcallŽ foŋ adult studiesǍ

- Associate of Arts degree iĥ CriĤiĥal Justice
- Associate of Scieĥce degree iĥ Geĥeral Studies
- Bachelor of Arts degree iĥ Busiĥess &amp; IĥtegratiŶe Leadership
- Bachelor of Arts degree iĥ CriĤiĥal Justice
- Bachelor of Arts degree iĥ MiĥistrŽ Studies

## ADULT STUDENT TUITION

Adult studeĥts paŽ a Ƌat ŋate peŋ seĤesteŋ houŋ foŋ tuitioĥ ǜŷith the eżceptioĥ of the Traĥsitioĥ to Teachiĥg ǜTƑTǝ pŋogŋaĤǝ. Additioĥal iĥfoŋĤatioĥ foŋ adult studeĥts caĥ be fouĥd oĥliĥe at aĥdersoĥ.edu/adĤissioĥs/adult .

Kiĥg, Pŋof. Kiseŋ, Pŋof. KĥifƊĥ, Pŋof. KuĤi, Pŋof. Laĥcasteŋ, Pŋof. Masek, Pŋof. MażƊeld, Pŋof. Poŷell, Pŋof. Receĥdez, Pŋof. Rice, Pŋof. Robbiĥs, Dŋ. Rodgeŋs, Pŋof. A. ShaŶeŋ, Pŋof. C. ShaŶeŋ, Pŋof. Shuĥtich, Pŋof. SilŶeus, Pŋof. SĤith, Pŋof. SĥŽdeŋ,  Pŋof. ThieĤet, Dŋ. Wallace, Dŋ. Wŋight, Pŋof. M. Yetteŋ, Dŋ. Yoŋk

The puŋpose of the School of Music &amp; PeŋfoŋĤiĥg Aŋts is to pŋoĤote the aŋtistic, iĥtellectual, aĥd peŋsoĥal gŋoŷth of studeĥts thŋough the peŋfoŋĤaĥce aĥd studŽ of Ĥusic, theatŋe, aĥd daĥce ŷithiĥ a coĤĤuĥitŽ of aŋtists aĥd scholaŋs.

The School of Music &amp; PeŋfoŋĤiĥg Aŋts offeŋs Bacheloŋ of Music degŋees iĥ Ĥusic educatioĥ, Ĥusical theatŋe, Ŷoice peŋfoŋĤaĥce, aĥd iĥstŋuĤeĥtal peŋfoŋĤaĥceǎ Bacheloŋ of Aŋts degŋees iĥ Ĥusic, Ĥusic busiĥess, Ĥusical theatŋe, theatŋe, aĥd ŷoŋship aŋtsǎ aĥd Ĥiĥoŋs iĥ daĥce, Ĥusic, Ĥusic peŋfoŋĤaĥce, aĥd theatŋe. The School of Music &amp; PeŋfoŋĤiĥg Aŋts also eĥdeaŶoŋs to giŶe all studeĥts oppoŋtuĥities foŋ cŋeatiŶe eżpeŋieĥces iĥ the peŋfoŋĤiĥg aŋts bŽ eĥcouŋagiĥg the deŶelopĤeĥt of aŋtistŋŽ aĥd scholaŋship thŋough classes, pŋiŶate Ĥusic studŽ, aĥd peŋfoŋĤaĥce.

Studeĥts iĥteĥdiĥg to becoĤe Ĥusic Ĥajoŋs, Ĥusical theatŋe Ĥajoŋs, oŋ theatŋe Ĥajoŋs should coĥsult the School of Music &amp; PeŋfoŋĤiĥg Aŋts ŷebsite foŋ auditioĥ foŋĤs aĥd ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. All pŋospectiŶe Ĥusic aĥd Ĥusical theatŋe Ĥajoŋs Ĥust coĤplete aĥ auditioĥ foŋ adĤissioĥ to the School of Music &amp; PeŋfoŋĤiĥg Aŋts. All fŋeshĤeĥ Ĥust coĤplete the fŋeshĤaĥ Ĥusic cuŋŋiculuĤ ŷith gŋades of C- oŋ betteŋ befoŋe ŋegisteŋiĥg foŋ uppeŋ-leŶel Ĥusic couŋses.

## FRESHMAN CURRICULUM FOR MUSIC

The fŋeshĤaĥ cuŋŋiculuĤ iĥ Ĥusic coĥsists of the folloŷiĥg couŋses ǜƐƑ hŋs.ǝǍ

- ƕ houŋs fŋoĤ MUSC ƐƏƐƏ, ƐƏƑƏ ǜtheoŋŽǝ
- Ƒ houŋs fŋoĤ MUSC ƐƏƒƏ, ƐƏƓƏ ǜauŋal coĤpŋeheĥsioĥǝ
- Ɠ houŋs fŋoĤ MUPF ƐƏƔƏ, ƐƏƕƏ ǜkeŽboaŋd classǝ

The fŋeshĤaĥ cuŋŋiculuĤ foŋ Ĥusic ĤaŽ be atteĤpted oĥlŽ tŷice. Withdŋaŷal fŋoĤ a fŋeshĤaĥ couŋse couĥts as oĥe atteĤpt to pass the couŋse. Tŋaĥsfeŋ studeĥts Ĥust take eżaĤiĥatioĥs to deteŋĤiĥe class placeĤeĥt iĥ fŋeshĤaĥ couŋses aĥd Ĥust pass the fŋeshĤaĥ cuŋŋiculuĤ ŷith gŋades of C- oŋ betteŋ bŽ the eĥd of theiŋ fouŋth seĤesteŋ of college studŽ, oŋ secoĥd seĤesteŋ at AU, iĥ oŋdeŋ to coĥtiĥue iĥ the Ĥajoŋ. Studeĥts ŷho ŷish to begiĥ a Ĥajoŋ iĥ Ĥusic afteŋ coĤpletiĥg theiŋ fouŋth seĤesteŋ of college studŽ Ĥust coĤplete the fŋeshĤaĥ cuŋŋiculuĤ ŷith gŋades of C- oŋ betteŋ oĥ the Ɗŋst atteĤpt. Studeĥts ŷho ŷish to ŋetake a couŋse iĥ the Ĥusic fŋeshĤaĥ cuŋŋiculuĤ afteŋ theiŋ fouŋth seĤesteŋ of college studŽ Ĥust petitioĥ the chaiŋ  of the School of Music &amp; PeŋfoŋĤiĥg Aŋts iĥ ŷŋitiĥg foŋ peŋĤissioĥ to do so.

## UPPER-DIVISION PERFORMANCE EVALUATION ǜUDPEǝ

Studeĥts iĥ Ĥusic oŋ Ĥusical theatŋe aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to pass the Uppeŋ-DiŶisioĥ PeŋfoŋĤaĥce EŶaluatioĥ ǜUDPEǝ to adŶaĥce to ƒƏƏƏ- aĥd ƓƏƏƏ-leŶel pŋiŶate Ĥusic studŽ, peŋfoŋĤ a juĥioŋ oŋ seĥioŋ ŋecital, coĥtiĥue a peŋfoŋĤaĥce eĤphasis, oŋ ŋegisteŋ foŋ Ĥusic educatioĥ Ĥethods couŋses oŋ studeĥt teachiĥg. Studeĥts usuallŽ take the UDPE at the eĥd of the sophoĤoŋe Žeaŋ.

## MUSIC ENSEMBLES

All Ĥusic Ĥajoŋs Ĥust paŋticipate iĥ appŋoŶed Ĥajoŋ eĥseĤbles each seĤesteŋ of eĥŋollĤeĥt ǜsee Music Haĥdbook foŋ a list of appŋoŶed Ĥajoŋ eĥseĤblesǝ. Music Ĥiĥoŋs aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to paŋticipate iĥ eĥseĤbles foŋ fouŋ seĤesteŋs. Studeĥts paŋticipate iĥ aĥ eĥseĤble foŋ Ɛ houŋ of cŋedit ǜoŋ zeŋo cŋedit if takiĥg ƐƗ houŋs of otheŋ couŋsesǝ.

## PRIVATE MUSIC STUDY

Music Ĥajoŋs eaŋĥ Ɛ-ƒ houŋs of cŋedit bŽ takiĥg ŷeeklŽ oĥe-houŋ pŋiŶate lessoĥs. ElectiŶe studeĥts eaŋĥ Ɛ houŋ of cŋedit bŽ takiĥg ŷeeklŽ half-houŋ oŋ oĥe-houŋ lessoĥs. Paŋticipatioĥ iĥ studio classes, studio ŋecitals, aĥd geĥeŋal studeĥt ŋecitals is paŋt of pŋiŶate studŽ at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ.

## MUSC

Music HistoŋŽ aĥd Liteŋatuŋe Couŋses

## ƑƐƐƏ Iĥtŋoductioĥ to Music Liteŋatuŋe

IĥtŋoductoŋŽ studŽ of Ĥusic liteŋatuŋe. Applies to the HuĤaĥistic &amp; Aŋtistic WaŽs of Kĥoŷiĥg [RaŶeĥ Coŋe] coĤpoĥeĥt of the Liberal Arts Core CurriculuĤ . ReŊuiŋed foŋ Ĥusic Ĥajoŋs. EXPECTATION Ǎ AbilitŽ to ŋead staĥdaŋd Ĥusic ĥotatioĥ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. II ǜeŶeĥ Žeaŋsǝ.

## ƑƑƏƏ Aŋt as Eżpeŋieĥce

Aĥ iĥteŋdiscipliĥaŋŽ iĥtŋoductioĥ to peŋfoŋĤiĥg aĥd Ŷisual aŋts thŋough Ɗŋst-haĥd eżpeŋieĥces atteĥdiĥg liŶe peŋfoŋĤaĥces aĥd, ŷheĥ possible, paŋticipatiĥg iĥ the actiŶitŽ aĥd talkiĥg ŷith the aŋtists. Iĥcludes studŽ of aesthetics, histoŋŽ, aĥd cŋaft. OFFERED Ǎ With sufƊcieĥt deĤaĥd.

## ƑƑƐƏ Music, the Aŋts, aĥd Cultuŋe

Aĥ eżaĤiĥatioĥ of Ĥajoŋ ŷoŋks of Westeŋĥ aŋt Ĥusic that eĤploŽ eleĤeĥts of aŋt, liteŋatuŋe, ƊlĤ, dŋaĤa, aĥd daĥce, ŷith eĤphasis oĥ opeŋa, oŋatoŋio, choŋal sŽĤphoĥŽ, pŋogŋaĤ sŽĤphoĥŽ, ballet, aĥd ƊlĤ Ĥusic geĥŋes. A studŽ of the pŋocesses bŽ ŷhich selected ŷoŋks ŷeŋe coĥceiŶed, coĤposed, pŋepaŋed, peŋfoŋĤed, ŋeceiŶed, aĥd uĥdeŋstood as eżpŋessioĥs of the huĤaĥ eżpeŋieĥce. Does ĥot couĥt toŷaŋd a Ĥusic Ĥajoŋ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I, II.

## ƑƑƑƏ Music iĥ SocietŽ

PŋoŶides a basis foŋ uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg aĥd appŋeciatiĥg aŋtistic Ĥusical eżpŋessioĥ. Does ĥot couĥt toŷaŋd a Ĥusic Ĥajoŋ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I, II.

## ƑƒƒƏ Iĥtŋoductioĥ to Woŋld Music

PŋoŶides a fŋaĤeŷoŋk foŋ eżpeŋieĥciĥg aĥd uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg Ĥusic fŋoĤ a ŶaŋietŽ of cultuŋes, Westeŋĥ aĥd ĥoĥ-Westeŋĥ. Focus oĥ belief sŽsteĤs, social oŋgaĥizatioĥ, cultuŋal coĥteżts, aĥd Ĥusical Ĥateŋials foŋ the puŋpose of ideĥtifŽiĥg siĤilaŋities aĥd diffeŋeĥces betŷeeĥ cultuŋes. Applies to the Global WaŽs of Kĥoŷiĥg [AU Eżpeŋieĥce] coĤpoĥeĥt of the Liberal Arts Core CurriculuĤ . EXPECTATION Ǎ AbilitŽ to ŋead staĥdaŋd Ĥusic ĥotatioĥ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I ǜodd Žeaŋsǝ.

## ƒƐƐƏ HistoŋŽ of Music: MedieŶal/Reĥaissaĥce

Geĥeŋal histoŋical suŋŶeŽ of Ĥusic fŋoĤ classical aĥtiŊuitŽ thŋough the Reĥaissaĥce. PREREQUISITE Ǎ MUSC ƑƐƐƏ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I.

## ƒƐƑƏ HistoŋŽ of Music: BaŋoŊue/Classic

Geĥeŋal histoŋical suŋŶeŽ of Ĥusic fŋoĤ ƐƕƔƏ to ƐƗƏƏ. Applies to the HuĤaĥistic &amp; Aŋtistic WaŽs of Kĥoŷiĥg [RaŶeĥ Coŋe] coĤpoĥeĥt of the Liberal Arts Core CurriculuĤ . PREREQUISITE Ǎ MUSC ƑƐƐƏ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I ǜodd Žeaŋsǝ.

## ƒƐƒƏ HistoŋŽ of Music: ƐƘth aĥd ƑƏth Ceĥtuŋies

## MUED ǜcoĥt.ǝ

## ƒƓƕƏ AdŶaĥced IĥstŋuĤeĥtal TechĥiŊues

Focuses oĥ peŋfoŋĤaĥce techĥiŊues aĥd pedagogŽ ŋelated to techĥicallŽ deĤaĥdiĥg iĥstŋuĤeĥts. Desigĥed to giŶe studeĥts aĥ iĥ-depth uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of highlŽ specialized iĥstŋuĤeĥts. EXPECTATION Ǎ Successful coĤpletioĥ of UDPE . PREREQUISITE Ǎ MUED ƐƑƏƏ, ƐƒƏƏ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I.

## ƒƓƖƏ AdŶaĥced Choŋal Coĥductiĥg

AdŶaĥced coĥductiĥg techĥiŊue, choŋal dictioĥ, choŋal toĥe, bodŽ aligĥĤeĥt, bŋeathiĥg techĥiŊue, iĥteŋpŋetatioĥ, ŋeheaŋsal techĥiŊue, aĥd stŽlistic eleĤeĥts. PREREQUISITE Ǎ MUSC ƑƏƑƏ, MUED ƑƓƖƏ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. II.

## ƒƓƗƏ AdŶaĥced IĥstŋuĤeĥtal Coĥductiĥg

Batoĥ techĥiŊue, scoŋe ŋeadiĥg, peŋfoŋĤaĥce, ŋeheaŋsal techĥiŊues, psŽchologŽ of coĥductiĥg. EXPECTATION Ǎ AbilitŽ to plaŽ aĥ oŋchestŋal iĥstŋuĤeĥt. PREREQUISITE Ǎ MUED ƑƓƖƏ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I.

## ƒƘƒƏ SeĤiĥaŋ iĥ GeŋĤaĥ Dictioĥ

SeĤiĥaŋ focuses oĥ special pŋobleĤs aĥd topics iĥ GeŋĤaĥ lŽŋic dictioĥ. Coĥducted iĥ a Ĥasteŋ-class foŋĤat, the seĤiĥaŋ iĥcludes both oŋal aĥd ŷŋitteĥ paŋticipatioĥ. PREREQUISITE Ǎ MUED ƑƔƐƏ, ƑƔƑƏ. OFFERED Ǎ With sufƊcieĥt deĤaĥd.

## ƒƘƓƏ SeĤiĥaŋ iĥ Fŋeĥch Dictioĥ

SeĤiĥaŋ focuses oĥ special pŋobleĤs aĥd topics iĥ Fŋeĥch lŽŋic dictioĥ. Coĥducted iĥ a Ĥasteŋ-class foŋĤat, the seĤiĥaŋ iĥcludes both oŋal aĥd ŷŋitteĥ paŋticipatioĥ. PREREQUISITE Ǎ MUED ƑƔƐƏ, ƑƔƑƏ. OFFERED Ǎ With sufƊcieĥt deĤaĥd.

## ƓƖƏƏ Methods of Teachiĥg Music iĥ the Public Schools

Taught iĥ coĥjuĥctioĥ ŷith the pŋofessioĥal seĤesteŋ. Mateŋials aĥd Ĥethods adapted to the speciƊc aŋeas aĥd leŶels iĥ ŷhich studeĥts aŋe iĥŶolŶed iĥ studeĥt teachiĥg. PREREQUISITE Ǎ MUED ƒƐƐƏ, ƒƐƑƏ, ƒƐƒƏ. OFFERED Ǎ Each seĤesteŋ.

## MUTR

## ƐƐƖƏ Iĥtŋo to Musical Theatŋe PeŋfoŋĤaĥce

This couŋse pŋepaŋes studeĥts foŋ the aŋtistic deĤaĥds of the Ĥusical stage bŽ deŶelopiĥg theiŋ siĥgiĥg, ĤusicalitŽ, peŋfoŋĤaĥce, aĥd pŋofessioĥal skills ŷith aĥ eĤphasis oĥ discipliĥaŋŽ staĥdaŋds aĥd iĥdustŋŽ eżpectatioĥs. Studeĥts eĥgage iĥ diŶeŋse peŋfoŋĤaĥce oppoŋtuĥities ŷhile focusiĥg oĥ self-discoŶeŋŽ, autheĥticitŽ, aĥd collaboŋatioĥ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I, II.

## ƒƔƒƏ Paŋtĥeŋiĥg foŋ Ballet aĥd Modeŋĥ Daĥce

## ƒƔƗƏ Daĥce IĤpŋoŶisatioĥ III

Studeĥts coĥtiĥue to deŶelop theiŋ seĥse of space, tiĤe, aĥd pŋopŋioceptioĥ ŷhile eżploŋiĥg the leŶels of phŽsical ŋelatioĥships, coĤĤuĥicatioĥ aĥd the phŽsical laŷs that goŶeŋĥ gŋaŶitŽ, ĤoĤeĥtuĤ aĥd iĥeŋtia to foŋĤ a coĥtiĥuous Ĥotioĥ coĥŶeŋsatioĥ. ## COMPUTER SCIENCE

The Ĥissioĥ of the DepartĤeĥt of CoĤputer Scieĥce is to pŋoŶide studeĥts ŷith a stŋoĥg fouĥdatioĥ iĥ the Ɗeld, build a loŶe foŋ lifeloĥg leaŋĥiĥg, aĥd igĥite a desiŋe to use theiŋ skills iĥ seŋŶice to the chuŋch aĥd to societŽ. The DepartĤeĥt of CoĤputer Scieĥce offeŋs thŋee staĥdaŋd Ĥajoŋs ǥ coĤputeŋ scieĥce ǜBacheloŋ of Scieĥce aĥd Bacheloŋ of Aŋtsǝ, data scieĥce ǜBacheloŋ of Scieĥce aĥd Bacheloŋ of Aŋtsǝ, aĥd cŽbeŋsecuŋitŽ ǜBacheloŋ of Aŋtsǝ, ŷhich is aĥ iĥteŋdiscipliĥaŋŽ Ĥajoŋ offeŋed iĥ coĥjuĥctioĥ ŷith the secuŋitŽ studies pŋogŋaĤ. Also, foŋ studeĥts ŷishiĥg to add a coĥceĥtŋatioĥ of couŋseŷoŋk iĥ these subjects to aĥ eżistiĥg Ĥajoŋ, tŷo coĤpleĤeĥtaŋŽ Ĥajoŋs aŋe offeŋedǥ coĤputeŋ scieĥce aĥd data scieĥce. The kĥoŷledge aĥd skills gaiĥed iĥ these Ĥajoŋs aŋe uĥiŊuelŽ suited to alloŷ ouŋ studeĥts to be seŋŶaĥt leadeŋs iĥ theiŋ coĤĤuĥities. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ coĤputeŋ scieĥce, cŽbeŋsecuŋitŽ, aĥd data scieĥce studeĥts aŋe iĤĤeŋsed iĥ pŋoject-based eżpeŋieĥtial leaŋĥiĥg iĥ both the classŋooĤ aĥd the coĤĤuĥitŽ.

Studeĥts deŶelop aĥd applŽ theiŋ kĥoŷledge outside the classŋooĤ bŽ coĤpletiĥg oĥ-caĤpus iĥteŋĥships ŷith aŋea coĤpaĥies oŋ the Ceĥter for SecuritŽ Studies aĥd CŽber Defeĥse , ŷoŋkiĥg ŷith Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ IĥforĤatioĥ TechĥologŽ SerŶices , aĥd ŷoŋkiĥg ŷithiĥ the DepartĤeĥt of CoĤputer Scieĥce to iĥstall aĥd Ĥaiĥtaiĥ seŋŶeŋs, ĥetŷoŋk, aĥd lab coĤputeŋs. Additioĥal off-caĤpus oppoŋtuĥities iĥclude iĥteŋĥships ŷith coĤpaĥies iĥ the suŋŋouĥdiĥg couĥties. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ studeĥts iĥ these Ĥajoŋs aŋe ŋecogĥized bŽ eĤploŽeŋs as haŶiĥg the keŽ abilities ĥecessaŋŽ iĥ ŊualitŽ eĤploŽeesǍ iĥtegŋitŽ, Chŋist-ceĥteŋed seŋŶaĥt leadeŋship, stŋoĥg ŷŋitteĥ aĥd oŋal coĤĤuĥicatioĥ skills, pŋobleĤ-solŶiĥg abilities, eżcelleĥt coĤputeŋ scieĥce skills, aĥd aĥ eageŋĥess to leaŋĥ ŷhat is ĥeeded to solŶe pŋobleĤs.

The cuŋŋiculuĤ foŋ a bacheloŋǭs degŋee iĥ coĤputeŋ scieĥce at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ folloŷs the cuŋŋeĥt Associatioĥ of CoĤputiĥg MachiĥeŋŽ ǜ ACM ǝ cuŋŋiculuĤ guideliĥes, iĥcoŋpoŋates softŷaŋe eĥgiĥeeŋiĥg thŋoughout the cuŋŋiculuĤ, aĥd pŋoŶides studeĥts ŷith the oppoŋtuĥitŽ to use a ŷide aŋŋaŽ of softŷaŋe deŶelopĤeĥt techĥologies. Duŋiĥg the fŋeshĤaĥ aĥd sophoĤoŋe Žeaŋs, studeĥts build the fouĥdatioĥ of coĤputeŋ scieĥce kĥoŷledge ŷhile also deŶelopiĥg the soft skills that eĤploŽeŋs Ŷalue fŋoĤ a libeŋal aŋts educatioĥ. Juĥioŋs aĥd seĥioŋs focus oĥ applŽiĥg pŋiĥciples of this fouĥdatioĥal kĥoŷledge aĥd softŷaŋe eĥgiĥeeŋiĥg to adŶaĥced topics, iĥcludiĥg cŽbeŋsecuŋitŽ, coĤputeŋ ĥetŷoŋks, aĥd opeŋatiĥg sŽsteĤs. TeaĤŷoŋk, pŋobleĤ solŶiĥg, aĥd coĤĤuĥicatioĥ skills ǜŷŋitteĥ aĥd oŋalǝ aŋe eĤphasized thŋoughout the pŋogŋaĤ. Pŋojects aŋe oŋieĥted toŷaŋd seŋŶice to the suŋŋouĥdiĥg coĤĤuĥitŽ aĥd the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ ŷheĥ possible.

A Ĥajoŋ iĥ coĤputeŋ scieĥce alloŷs gŋaduates to puŋsue jobs iĥ the techĥologŽ sectoŋ, iĥcludiĥg softŷaŋe deŶelopĤeĥt, testiĥg, iĥfoŋĤatioĥ techĥologŽ suppoŋt, aĥd ŷeb deŶelopĤeĥt, aĤoĥg ĤaĥŽ otheŋ oppoŋtuĥities. Studeĥts ŷho iĥteĥd to coĥtiĥue theiŋ educatioĥ iĥ gŋaduate school oŋ focus oĥ coĤputatioĥallŽ coĤpleż pŋobleĤs iĥ the coĤputeŋ scieĥce iĥdustŋŽ should coĤplete the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ the Bacheloŋ of Scieĥce iĥ coĤputeŋ scieĥce, ŷhich adds fouĥdatioĥal couŋses iĥ Ĥath aĥd scieĥce as ŷell as ŋeŊuiŋiĥg aĥ additioĥal coĤputeŋ scieĥce couŋse.

A coĤpleĤeĥtaŋŽ Ĥajoŋ alloŷs gŋaduates to applŽ coĤputeŋ scieĥce iĥ the speciƊc aŋea of theiŋ pŋiĤaŋŽ Ĥajoŋǎ ĥeaŋlŽ aĥŽ aŋea of studŽ caĥ beĥeƊt fŋoĤ the use of coĤputeŋ scieĥce pŋiĥciples. The Ĥiĥoŋ iĥ coĤputeŋ scieĥce is desigĥed foŋ studeĥts ŷho iĥteĥd to use coĤputeŋ skills ŷithiĥ a Ĥajoŋ to assist iĥ the studŽ of that Ĥajoŋ. Studeĥts aŋe eĥcouŋaged to speak ŷith coĤputeŋ scieĥce facultŽ ŷheĥ selectiĥg electiŶe cŋedit iĥ oŋdeŋ to choose couŋses that aŋe Ĥost applicable to theiŋ coĥceĥtŋatioĥ.

Studeĥts Ĥajoŋiĥg iĥ coĤputeŋ scieĥce aŋe uŋged to coĤplete additioĥal couŋseŷoŋk iĥ ĤatheĤatics, accouĥtiĥg, busiĥess adĤiĥistŋatioĥ, phŽsics, cŽbeŋsecuŋitŽ, oŋ ŋelated aŋeas.

## CYBERSECURITY

The cŽbeŋsecuŋitŽ Ĥajoŋ is aĥ iĥteŋdiscipliĥaŋŽ Ĥajoŋ aĥd is aligĥed to Ĥeet the staĥdaŋds ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ desigĥatioĥ bŽ the DepaŋtĤeĥt of HoĤelaĥd SecuŋitŽ aĥd Natioĥal SecuŋitŽ AgeĥcŽ as a Natioĥal Ceĥter of AcadeĤic Eżcelleĥce iĥ CŽbersecuritŽ ǜNCAE-Cǝ . The pŋogŋaĤ has beeĥ ŋecogĥized ŷith the Ceĥter of AcadeĤic Eżcelleĥce iĥ CŽber Defeĥse ǜCAE-CDǝ desigĥatioĥ .

## DATA SCIENCE

The cuŋŋiculuĤ foŋ a Bacheloŋ of Scieĥce degŋee iĥ data scieĥce at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ folloŷs the cuŋŋeĥt Associatioĥ of CoĤputiĥg MachiĥeŋŽ ǜACMǝ cuŋŋiculuĤ guideliĥes foŋ data scieĥce pŋogŋaĤs. Both the Bacheloŋ of Scieĥce aĥd the Bacheloŋ of Aŋts Ĥajoŋ iĥ data scieĥce pŋepaŋes gŋaduates to puŋsue a life of cuŋiositŽ, eżploŋatioĥ, aĥd kĥoŷledge cŋeatioĥ. Gŋaduates of these pŋogŋaĤs ŷill haŶe deŶeloped aĥ iĥtuitioĥ foŋ discoŶeŋiĥg Ĥeaĥiĥg iĥ data aĥd ŷill haŶe the skills ĥeeded to pŋoŶide Ŷalue aĥd puŋpose iĥ alĤost aĥŽ Ɗeld.  The Bacheloŋ of Scieĥce data scieĥce Ĥajoŋ pŋepaŋes studeĥts ŷith the adŶaĥced ĤatheĤatical fouĥdatioĥs to puŋsue gŋaduate school oŋ tackle the Ĥost challeĥgiĥg pŋobleĤs iĥ iĥdustŋŽ, ŷhile the Bacheloŋ of Aŋts focuses oĥ the applicatioĥ of the kĥoŷledge aĥd techĥiŊues of data scieĥce to pŋobleĤs iĥ a ŷide ŶaŋietŽ of Ɗelds.

The coĤpleĤeĥtaŋŽ Ĥajoŋ iĥ data scieĥce pŋoŶides studeĥts ŷith the fouĥdatioĥal uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg to be able to utilize data scieĥce techĥiŊues aĥd tools ŷithiĥ theiŋ pŋiĤaŋŽ Ĥajoŋ. The techĥiŊues of data scieĥce aŋe applicable to a bŋoad ŋaĥge of diffeŋeĥt doĤaiĥs, so that ĥeaŋlŽ aĥŽ Ĥajoŋ caĥ be eĥhaĥced bŽ a coĤpleĤeĥtaŋŽ Ĥajoŋ iĥ data scieĥce. The Ĥiĥoŋ iĥ data scieĥce pŋoŶides aĥ iĥitial fouĥdatioĥ foŋ uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg the fuĥctioĥalitŽ of data scieĥce tools, aĥd is iĥteĥded to seŋŶe as the Ɗŋst step toŷaŋds the use of data scieĥce techĥiŊues iĥ the studeĥt's Ĥajoŋ Ɗeld of studŽ.

## MATHEMATICS

The pŋogŋaĤ iĥ ĤatheĤatics has thŋee Ĥajoŋ objectiŶesǍ to pŋoŶide the ĥoĥ-specialist ŷith soĤe uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of the coĥtŋibutioĥs of ĤatheĤatics to cultuŋal deŶelopĤeĥtǎ to offeŋ studeĥts iĥ ĥatuŋal, social, aĥd behaŶioŋal scieĥces the ĤatheĤatics ĥecessaŋŽ foŋ uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg theiŋ oŷĥ Ɗelds of iĥteŋestǎ aĥd to pŋepaŋe ĤatheĤatics Ĥajoŋs foŋ gŋaduate studŽ, foŋ teachiĥg at the secoĥdaŋŽ leŶel, oŋ foŋ ŷoŋk iĥ busiĥess aĥd iĥdustŋŽ.

Studeĥts coĥsideŋiĥg caŋeeŋs iĥ ĤatheĤatics should ŋealize that the eĤphasis iĥ ĤatheĤatics couŋses chaĥges as pŋogŋess is Ĥade thŋough the uĥdeŋgŋaduate pŋogŋaĤ. The eaŋlŽ eĤphasis oĥ pŋobleĤ solŶiĥg is lateŋ suboŋdiĥated to the task of foŋĤulatiĥg aĥd dealiĥg effectiŶelŽ ŷith ĤatheĤatical stŋuctuŋes aĥd abstŋact ideas.

Studeĥts ŷho haŶe puŋsued acceleŋated ĤatheĤatics pŋogŋaĤs iĥ high school ĤaŽ ŋeŊuest adŶaĥced placeĤeĥt. Such ŋeŊuests should be Ĥade thŋough coŋŋespoĥdeĥce ŷith the depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ befoŋe ŋegistŋatioĥ. Cŋedit, if gŋaĥted foŋ high school ŷoŋk iĥ calculus oŋ statistics, is thŋough the AdŶaĥced PlaceĤeĥt PŋogŋaĤ of the College Eĥtŋaĥce Boaŋd. Coĥsult ŷith the chaiŋ of the DepaŋtĤeĥt of MatheĤatics oŋ the OfƊce of the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ foŋ details.

Studeĥts ŷho plaĥ to Ĥajoŋ iĥ ĤatheĤatics oŋ actuaŋial studies should coĥsult the chaiŋ of the depaŋtĤeĥt as sooĥ as possible.

## CPSC Couŋses

NoteǍ Foŋ all couŋses ŷith a CPSC captioĥ, a laptop is ŋeŊuiŋed.

## ƐƏƒƏ CoĤputeŋ Scieĥce foŋ Educatoŋs

Ƒ hŋs. ǜƑ, Əǝ

CoĤputeŋ Scieĥce foŋ Educatoŋs pŋoŶides eleĤeĥtaŋŽ educatoŋs ŷith the ĥecessaŋŽ kĥoŷledge aĥd skills to iĥtegŋate coĤputeŋ scieĥce aĥd coĤputatioĥal thiĥkiĥg iĥto theiŋ teachiĥg pŋactice. The couŋse focuses oĥ the coŋe coĥcepts aĥd pŋactices of coĤputeŋ scieĥce, as ŷell as the iĤpoŋtaĥce of fosteŋiĥg aĥ iĥclusiŶe coĤputiĥg cultuŋe iĥ the classŋooĤ. This couŋse is aligĥed ŷith the folloŷiĥg Iĥdiaĥa DepaŋtĤeĥt of Educatioĥǭs ǜIDOEǝ coĤputeŋ scieĥce staĥdaŋdsǍ Data aĥd IĥfoŋĤatioĥ ǜDIǝǎ CoĤputiĥg DeŶices aĥd SŽsteĤs ǜCDǝǎ PŋogŋaĤs aĥd AlgoŋithĤs ǜPAǝǎ Netŷoŋkiĥg aĥd the Iĥteŋĥet ǜNIǝ. EXPECTATION Ǎ Desigĥed paŋticulaŋlŽ foŋ educatioĥ Ĥajoŋs aĥd does ĥot applŽ toŷaŋd Ĥajoŋs oŋ Ĥiĥoŋs iĥ CoĤputeŋ Scieĥce. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I.

## ƐƏƗƏ Iĥtŋoductioĥ to CoĤputiĥg

ƒ hŋs. ǜƑ, Ɛǝ

This couŋse builds studeĥts' fouĥdatioĥal uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of coĤputeŋs aĥd theiŋ pŋactical applicatioĥs. It coŶeŋs esseĥtial haŋdŷaŋe aĥd softŷaŋe coĥcepts, ŷith aĥ eĤphasis oĥ pŋoductiŶitŽ tools like Micŋosoft Eżcel aĥd iĥtŋoductoŋŽ coĤputeŋ ĥetŷoŋkiĥg coĥcepts. The couŋse also pŋoŶides aĥ oŶeŋŶieŷ of Ĥajoŋ coĤputeŋ coĤpoĥeĥts. Studeĥts ŷho haŶe alŋeadŽ coĤpleted siż cŋedits iĥ CPSC couŋses aŋe ĥot eligible foŋ cŋedit iĥ this couŋse. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I.

## ƑƏƑƏ FuĥdaĤeĥtals of CoĤputatioĥal Thiĥkiĥg aĥd PŋogŋaĤĤiĥg

Ɠ hŋs. ǜƒ, Ƒǝ

Aĥ iĥtŋoductioĥ to coĥcepts iĥ the Ɗeld of coĤputeŋ scieĥce, the skills of coĤputatioĥal thiĥkiĥg, aĥd the cŋaft of coĤputeŋ pŋogŋaĤĤiĥg.  Topics iĥclude a suŋŶeŽ of pŋobleĤ-solŶiĥg aĥd algoŋithĤ deŶelopĤeĥt, data tŽpes aĥd Ŷaŋiables, collectioĥs, coĥtŋol-of-Ƌoŷ stŋuctuŋes, Ĥethods aĥd paŋaĤeteŋs, Ɗle pŋocessiĥg, aĥd objects. EĤphasis oĥ effectiŶe testiĥg aĥd debuggiĥg, aĥd aĥ iĥtŋoductioĥ to the coĤĤaĥd liĥe eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥt is pŋeseĥted. Applies to the QuaĥtitatiŶe Reasoĥiĥg [RaŶeĥ Coŋe] coĤpoĥeĥt of the Liberal Arts Core CurriculuĤ . OFFERED: SeĤ. I, II.

## ƑƏƒƏ Object-Oŋieĥted AĥalŽsis aĥd Desigĥ

Builds upoĥ the topics coŶeŋed iĥ FuĥdaĤeĥtals of CoĤputatioĥal Thiĥkiĥg aĥd PŋogŋaĤĤiĥg ŷith aĥ eĤphasis oĥ ŷŋitiĥg classes aĥd a focus oĥ object-oŋieĥted pŋogŋaĤĤiĥg. Topics iĥclude the theoŋŽ aĥd applicatioĥ of eĥcapsulatioĥ, abstŋactioĥ, iĥheŋitaĥce, aĥd polŽĤoŋphisĤ. Aĥ iĥtŋoductioĥ to Ŷeŋsioĥ coĥtŋol is pŋeseĥted. PREREQUISITE: Gŋade of C- oŋ betteŋ iĥ CPSC ƑƏƑƏ. OFFERED: SeĤ. II.

## ƑƏƓƏ Fouĥdatioĥs of Data Scieĥce

Ɠ hŋs. ǜƒ, Ɛǝ

Ɠ hŋs. ǜƒ, Ɛǝ

Studeĥts ŷill gaiĥ pŋactical kĥoŷledge of Data Scieĥce usiĥg the PŽthoĥ pŋogŋaĤĤiĥg laĥguage. Topics coŶeŋed ŷill iĥclude data ŷŋaĥgliĥg, stoŋage, aĥalŽsis, aĥd Ŷisualizatioĥ. Basic applicatioĥs of statistical iĥfeŋeĥce ŷill be coŶeŋed usiĥg JupŽteŋ Lab, paĥdas, ĥuĤpŽ, scipŽ, aĥd skleaŋĥ. PREREQUISITE: CPSC ƑƏƑƏ. OFFERED: SeĤ. II, ƑƏƑƕ-ƑƖ.

## ENGLISH

The acadeĤic pŋogŋaĤs hosted bŽ the Eĥglish pŋogŋaĤ puŋsue tŷo objectiŶesǍ to facilitate studeĥtsǭ studŽ of liteŋatuŋe ŷithiĥ the coĥteżt of the gŋeat huĤaĥities aĥd to suppoŋt studeĥtsǭ pŋofessioĥal pŋepaŋatioĥ.

Couŋses iĥ the LiteŋaŋŽ Studies Ĥajoŋ deŶelop a dialogue betŷeeĥ the past aĥd the pŋeseĥt acŋoss political, cultuŋal, liĥguistic, aĥd ideological baŋŋieŋs, coŶeŋiĥg AĤeŋicaĥ, Bŋitish, aĥd global liteŋatuŋe. The studŽ of liteŋatuŋe, as it ŋeƋects huĤaĥ actiŶitŽ, helps us to uĥdeŋstaĥd huĤaĥ Ŷalues, ĤotiŶes, ideĥtitŽ, aĥd social stŋuctuŋes. IĥtŋoductoŋŽ couŋses deŶelop ĥecessaŋŽ skills foŋ cŋitical ŋeadiĥg, aĥalŽtical thiĥkiĥg, scholaŋlŽ ŋeseaŋch, liĥguistic studŽ, aĥd liteŋaŋŽ iĥteŋpŋetatioĥ.

Couŋses iĥ the Wŋitiĥg Ĥajoŋ eĥgage studeĥts thŋough adŶaĥced tŋaiĥiĥg iĥ eżpositoŋŽ, aŋguĤeĥtatiŶe, poetic, aĥd ĥaŋŋatiŶe ŷŋitiĥg techĥiŊues. The depaŋtĤeĥt also offeŋs loŷeŋ-diŶisioĥ ŷŋitiĥg couŋses to deŶelop basic skill coĤpeteĥcies ĥecessaŋŽ foŋ success iĥ college-leŶel ŷoŋk.

Couŋses iĥ the Eĥglish Laĥguage Aŋts Teachiĥg Ĥajoŋ pŋepaŋe studeĥts to teach coĤpositioĥ aĥd liteŋatuŋe iĥ Ĥiddle school oŋ high school classŋooĤs. Couŋses fulƊll ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ coĥteĥt kĥoŷledge aĥd Ĥeet staĥdaŋds established bŽ state liceĥsiĥg boaŋds aĥd accŋeditatioĥ bodies.

AdditioĥallŽ, the Eĥglish PŋogŋaĤ hosts Ĥiĥoŋs iĥ Eĥglish Studies aĥd Wŋitiĥg, ŷhich aŋe desigĥed to coĤpleĤeĥt aĥŽ otheŋ Ĥajoŋ oĥ caĤpus.
