## HISTORY

The tŋaditioĥal Ĥodel of educatioĥ iĥ histoŋŽ has beeĥ to pŋepaŋe histoŋŽ Ĥajoŋs foŋ possible gŋaduate-leŶel ŷoŋk aĥd offeŋiĥg histoŋŽ aĥd educatioĥ Ĥajoŋs the ĥecessaŋŽ coĤpŋeheĥsiŶe uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of histoŋŽ subjects to puŋsue caŋeeŋs iĥ educatioĥ. Such is the Ĥodel foŋ both loŷeŋ- aĥd uppeŋ-leŶel couŋseŷoŋk iĥ histoŋŽ, ĥot oĥlŽ at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ but ĥeaŋlŽ all libeŋal aŋts uĥiŶeŋsities.

This is as it should be, aĥd ŷe ceŋtaiĥlŽ do ĥot ĥeglect these goals. HoŷeŶeŋ, the histoŋŽ facultŽ of Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ belieŶe it cŋitical foŋ studeĥts to thiĥk holisticallŽ aĥd delibeŋatelŽ iĥtegŋate iĥto ouŋ tŋaditioĥal histoŋical faŋe bŋoadeŋ theoŋetical issues aĥd life skills ǥ paŋticulaŋlŽ coĤĤuĥicatioĥ aĥd cŋitical-thiĥkiĥg skills ǥ that studeĥts ŷill Ɗĥd useful aĥd Ĥaŋketable.

AccoŋdiĥglŽ, ouŋ couŋse offeŋiĥgs puŋsue thŋee pŋiĤaŋŽ goalsǍ

- Histoŋical coĥteĥt aĥd cŋitical-thiĥkiĥg skills Ǎ The tŋaditioĥal Ĥatteŋ of a histoŋŽ couŋse focuses oĥ Ĥajoŋ eŶeĥts, theĤes, people, etc. Studeĥts ŷill coĥtiĥue to ŋeceiŶe a stŋoĥg aĥd coĤpŋeheĥsiŶe educatioĥ iĥ the bŋead-aĥd-butteŋ topics that haŶe alŷaŽs deƊĥed the histoŋŽ discipliĥe.
- Theoŋetical coĥteĥt aĥd cŋitical-thiĥkiĥg skills: PaŋticulaŋlŽ iĥ uppeŋ-diŶisioĥ histoŋŽ couŋses, the bŋoadeŋ theĤes aĥd issues ŷhich aŋe ŋooted iĥ histoŋical eŶeĥts aĥd issues also focus to speak diŋectlŽ to pŋeseĥt as ŷell as past coĥceŋĥs, such as the pŋoĤise aĥd pŋobleĤs of deĤocŋacŽ, the ĥatuŋe of coĤĤuĥitŽ, global affaiŋs, aĥd the Ŷaŋious challeĥges ŋelated to ŷŋitiĥg aĥd uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg biogŋaphŽ.
- Wŋitiĥg aĥd coĤĤuĥicatioĥ skills Ǎ Uppeŋ-leŶel histoŋŽ couŋses iĥ paŋticulaŋ place aĥ eĤphasis oĥ deŶelopiĥg the studeĥtǭs coĤĤuĥicatioĥ skills but ŷith diffeŋeĥt Ŷaŋiatioĥs foŋ each couŋse, such as tŋaditioĥal teŋĤ papeŋsǎ a seŋies of bŋief, shoŋteŋ papeŋs culĤiĥatiĥg iĥ a laŋgeŋ pŋojectǎ peŋsoĥal iĥteŋŶieŷsǎ ethical aĥd pŋofessioĥal use of electŋoĥic coĤĤuĥicatioĥs such as Tŷitteŋǎ aŋchiŶal ŋeseaŋchǎ aĥd/oŋ ŷŋitiĥg pŋojects puŋsued iĥ cooŋdiĥatioĥ ŷith eżpeŋieĥtial aĥd techĥologŽ-dŋiŶeĥ coĤpoĥeĥts.

The histoŋŽ degŋee pŋepaŋes studeĥts foŋ gŋaduate aĥd laŷ schoolǎ caŋeeŋs iĥ public seŋŶice, ĤuseuĤs, aŋchiŶes, aĥd ĥoĥpŋoƊt associatioĥsǎ educatioĥǎ aĥd ĤaĥŽ otheŋ diŶeŋse Ɗelds.

## PUBLIC HISTORY

The public histoŋŽ Ĥajoŋ aĥd Ĥiĥoŋ pŋepaŋes studeĥts ŷho ŷish to ŷoŋk iĥ the Ɗeld of histoŋŽ outside the classŋooĤ, iĥ settiĥgs ŷheŋe histoŋŽ is eĥcouĥteŋed bŽ the publicǍ ĤuseuĤs, coĤĤuĥitŽ histoŋŽ ceĥteŋs, ĥatioĥal paŋks aĥd histoŋical sites, aĥd ĤaĥŽ Ĥoŋe settiĥgs. Public histoŋiaĥs ǥ ĤuseuĤ staff aĥd cuŋatoŋs, goŶeŋĥĤeĥt histoŋiaĥs, aŋchiŶists, histoŋical site iĥteŋpŋeteŋs, pŋeseŋŶatioĥists ǥ coĤe fŋoĤ a ŶaŋietŽ of discipliĥes.

Pŋepaŋatioĥ foŋ ŷoŋk iĥ public histoŋŽ is theŋefoŋe, aĥd ĥecessaŋilŽ, iĥteŋdiscipliĥaŋŽ, as it pŋepaŋes iĥdiŶiduals to pŋeseŋŶe aĥd tŋaĥsĤit ouŋ past to the ĥoĥ-acadeĤic public.

## SOCIAL STUDIES TEACHING

To fulƊll the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ teachiĥg social studies at the seĥioŋ high/Ĥiddle school leŶel, studeĥts Ĥust coĤplete speciƊc couŋses iĥ tŷo teachiĥg Ɗelds aĥd iĥ pŋofessioĥal educatioĥ. The ŋeŊuiŋed teachiĥg Ɗelds aŋe histoŋical peŋspectiŶes aĥd goŶeŋĥĤeĥt &amp; citizeĥship. Studeĥts aŋe stŋoĥglŽ eĥcouŋaged to puŋsue a thiŋd Ɗeld of liceĥsuŋe iĥ ecoĥoĤics, psŽchologŽ, sociologŽ, oŋ special educatioĥ.

All couŋses listed foŋ histoŋical peŋspectiŶes, aĥd soĤe couŋses listed foŋ goŶeŋĥĤeĥt &amp; citizeĥship, ecoĥoĤics, psŽchologŽ, aĥd sociologŽ, Ĥeet the staĥdaŋds foŋ social studies teachiĥg as established bŽ the Natioĥal Couĥcil foŋ the Social Studies, thus pŋepaŋiĥg caĥdidates to teach the folloŷiĥg cŋiteŋiaǍ

- cultuŋe aĥd cultuŋal diŶeŋsitŽ
- coĥtiĥuitŽ aĥd chaĥge
- people, places, aĥd eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥt
- iĥdiŶidual deŶelopĤeĥt aĥd ideĥtitŽ
- iĥdiŶiduals, gŋoups, aĥd iĥstitutioĥs

## DEPARTMENT OF NATURAL SCIENCES

Dŋ. TŽleŋ WilliaĤsoĥ, chaiŋ FacultŽǍ Dŋ. Baĥkole, Dŋ. Caŋŋ, Dŋ. R. TaŽloŋ, Dŋ. WilliaĤsoĥ

The DepaŋtĤeĥt of Natuŋal Scieĥces pŋoŶides a ŊualitŽ educatioĥal pŋogŋaĤ coĤbiĥiĥg a bŋoad coŋe cuŋŋiculuĤ ŷith fouŋ aŋeas of specializatioĥǍ

- Pŋe-Pŋofessioĥal: cuŋŋiculuĤ desigĥed to eĥhaĥce the studeĥtǭs appŋeciatioĥ of aĥd success iĥ a pŋofessioĥal educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ iĥ Ŷaŋious Ĥedical aŋts.
- Moleculaŋ/BiocheĤistŋŽ/MicŋobiologŽ: cuŋŋiculuĤ desigĥed to pŋoŶide the skills, kĥoŷledge, aĥd aĥalŽtic abilitŽ to succeed iĥ Ĥodeŋĥ biologŽ ŋeseaŋch aĥd/oŋ iĥdustŋial aŋeĥas.
- Scieĥce Educatioĥ: cuŋŋiculuĤ choseĥ to pŋepaŋe studeĥts to be at the foŋefŋoĥt of scieĥce educatioĥ foŋ the ƑƐst ceĥtuŋŽ.
- EcologŽ/EĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥtal: cuŋŋiculuĤ desigĥed to pŋepaŋe foŋ bacheloŋ eĥtŋŽ pŋogŋaĤs iĥ Ɗeld biologŽ aĥd eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥtal scieĥce aĥd gŋaduate studies iĥ the Ɗelds of ecologŽ, the eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥt, aĥd zoologŽ.

Foŋ those studeĥts ŷaĥtiĥg to go oĥ to gŋaduate school oŋ Ĥedical school, a BS iĥ BiologŽ oŋ BiocheĤistŋŽ is stŋoĥglŽ ŋecoĤĤeĥded. Foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ ŋegaŋdiĥg these pŋogŋaĤs, coĥtact the depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ oŋ Ŷisit the depaŋtĤeĥtal ofƊce ǜHaŋtuĥg ƑƏƕǝ.

The ecologŽ/eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥtal coĥceĥtŋatioĥ is gŋeatlŽ eĥhaĥced thŋough Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs paŋticipatioĥ iĥ pŋogŋaĤs offeŋed bŽ the Au Sable Iĥstitute . The iĥstitute has Ɗeld statioĥs iĥ ĥoŋtheŋĥ Michigaĥ, Vaŋa Blaĥca ǜCosta Ricaǝ, aĥd TaĤil Nadu ǜSouth Iĥdiaǝ, as ŷell as offeŋiĥg oĥliĥe couŋses. Each statioĥ offeŋs Ɗeld couŋses ǜĤostlŽ duŋiĥg the suĤĤeŋǝ iĥ ecologŽ aĥd eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥtal scieĥce appŋopŋiate to its locatioĥ. Studeĥts takiĥg couŋses fŋoĤ Au Sable ŋeĤaiĥ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ studeĥts. Siĥce the uĥiŶeŋsitŽ has beeĥ ideĥtiƊed as aĥ iĥstitutioĥ eligible foŋ Ɗĥaĥcial gŋaĥts, ŊualiƊed studeĥts ĤaŽ be aŷaŋded Au Sable felloŷships aĥd scholaŋships. Iĥteŋested studeĥts should coĥtact Dŋ. Scott Caŋŋ foŋ fuŋtheŋ applicatioĥ iĥfoŋĤatioĥ.

The depaŋtĤeĥt uĥdeŋtakes adŶisiĥg aĥd supeŋŶisioĥ of uĥdeŋgŋaduate pŋogŋaĤs iĥ a ŶaŋietŽ of health aĥd scieĥce Ŷocatioĥs otheŋ thaĥ those speciƊcallŽ Ĥeĥtioĥed aboŶe ǜe.g. phaŋĤacŽ, phŽsical aĥd occupatioĥal theŋapŽ, phŽsiciaĥǭs assistaĥt, etc.ǝ. These pŋe-pŋofessioĥal pŋogŋaĤs ŋeŊuiŋe coĤpletioĥ of tŷo to fouŋ Žeaŋs at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ folloŷed bŽ gŋaduate oŋ cliĥical tŋaiĥiĥg at aĥotheŋ iĥstitutioĥ iĥ oŋdeŋ to eĥteŋ the pŋofessioĥ oŋ staĥd foŋ liceĥsuŋe eżaĤiĥatioĥs. BiologŽ facultŽ shaŋe adŶisiĥg foŋ these pŋogŋaĤs aĥd iĥteŋested studeĥts should coĥtact theĤ foŋ additioĥal iĥfoŋĤatioĥ.

## BIOLOGY TEACHING TRACK ǜƒ+Ɛǝ

PsŽchologŽ is the scieĥtiƊc studŽ of the bŋaiĥ, Ĥiĥd, aĥd behaŶioŋ. It is appŋoached fŋoĤ phŽsiological, cogĥitiŶe, aĥd social peŋspectiŶes. This ŋeŊuiŋes the deŶelopĤeĥt of skills iĥ cŋitical thiĥkiĥg, ŊuaĥtitatiŶe ŋeasoĥiĥg, speakiĥg, ŷŋitiĥg, aĥd ethical decisioĥ-Ĥakiĥg.

## CRIMINAL JUSTICE

The cŋiĤiĥal justice pŋogŋaĤ is dedicated to ĥuŋtuŋiĥg pŋiĥcipled leadeŋs ŷho iĥtegŋate Chŋistiaĥ Ŷalues ŷith the highest staĥdaŋds of pŋofessioĥal eżcelleĥce iĥ the Ɗeld of cŋiĤiĥal justice. Rooted iĥ ouŋ coĤĤitĤeĥt to the Chŋistiaĥ faith, ouŋ Ĥissioĥ is to educate aĥd eĤpoŷeŋ studeĥts to Ĥake Ĥeaĥiĥgful coĥtŋibutioĥs to societŽ, pŋoĤotiĥg justice, coĤpassioĥ, iĥtegŋitŽ, aĥd faiŋĥess.

The CŋiĤiĥal Justice pŋogŋaĤ offeŋs a Ĥajoŋ, aĥ associate's degŋee, aĥd a Ĥiĥoŋ, aŶailable both iĥ-peŋsoĥ aĥd oĥliĥe. The cŋiĤiĥal justice oĥliĥe degŋee pŋogŋaĤs aŋe desigĥed foŋ adult studeĥts puŋsuiĥg caŋeeŋs iĥ cŋiĤiĥal justice, as ŷell as foŋ iĥdiŶiduals alŋeadŽ eĤploŽed iĥ the cŋiĤiĥal justice Ɗeld.

## MAJORS

## CRIMINAL JUSTICE MAJOR  ǜBA ƐƑƏ hŋs. ǎ CRIM ƒƓ hŋs. ǝ

The cŋiĤiĥal justice Ĥajoŋ eĥables studeĥts to eĥteŋ eĤploŽĤeĥt iĥ Ɗelds ŋelated to laŷ eĥfoŋceĤeĥt, couŋts, coŋŋectioĥs, ŶictiĤ adŶocacŽ aĥd assistaĥce, aĥd also pŋoŶides a fouĥdatioĥ foŋ gŋaduate studŽ. Studeĥts gaiĥ pŋepaŋatioĥ foŋ caŋeeŋs thŋoughout cŋiĤiĥal justice iĥ the pŋiŶate occupatioĥal sectoŋ as ŷell as ŷith public ageĥcies at the local, state, oŋ fedeŋal leŶel.

- CRIM ƑƔƐƏ, ƑƔƑƏ, ƒƐƐƏ
- Ɠ houŋs fŋoĤ CRIM ƓƗƐƏ aĥd ƒ houŋs fŋoĤ CRIM ƓƘƏƏ
- SOCI ƑƏƑƏ oŋ SOCI ƑƏƐƏ
- SOCI ƒƖƏƏ
- Ƙ houŋs fŋoĤ additioĥal CRIM couŋses
- Studeĥts ŷho ŷish to take additioĥal couŋseŷoŋk pŋoŶidiĥg Ĥoŋe bŋeadth aĥd depth iĥ the Ɗeld should coĥsult ŷith theiŋ adŶisoŋ coĥceŋĥiĥg the appŋopŋiate couŋses.

- Studeĥts ŷho ŷish to take additioĥal couŋseŷoŋk pŋoŶidiĥg added bŋeadth aĥd depth iĥ the Ɗeld should coĥsult ŷith theiŋ adŶisoŋ coĥceŋĥiĥg the appŋopŋiate couŋses.

## POLITICAL SCIENCE

The political scieĥce pŋogŋaĤ offeŋs thŋee Ĥajoŋs, each of ŷhich is desigĥed to tŋaĥsfoŋĤ studeĥts ŷith aĥ iĥteŋest iĥ oŋ coĥceŋĥ foŋ politics iĥto gŋaduates ŷho caĥ uĥdeŋstaĥd, eŶaluate, Ĥaĥage, aĥd shape political eŶeĥts aĥd goŶeŋĥĤeĥtal actioĥs iĥ a Ĥaĥĥeŋ coĥsisteĥt ŷith a Chŋistiaĥ faith peŋspectiŶe.

The Ĥajoŋs offeŋed bŽ the political scieĥce pŋogŋaĤ pŋoŶide eżcelleĥt tŋaiĥiĥg foŋ a ŶaŋietŽ of caŋeeŋs. Receĥt gŋaduates aŋe ŷoŋkiĥg iĥ goŶeŋĥĤeĥt ǜĥatioĥal, state, aĥd localǝ, laŷ, electoŋal politics, ĥoĥpŋoƊts, aĥd busiĥess.

Studeĥts iĥ the political scieĥce pŋogŋaĤ aŋe eżpected to successfullŽ coĤplete the fouĥdatioĥal couŋses befoŋe atteĤptiĥg uppeŋ-diŶisioĥ couŋseŷoŋk. TheŽ aŋe also stŋoĥglŽ eĥcouŋaged to puŋsue a Ĥiĥoŋ oŋ a secoĥd Ĥajoŋ iĥ oĥe oŋ Ĥoŋe of the folloŷiĥgǍ histoŋŽ, ecoĥoĤics, Ĥodeŋĥ laĥguages, jouŋĥalisĤ, legal studies, peace aĥd coĥƋict tŋaĥsfoŋĤatioĥ, psŽchologŽ, sociologŽ, oŋ ŷoĤeĥǭs studies. Miĥoŋs oŋ secoĥd Ĥajoŋs should be selected oĥlŽ afteŋ coĥsultatioĥ ŷith a political scieĥce pŋogŋaĤ adŶisoŋ. Studeĥts aŋe also eĥcouŋaged to coĥsideŋ coĤpletiĥg aĥ iĥteŋĥship oŋ takiĥg a seĤesteŋ to paŋticipate iĥ aĥ off-caĤpus pŋogŋaĤ. Appŋopŋiate oppoŋtuĥities caĥ be ideĥtiƊed bŽ coĥsultiĥg a political scieĥce pŋogŋaĤ adŶisoŋ.

## SECURITY STUDIES

## DiŋectoŋǍ Dŋ. Michael Fŋaĥk

The SecuŋitŽ Studies PŋogŋaĤ is desigĥed to deŶelop gŋaduates ŷith the pŋactical kĥoŷledge, techĥical skills, aĥd pŋofessioĥal ethics fŋoĤ a Chŋistiaĥ-faith peŋspectiŶe, to seŋŶe oĥ the fŋoĥt liĥes iĥ defeĥdiĥg the ĥatioĥ, ouŋ coĤĤuĥities, aĥd iĥstitutioĥs fŋoĤ thŋeats, foŋeigĥ aĥd doĤestic, iĥ both the phŽsical aĥd cŽbeŋ ŋealĤs.

The pŋogŋaĤ coĥsists of Ĥajoŋs iĥ ĥatioĥal secuŋitŽ aĥd cŽbeŋsecuŋitŽ. Each Ĥajoŋ has aĥ iĥteŋdiscipliĥaŋŽ cuŋŋiculuĤ that iĥcludes fouĥdatioĥal couŋses, ĥatioĥal secuŋitŽ policŽ couŋses, Chŋistiaĥ ethics, aĥd ŋeleŶaĥt electiŶes.

Studeĥts iĥ both Ĥajoŋs aŋe eżpected to successfullŽ coĤplete the fouĥdatioĥal couŋses befoŋe atteĤptiĥg uppeŋ- diŶisioĥ couŋseŷoŋk. Studeĥts aŋe stŋoĥglŽ eĥcouŋaged to discuss secoĥd Ĥajoŋs, Ĥiĥoŋs, aĥd iĥteŋĥship oppoŋtuĥities ŷith a pŋogŋaĤ adŶisoŋ.

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ has beeĥ desigĥated bŽ the Natioĥal SecuritŽ AgeĥcŽ as a Ceĥter of AcadeĤic Eżcelleĥce iĥ CŽber Defeĥse Educatioĥ ǜCAE-CDǝ, ceŋtifŽiĥg the cŽbeŋsecuŋitŽ Ĥajoŋ as a Ŷalidated PŋogŋaĤ of StudŽ.

## SOCIAL WORK

DiŋectoŋǍ Dŋ. LollŽ Baŋgeŋstock

The social ŷoŋk Ĥajoŋ is accŋedited bŽ the Couĥcil oĥ Social Woŋk Educatioĥ ǜCSWEǝ aĥd pŋepaŋes studeĥts to becoĤe geĥeŋalist social ŷoŋk pŋactitioĥeŋs iĥ eĥtŋŽ-leŶel huĤaĥ seŋŶice positioĥs oŋ to eĥteŋ gŋaduate studŽ iĥ social ŷoŋk. Gŋaduates aŋe eligible to applŽ foŋ cŋedeĥtialiĥg as begiĥĥiĥg-leŶel social ŷoŋk pŋactitioĥeŋs iĥ Ĥost states.

## Missioĥ

The Ĥissioĥ of the Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Social Woŋk PŋogŋaĤ is to pŋepaŋe coĤpeteĥt, coĤpassioĥate, aĥd effectiŶe eĥtŋŽ-leŶel social ŷoŋkeŋs ŷhoǍ

- Eżeŋcise pŋofessioĥalisĤ aĥd iĥtegŋitŽ bŽ deĤoĥstŋatiĥg kĥoŷledge, skills, aĥd Ŷalues gŋouĥded iĥ a peŋsoĥ-iĥ-eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥt fŋaĤeŷoŋk aĥd thŋough a coĤĤitĤeĥt to scieĥtiƊc iĥŊuiŋŽ aĥd eŶideĥce-based pŋactice.
- Puŋsue social, ŋacial, ecoĥoĤic, aĥd eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥtal justice bŽ actiŶelŽ ŷoŋkiĥg to challeĥge oppŋessiŶe sŽsteĤs aĥd to eĤpoŷeŋ Ĥaŋgiĥalized aĥd Ŷulĥeŋable populatioĥs.
- Respect huĤaĥ diŶeŋsitŽ bŽ Ŷaluiĥg the digĥitŽ aĥd ŷoŋth of eŶeŋŽ peŋsoĥ aĥd pŋoĤotiĥg iĥclusiŶe aĥd eŊuitable policies aĥd pŋactices.
- AdŶocate foŋ uĥiŶeŋsal huĤaĥ ŋights bŽ ŷoŋkiĥg to eliĤiĥate poŶeŋtŽ aĥd to cŋeate societal coĥditioĥs that adŶaĥce huĤaĥ aĥd coĤĤuĥitŽ ŷell-beiĥg.
- CultiŶate huĤaĥ ŋelatioĥships bŽ eĥgagiĥg iĥ collaboŋatiŶe paŋtĥeŋships ŷith iĥdiŶiduals, faĤilies, gŋoups, oŋgaĥizatioĥs, aĥd coĤĤuĥities both locallŽ aĥd globallŽ.
- Pŋactice seŋŶice to otheŋs bŽ coĤĤittiĥg to do good, seek justice, ŋebuke aĥd ŋectifŽ the heaŋts of oppŋessoŋs, defeĥd oŋphaĥs aĥd ŷidoŷs, aĥd help those iĥ ĥeed ǜbased oĥ Isaiah ƐǍƐƖǝ.

ǜŋeŶised ƑƏƑƓǝ

## AdĤissioĥ to the Social Woŋk PŋogŋaĤ

The Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Social Woŋk PŋogŋaĤ is a caŋefullŽ coĥstŋucted baccalauŋeate degŋee cuŋŋiculuĤ accŋedited bŽ the Couĥcil oĥ Social Woŋk Educatioĥ ǜCSWEǝ.

Studeĥts ĤaŽ applŽ foŋ adĤissioĥ to the pŋogŋaĤ ŷheĥ theŽ haŶeǍ

- coĤpleted SOCI ƑƏƐƏ oŋ ƑƏƑƏǎ SOWK ƑƏƏƏ, ƑƐƏƏ
- eaŋĥed a ĤiĥiĤuĤ Ƒ.Ə cuĤulatiŶe GPA
- eaŋĥed a ĤiĥiĤuĤ Ƒ.Ɣ GPA iĥ the Ĥajoŋ ŷith a gŋade of C- oŋ betteŋ iĥ all couŋses applicable to the Ĥajoŋ
- eaŋĥed a gŋade of C- oŋ betteŋ iĥ ENGL ƐƐƑƏ oŋ its eŊuiŶaleĥt

The pŋocess foŋ applŽiĥg to the Social Woŋk PŋogŋaĤ is toǍ

- subĤit a coĤpleted applicatioĥ foŋĤ
- subĤit tŷo letteŋs of ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥ
- coĤplete aĥ oĥliĥe social ŷoŋk ethics Ŋuiz
- coĤplete aĥ iĥteŋŶieŷ ŷith the Social Woŋk PŋogŋaĤ facultŽ

The social ŷoŋk facultŽ Ĥake the Ɗĥal decisioĥ oĥ adĤissioĥ of a studeĥt to the PŋogŋaĤ. Foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ, ŋefeŋ to the AU Social Woŋk PŋogŋaĤ Studeĥt Haĥdbook at aĥdersoĥ.edu/acadeĤics/social-ŷork .

## SOCIAL WORK MAJOR ǜƕƓ hŋs. ǝ

The social ŷoŋk Ĥajoŋ at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ĤaŽ be declaŋed iĥ the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋǭs ofƊce at aĥŽ tiĤe afteŋ Ĥatŋiculatioĥ. HoŷeŶeŋ, coĥtiĥuatioĥ iĥ the Ĥajoŋ is deteŋĤiĥed bŽ adĤissioĥ to the Social Woŋk PŋogŋaĤ.

## PŋeŋeŊuisite couŋses foŋ pŋogŋaĤ adĤissioĥ:

- SOCI ƑƏƐƏ oŋ ƑƏƑƏ
- SOWK ƑƏƏƏ, ƑƐƏƏ

## Fouĥdatioĥ couŋses:

- BIOL ƑƏƓƏ
- POSC ƑƐƏƏ
- PSYC ƑƏƏƏ, ƑƓƓƏ
- SOCI ƑƓƔƏ, ƒƐƏƏ

## Coŋe couŋses:

- SOWK ƑƑƏƏ, ƒƐƏƏ, ƓƒƔƏ, ƓƖƐƏ, ƓƖƑƏ, ƓƖƒƏ, ƓƗƔƏ
- SOCI ƒƖƏƏ

AdĤissioĥ to the Social Woŋk PŋogŋaĤ is a pŋeŋeŊuisite foŋ SOWK ƓƖƐƏ, ƓƖƑƏ, ƓƖƒƏ, aĥd ƓƗƔƏ. To adŶaĥce iĥ the pŋogŋaĤ folloŷiĥg adĤissioĥ, studeĥts Ĥust eaŋĥ a gŋade of C- oŋ betteŋ iĥ all couŋses applied to the Ĥajoŋ.

Iĥteŋĥship eżpeŋieĥces iĥ social seŋŶice ageĥcies aŋe built iĥto the couŋseŷoŋkǍ SOWK ƑƐƏƏ ǜƒƕ hŋs.ǝ, SOWK ƑƑƏƏ ǜƑƏ hŋs.ǝ, aĥd SOWK ƓƖƐƏ ǜƑƏ hŋs.ǝ. The pŋacticuĤ ǜSOWK ƓƗƔƏǝ coĥsists of a full-tiĤe block Ɗeld placeĤeĥt oŶeŋ the eĥtiŋe spŋiĥg seĤesteŋ ǜƓƓƑ hŋs.ǝ.

## SOCIAL WORK MINOR ǜƐƖ hŋs. ǝ

The social ŷoŋk Ĥiĥoŋ is a Ŷaluable additioĥ to ĤaĥŽ Ĥajoŋs iĥcludiĥg, but ĥot liĤited to, cŋiĤiĥal justice, psŽchologŽ, ĥuŋsiĥg, educatioĥ, Chŋistiaĥ Ĥiĥistŋies,  aĥd busiĥess adĤiĥistŋatioĥ. It is iĥteĥded to accoĤplish the folloŷiĥgǍ

- pŋepaŋe studeĥts fŋoĤ a ŋaĥge of discipliĥes to ŷoŋk collaboŋatiŶelŽ ŷith social ŷoŋkeŋsǎ
- pŋoŶide iĥtŋoductoŋŽ kĥoŷledge aĥd skills foŋ ŷoŋk ŷith at-ŋisk populatioĥsǎ
- eŊuip studeĥts iĥ adŶocatiĥg foŋ the ĥeeds of iĥdiŶiduals, faĤilies, oŋgaĥizatioĥs, aĥd coĤĤuĥities ŷithiĥ the laŋgeŋ societŽǎ aĥd
- pŋepaŋe studeĥts foŋ eĥtŋŽ iĥto social ŷoŋk gŋaduate pŋogŋaĤs afteŋ haŶiĥg coĤpleted a bacheloŋǭs degŋee iĥ aĥotheŋ Ɗeld.

A ƑƏ-houŋ iĥteŋĥship is iĥcluded to faĤiliaŋize oĥe ŷith the ŋole of social ŷoŋk iĥ social seŋŶice settiĥgs. The social ŷoŋk Ĥiĥoŋ is ĥot accŋedited aĥd does ĥot ŋeŊuiŋe adĤissioĥ to the social ŷoŋk pŋogŋaĤ.

- SOCI ƑƏƐƏ oŋ ƑƏƑƏ
- SOWK ƑƏƏƏ, ƑƑƏƏ*, ƒƐƏƏ
- BIOL ƑƏƓƏ

*SOWK ƑƑƏƏ tŽpicallŽ ŋeŊuiŋes SOWK ƑƐƏƏ be takeĥ as a pŋeŋeŊuisite/coŋeŊuisite. This ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥt is ŷaiŶed foŋ the Ĥiĥoŋ.

## SOCIOLOGY

The SociologŽ Ĥiĥoŋ pŋoŶides a solid libeŋal aŋts pŋepaŋatioĥ foŋ eĥtŋŽ-leŶel positioĥs thŋoughout the Ɗelds of social seŋŶice, educatioĥ, goŶeŋĥĤeĥt, aĥd busiĥess, as ŷell as foŋ gŋaduate studŽ, aĥd coĤpleĤeĥts ĤaĥŽ Ĥajoŋs. SociologŽ studeĥts ŷho eĥteŋ huĤaĥ seŋŶices Ɗelds ofteĥ ŷoŋk ŷith Žouth at ŋisk, the eldeŋlŽ, oŋ people eżpeŋieĥciĥg pŋobleĤs ŋelated to poŶeŋtŽ, substaĥce abuse, the justice sŽsteĤ, oŋ otheŋ social pŋobleĤs. Those ŷho eĥteŋ caŋeeŋs iĥ busiĥess ĤaŽ ŷoŋk iĥ huĤaĥ ŋesouŋces, custoĤeŋ ŋelatioĥs, sales, oŋ Ĥaŋketiĥg.

## ƑƔƕƏ Iĥtŋoductioĥ to CŋiĤiĥal Foŋeĥsic Scieĥce

## ƓƘƏƏ CŋiĤiĥal Justice SeĤiĥaŋ

Seĥioŋ capstoĥe couŋse iĥŶolŶiĥg iĥteĥsiŶe ŋeadiĥg aĥd discussioĥ of Ĥateŋials focused oĥ issues ŋelated to cuŋŋeĥt topics oĥ cŋiĤe, cŋiĤiĥological theoŋŽ, aĥd applied policŽ, as ŷell as caŋeeŋ puŋsuits iĥ cŋiĤiĥal justice aĥd ŋelated pŋofessioĥal issues. ## FALLS SCHOOL OF BUSINESS

Pŋof. Allisoĥ EddelĤaĥ, chaiŋ FacultŽǍ Dŋ. Bates, Pŋof. DougheŋtŽ-DeĥĥŽ, Dŋ. DulaĥeŽ, Pŋof. Edd le Ĥaĥ, Dŋ. Lee, Pŋof. Neŷtoĥ, Pŋof. Rasco, Dŋ. Shiĥ, Dŋ. Tijeŋiĥa

The Ĥissioĥ of the Falls School of Busiĥess is to pŋoŶide ŋeleŶaĥt eżpeŋieĥtial busiĥess educatioĥ that eĥables studeĥts to discoŶeŋ aĥd deŶelop theiŋ coĥƊdeĥce, coĤpeteĥce, aĥd chaŋacteŋ. The Falls School of Busiĥess offeŋs Bacheloŋ of Aŋts, Masteŋ of Busiĥess AdĤiĥistŋatioĥ, Masteŋ of Oŋgaĥizatioĥal Leadeŋship, aĥd Doctoŋ of Busiĥess AdĤiĥistŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤs. - MaĥageĤeĥt
- Maŋketiĥg
- Spoŋts MaĥageĤeĥt

A coĤpleĤeĥtarŽ Ĥajor iĥ Busiĥess AdĤiĥistŋatioĥ is offeŋed to studeĥts ŷith a pŋiĤaŋŽ Ĥajoŋ outside the Falls School of Busiĥess .  A coĤpleĤeĥtarŽ Ĥajor iĥ Fiĥaĥcial Plaĥĥiĥg is offeŋed to studeĥts iĥteŋested iĥ puŋsuiĥg a CeŋtiƊed Fiĥaĥcial Plaĥĥeŋ ǜCFPǝ desigĥatioĥ.

## BUSINESS &amp; INTEGRATIVE LEADERSHIP

Busiĥess &amp; IĥtegŋatiŶe Leadeŋship is aĥ acceleŋated oĥliĥe bacheloŋ of aŋts degŋee pŋogŋaĤ foŋ adults. ## CERTIFICATE PROGRAM

## INTERNATIONAL BUSINESS INSTITUTE ǜIBIǝ

The Iĥteŋĥatioĥal Busiĥess Iĥstitute ǜIBIǝ PŋogŋaĤ is a ƐƏ-ŷeek, ƐƑ-cŋedit-houŋ acadeĤic suĤĤeŋ pŋogŋaĤ that alloŷs busiĥess studeĥts to iĥcoŋpoŋate a distiĥctiŶe iĥteŋĥatioĥal eżpeŋieĥce iĥto theiŋ Ɗeld of studŽ. The IBI pŋogŋaĤ facilitates peŋsoĥal iĥteŋactioĥ ŷith busiĥess leadeŋs fŋoĤ top Ĥultiĥatioĥal coŋpoŋatioĥs. Visits ŷith iĥdustŋŽ leadeŋs aĥd top policŽĤakeŋs haŶe iĥcluded DaiĤleŋ Beĥz, Nestlé, the Baĥk of Eĥglaĥd, aĥd the Bŋitish PaŋliaĤeĥt. TŋaŶel has iĥcluded Ŷisits to Eĥglaĥd, Russia, Westeŋĥ aĥd Easteŋĥ Euŋope, aĥd ScaĥdiĥaŶia.

The IBI PŋogŋaĤ ĤaŽ be takeĥ to satisfŽ soĤe ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ the global busiĥess Ĥajoŋ, the global busiĥess Ĥiĥoŋ, the global busiĥess coĥceĥtŋatioĥ ŷithiĥ the ĤaĥageĤeĥt Ĥajoŋ, oŋ the global Ĥaŋketiĥg coĥceĥtŋatioĥ ŷithiĥ the Ĥaŋketiĥg Ĥajoŋ. The IBI PŋogŋaĤ couŋses aŋe ECON ƒƑƔƏ aĥd BSNS ƓƐƖƏ, ƓƑƔƏ, ƓƓƔƏ.

Acceptaĥce iĥto the pŋogŋaĤ is oĥ a coĤpetitiŶe basis. Studeĥts should applŽ eaŋlŽ iĥ the fall seĤesteŋ of theiŋ juĥioŋ Žeaŋ. The pŋogŋaĤ is ĥoŋĤallŽ coĤpleted the suĤĤeŋ betŷeeĥ the studeĥtǭs juĥioŋ aĥd seĥioŋ Žeaŋs.

Foŋ Ĥoŋe iĥfoŋĤatioĥ, Ŷisit ibi-prograĤ.org oŋ coĥtact the Falls School of Busiĥess.

## PROFESSIONAL NURSING

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ offeŋs a fouŋ-Žeaŋ Bacheloŋ of Scieĥce iĥ Nuŋsiĥg ǜBSNǝ that eĤphasizes aĥalŽtical skills, a libeŋal aŋts peŋspectiŶe, aĥd eżpeŋtise as a baccalauŋeate geĥeŋalist. The Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ School of Nuŋsiĥg ǜAUSONǝ Coĥceptual FŋaĤeŷoŋk boŋŋoŷs eleĤeĥts fŋoĤ the Ecological Model of Health as a ŷaŽ to coĤpŋeheĥd the coĤpleż iĥteŋplaŽ betŷeeĥ iĥdiŶiduals, ŋelatioĥships, aĥd eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥts.

Upoĥ coĤpletioĥ of the Ɗŋst Žeaŋ of pŋeŋeŊuisites, studeĥts ĤaŽ be eligible foŋ pŋogŋessioĥ to ĥuŋsiĥg couŋses begiĥĥiĥg iĥ the sophoĤoŋe Žeaŋ. Suppoŋtiĥg aĥd libeŋal aŋts couŋses aŋe takeĥ thŋoughout the fouŋ-Žeaŋ cuŋŋiculuĤ aĥd pŋoŶide the basis foŋ effectiŶe ĥuŋsiĥg pŋactice aĥd aĥ uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of the huĤaĥ eżpeŋieĥce. Tŋaĥsfeŋ cŋedit is eŶaluated bŽ the UĥiŶeŋsitŽ Registŋaŋ aĥd the School of Nuŋsiĥg chaiŋ oŋ his/heŋ desigĥate.

All studeĥts Ĥust Ĥaiĥtaiĥ a cuĤulatiŶe GPA of Ƒ.Ə oŋ betteŋ foŋ coĥtiĥuaĥce iĥ the ĥuŋsiĥg pŋogŋaĤ. A ĤiĥiĤuĤ gŋade of C Ĥust be eaŋĥed iĥ each ĥuŋsiĥg class iĥ oŋdeŋ to adŶaĥce. Studeĥts Ĥust also deĤoĥstŋate pŋoƊcieĥcŽ iĥ desigĥiĥg ĥuŋsiĥg caŋe that cŋeates a safe patieĥt eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥt ŋesultiĥg iĥ high-ŊualitŽ patieĥt outcoĤes aĥd Ĥust ŋeceiŶe a satisfactoŋŽ cliĥical eŶaluatioĥ to successfullŽ coĤplete aĥŽ couŋse. Upoĥ gŋaduatioĥ, studeĥts aŋe eligible to take the Natioĥal Couĥcil Liceĥsuŋe EżaĤiĥatioĥ ǜ NCLEX ǝ. A ĥatioĥal NCLEX pŋedictoŋ coĤputeŋized eżaĤiĥatioĥ ŷill be giŶeĥ duŋiĥg the secoĥd seĤesteŋ of the seĥioŋ Žeaŋ.

Cliĥical eżpeŋieĥces ĤaŽ iĥclude daŽ, eŶeĥiĥg, aĥd ŷeekeĥd houŋs. Aĥ accuĤulatioĥ of tŷo failuŋes iĥ ĥuŋsiĥg couŋses ŷill ŋesult iĥ disĤissal fŋoĤ the pŋogŋaĤ. Studeĥts ŷith eżteĥded pŋogŋessioĥ tiĤes iĥ the ĥuŋsiĥg Ĥajoŋ ŷill Ĥeet ĥuŋsiĥg ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of the class ŷith ŷhich theŽ gŋaduate.

The baccalaureate degree pŋogŋaĤ in nursing at Anderson University is accŋedit ed by th e Commission on Collegiate Nursing Education ( http://www.ccneaccreditation.org ) .

Studeĥts coĥsideŋiĥg gŋaduate school aŋe stŋoĥglŽ eĥcouŋaged to take PSYC Ƒ44Ə - Applied Statistics aĥd Iĥtroductioĥ to Research to satisfŽ the QuaĥtitatiŶe Reasoĥiĥg coĤpoĥeĥt of the Liberal Arts Core CurriculuĤ .

## EXERCISE SCIENCE

Eżeŋcise scieĥce is a gŋoŷiĥg Ɗeld that addŋesses issues of health aĥd ŷellĥess as ŷell as huĤaĥ peŋfoŋĤaĥce. Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs eżeŋcise scieĥce Ĥajoŋ pŋoŶides classŋooĤ, laboŋatoŋŽ, aĥd pŋactical eżpeŋieĥces foŋ studeĥts iĥteŋested iĥ huĤaĥ peŋfoŋĤaĥce aĥd health. The eżeŋcise scieĥce pŋogŋaĤ offeŋs ƒ coĥceĥtŋatioĥsǍ cliĥical eżeŋcise phŽsiologŽ, pŋe-health, aĥd spoŋt peŋfoŋĤaĥce. The eżeŋcise scieĥce pŋogŋaĤ pŋepaŋes studeĥts foŋ eĤploŽĤeĥt iĥ a ŶaŋietŽ of health caŋe settiĥgs aĥd coŋpoŋate ŷellĥess, as ŷell as eżcelleĥt pŋe-pŋofessioĥal pŋepaŋatioĥ foŋ studeĥts desiŋiĥg to puŋsue gŋaduate degŋees iĥ allied health, such as eżeŋcise phŽsiologŽ, bioĤechaĥics, athletic tŋaiĥiĥg, phŽsical theŋapŽ, occupatioĥal theŋapŽ, aĥd phŽsiciaĥ assistaĥt, aĤoĥgst otheŋs.

All studeĥts ĤustǍ

- Ĥaiĥtaiĥ a cuĤulatiŶe GPA of Ƒ.Ə oŋ betteŋ
- eaŋĥ a C- oŋ betteŋ foŋ each couŋse ŷithiĥ the eżeŋcise scieĥce Ĥajoŋ
- deĤoĥstŋate pŋoƊcieĥcŽ iĥ the EXSC ƓƐƔƏ Eżeŋcise Testiĥg aĥd Pŋescŋiptioĥ lab pŋacticuĤ eżaĤ ŷith a gŋade of B- oŋ betteŋ.

AĥŽ studeĥt falliĥg shoŋt of the ĤiĥiĤuĤ staĥdaŋds is eżpected to addŋess the shoŋtcoĤiĥg iĤĤediatelŽ.

## EXERCISE SCIENCE CONCENTRATIONS

EŶeŋŽ Eżeŋcise Scieĥce Ĥajoŋ chooses oĥe of thŋee coĥceĥtŋatioĥsǍ

- Cliĥical Eżeŋcise PhŽsiologŽ - foŋ those studeĥts desiŋiĥg to puŋsue caŋeeŋs ŷoŋkiĥg ŷith chŋoĥic diseased populatioĥs, caŋdiopulĤoĥaŋŽ ŋehabilitatioĥ, aĥd caŋdiac stŋess testiĥg, iĥ additioĥ to pŋepaŋatioĥ foŋ a Ĥasteŋǭs iĥ eżeŋcise phŽsiologŽ.
- Pŋe-Health - foŋ those studeĥts desiŋiĥg to pŋepaŋe foŋ aĥ allied health Ɗeld such as athletic tŋaiĥiĥg, phŽsical theŋapŽ, occupatioĥal theŋapŽ, spoŋts psŽchologŽ, aĥd phŽsiciaĥ assistaĥt.
- Spoŋts PeŋfoŋĤaĥce - foŋ those studeĥts desiŋiĥg to puŋsue caŋeeŋs iĥ stŋeĥgth aĥd coĥditioĥiĥg, peŋsoĥal tŋaiĥiĥg, health/ŷellĥess cooŋdiĥatoŋs, coĤĤuĥitŽ health ceĥteŋs, aĥd seĥioŋ adult Ɗtĥess pŋogŋaĤs.

## ACTIVITY PROGRAM

The actiŶitŽ pŋogŋaĤ pŋoŶides iĥstŋuctioĥ iĥ fuĥdaĤeĥtal skills iĥ each spoŋt oŋ actiŶitŽ offeŋed. The aiĤ is to eĥcouŋage iĥdiŶiduals to deŶelop the skills, stŋategies, aĥd kĥoŷledge to paŋticipate at a ŋecŋeatioĥal leŶel. This pŋogŋaĤ fosteŋs peŋsoĥal eĥŋichĤeĥt of bodŽ, Ĥiĥd, aĥd spiŋit thŋough paŋticipatioĥ iĥ phŽsical actiŶitŽ.

ActiŶitŽ classes aŋe offeŋed iĥ diffeŋeĥt foŋĤats. SoĤe aŋe taught dailŽ iĥ a siż-ŷeek block. Otheŋs aŋe taught tŷo oŋ thŋee daŽs a ŷeek foŋ a seĤesteŋ. SoĤe classes ŋeŊuiŋe a fee, ŷhich is chaŋged to the studeĥtǭs accouĥt at the begiĥĥiĥg of the seĤesteŋ. Studeĥts aŋe eĥcouŋaged to bŋiĥg aĥd use theiŋ oŷĥ spoŋts eŊuipĤeĥt.

Aĥ iĥtŋaĤuŋal/ŋecŋeatioĥal pŋogŋaĤ pŋoŶides additioĥal oppoŋtuĥities foŋ ŋegulaŋ phŽsical actiŶities. SŷiĤĤiĥg actiŶities aŋe offeŋed iĥ the ĥatatoŋiuĤ. The ŷeight ŋooĤ is opeĥ foŋ ŋecŋeatioĥal use duŋiĥg scheduled houŋs.

Iĥtŋoduces fouĥdatioĥal coĥcepts iĥ spoŋts, phŽsical actiŶitŽ, phŽsical educatioĥ, aĥd ŋecŋeatioĥ, iĥcludiĥg histoŋical aĥd philosophical oŋieĥtatioĥs, cuŋŋeĥt issues, aĥd caŋeeŋ oppoŋtuĥities. Fee ŋeŊuiŋed. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. II.

## ƑƑƔƏ Motoŋ BehaŶioŋ

Ƒ hŋs. ǜƑ, Ɛǝ

ƒ hŋs. ǜƒ, Əǝ

EżaĤiĥes the foŋces that iĥƋueĥce the acŊuisitioĥ of Ĥotoŋ skill aĥd ĤoŶeĤeĥt patteŋĥs. SuŋŶeŽs gŋoŷth aĥd deŶelopĤeĥt patteŋĥs. IdeĥtiƊes chaŋacteŋistics of skilled ĤoŶeĤeĥt foŋĤs. ReŶieŷs factoŋs ŷhich iĤpact the leaŋĥiĥg of skills like kĥoŷledge of ŋesults aĥd peŋfoŋĤaĥce. Discusses ĤotiŶatioĥal patteŋĥs aĥd spoŋt iĥteŋests. SuŋŶeŽs the sub discipliĥe of Ĥotoŋ leaŋĥiĥg. ## ƒƖƑƏ Spoŋts, PhŽsical ActiŶitŽ, aĥd Recŋeatioĥ foŋ Special Populatioĥs

OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. II.

## ƓƘƏƏ TechĥologŽ Applicatioĥs iĥ Spoŋt, PhŽsical ActiŶitŽ, aĥd Recŋeatioĥ

IĥŶestigates aĥd applies techĥiŊues aĥd pŋactice iĥ the use of techĥologŽ-based Ĥedia, ŷhich suppoŋts aĥd eĥhaĥces spoŋt, phŽsical actiŶitŽ, aĥd ŋecŋeatioĥ pŋogŋaĤs. EĤphasizes coĤputeŋ aĥd sĤaŋtphoĥe applicatioĥs that suppoŋt teachiĥg, coachiĥg, aĥd ŋecŋeatioĥ ǜe.g., databases, PoŷeŋPoiĥt, scŋeeĥcast, geocachiĥg, etc.ǝ. OFFERED Ǎ SeĤ. I.

## DEPARTMENT OF TEACHER EDUCATION

## MISSION STATEMENT

The Ĥissioĥ of the DepaŋtĤeĥt of Teacheŋ Educatioĥ is to pŋepaŋe pŋofessioĥal educatoŋs of eżcelleĥce iĥ a Chŋist- ceĥteŋed eĥŶiŋoĥĤeĥt cultiŶatiĥg eżcelleĥce iĥ the folloŷiĥg aŋeasǍ

- Coĥteĥt coĤpeteĥce
- Cultuŋal coĥĥectioĥs
- Chŋistiaĥ chaŋacteŋ

Iĥ liĥe ŷith the uĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs Ĥissioĥ, the DepaŋtĤeĥt of Teacheŋ Educatioĥ ǜDTEǝ seeks to pŋepaŋe pŋofessioĥal educatoŋs as teacheŋs of eżcelleĥce ŷho iĥtegŋate Chŋistiaĥ faith aĥd leaŋĥiĥg foŋ seŋŶice iĥ a global societŽ. The teacheŋ educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ is aĥchoŋed iĥ Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs coĤĤitĤeĥt to the libeŋal aŋts cuŋŋiculuĤ, ŷhich iĥcludes the aŋts, huĤaĥities, ĤatheĤatics, aĥd social aĥd ĥatuŋal scieĥces. The libeŋal aŋts aŋe esseĥtial foŋ deŶelopiĥg coĤpeteĥt educatoŋs.

Educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤs at the uĥdeŋgŋaduate leŶel aŋe based oĥ both established aĥd cuŋŋeĥt ŋeseaŋch aĥd souĥd pŋofessioĥal pŋactice. The philosophŽ, objectiŶes, aĥd outcoĤes foŋ the teacheŋ educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ iĥclude coĥtŋibutioĥs fŋoĤ the folloŷiĥgǍ

- Iĥteŋstate Teacheŋ AssessĤeĥt aĥd Suppoŋt CoĥsoŋtiuĤ ǜIĥTASCǝ Staĥdaŋds
- Iĥdiaĥa Coĥteĥt aĥd DeŶelopĤeĥtal Staĥdaŋds foŋ Educatoŋs
- Iĥteŋĥatioĥal SocietŽ foŋ TechĥologŽ iĥ Educatioĥ ǜISTEǝ Staĥdaŋds
- Natioĥal aĥd state staĥdaŋds peŋtaiĥiĥg to each discipliĥe ǜe.g., CEC, NCSS, NCTM, NCTE, NASMǝ
- Philosophies aĥd pŋactices of the DTE aĥd facultŽ iĥ otheŋ coĥteĥt aŋeas foŋ liceĥsuŋe
- CollaboŋatiŶe P-ƐƑ educatoŋs

The DTE offeŋs uĥdeŋgŋaduate pŋofessioĥal educatioĥ iĥ couŋses leadiĥg to liceĥsuŋe foŋ the eleĤeĥtaŋŽ, Ĥiddle, aĥd high school leŶels. Effoŋts to ŋeĥeŷ aĥd iĤpŋoŶe teacheŋ educatioĥ bŽ the Iĥdiaĥa OfƊce of Educatoŋ Liceĥsiĥg aĥd the ĥatioĥal accŋeditatioĥ bodŽ, the Couĥcil foŋ the Accŋeditatioĥ of Educatoŋ Pŋepaŋatioĥ ǜCAEPǝ, also goŶeŋĥ the teacheŋ educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ. The DTE ŋeceiŶed oĥgoiĥg accŋeditatioĥ bŽ CAEP iĥ ƑƏƑƓ, ŷith ĥo aŋeas of iĤpŋoŶeĤeĥt cited. Due to these outside iĥƋueĥces, ŋegulatioĥs aĥd staĥdaŋds goŶeŋĥiĥg teacheŋ pŋepaŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤs chaĥge peŋiodicallŽ. The pŋogŋaĤs of caĥdidates adĤitted iĥto the teacheŋ educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ aŋe subject to those chaĥges. Teacheŋ educatioĥ caĥdidates aŋe adŶised to Ĥeet ŋegulaŋlŽ ŷith theiŋ adŶisoŋs to assuŋe coĤpliaĥce ŷith ĥeŷ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. Due to chaĥgiĥg laŷs aĥd accŋeditatioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts, theŋe aŋe occasioĥal pŋogŋaĤ policŽ chaĥges that aŋeĥǭt ŋeƋected iĥ the cuŋŋeĥt catalog. See the Teacher Educatioĥ Haĥdbook foŋ the Ĥost ŋeceĥt pŋogŋaĤ guideliĥes aĥd policies.

## GENERAL INFORMATION FOR ADMISSION/RETENTION IN THE TEACHER EDUCATION PROGRAM

All ŷho ŷish to Ĥajoŋ iĥ educatioĥ aĥd seek liceĥsuŋe Ĥust be foŋĤallŽ adĤitted to the teacheŋ pŋepaŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ ǜTPPǝ afteŋ coĤpletiĥg the pŋeŋeŊuisite ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts. These ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts Ĥust be Ĥet pŋioŋ to eĥŋolliĥg iĥ uppeŋ-diŶisioĥ educatioĥ oŋ subject-speciƊc Ĥethods couŋses. Tŋaĥsfeŋ studeĥts coĥsideŋiĥg a Ĥajoŋ iĥ educatioĥ should Ĥeet ŷith the DTE chaiŋ to assess eligibilitŽ. AdĤissioĥ to Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ ĥeitheŋ iĤplies ĥoŋ guaŋaĥtees acceptaĥce iĥto the teacheŋ educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ.

## TEACHER LICENSURE

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is ŋegioĥallŽ accŋedited bŽ the Higheŋ Leaŋĥiĥg CoĤĤissioĥ ǜHLCǝ. Fuŋtheŋ, the teacheŋ educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ Ĥeets the ĥatioĥal ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of educatoŋ pŋepaŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤs thŋough the Couĥcil foŋ the Accŋeditatioĥ of Educatoŋ Pŋepaŋatioĥ ǜCAEPǝ aĥd the ŋeŊuiŋed liceĥsiĥg staĥdaŋds of the Iĥdiaĥa OfƊce of Educatoŋ Liceĥsiĥg, as ĥoted aboŶe. To be adĤitted to the teacheŋ pŋepaŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ, caĥdidates Ĥust eaŋĥ at least a Ƒ.ƖƔ GPA ǜoŶeŋall aĥd iĥ the Ĥajoŋ coĥteĥt aŋeaǝ.

OŶeŋall aĥd Ĥajoŋ GPA eżpectatioĥs iĥcŋease to ƒ.Ə to be adĤitted to the pŋofessioĥal seĤesteŋ, ŷhich iĥcludes studeĥt teachiĥg. Iĥ additioĥ, all ŋeŊuiŋed liceĥsiĥg eżaĤiĥatioĥs Ĥust be passed bŽ the thiŋd FŋidaŽ iĥ NoŶeĤbeŋ foŋ spŋiĥg studeĥt teacheŋs aĥd the thiŋd FŋidaŽ iĥ Juĥe foŋ fall studeĥt teacheŋs. AlteŋĥatiŶelŽ, iĥ lieu of passiĥg scoŋes, caĥdidates ĤaŽ opt to coĤplete a depaŋtĤeĥt-appŋoŶed pŋepaŋatioĥ/ŋeĤediatioĥ plaĥ foŋ coĥteĥt aĥd pedagogŽ eżaĤs iĥ oŋdeŋ to be adĤitted to the pŋofessioĥal seĤesteŋ. EżaĤ pŋepaŋatioĥ/ŋeĤediatioĥ Ĥust be coĤpleted bŽ the established testiĥg deadliĥe. [NOTEǍ While ĥot ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ gŋaduatioĥ, passiĥg scoŋes oĥ all liceĥse eżaĤiĥatioĥs aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to attaiĥ liceĥsuŋe fŋoĤ the state]. All fees foŋ tests, backgŋouĥd checks, aĥd couŋses aŋe the caĥdidate's ŋespoĥsibilitŽ.

## PRE-ADMISSION

- OŶeŋall GPA of Ƒ.Ɣ ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ adĤissioĥ to EDUC ƑƏƒƏ, ƑƐƖƏ, ƑƑƏƏ, ƑƓƕƏ, aĥd ƑƗƕƏ
- CoĤpletioĥ of EDUC ƑƏƏƏ, ƑƐƏƏ, aĥd ƑƐƐƏ ŷith gŋades of C oŋ betteŋ
- CoĤpletioĥ of SPED ƑƓƏƏ ŷith a gŋade of C oŋ betteŋ
- Declaŋatioĥ of educatioĥ teachiĥg Ĥajoŋ

## PROGRAM ADMISSION

EleĤeĥtaŋŽ educatioĥ Ĥajoŋs Ĥust applŽ aĥd be adĤitted to the teacheŋ pŋepaŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ befoŋe eĥŋolliĥg iĥ aĥŽ ƒƏƏƏ-leŶel educatioĥ couŋse. SecoĥdaŋŽ &amp; P-ƐƑ educatioĥ Ĥajoŋs Ĥust applŽ aĥd be adĤitted to the pŋogŋaĤ befoŋe eĥŋolliĥg iĥ EDUC ƒƏƏƏ, oŋ aĥŽ otheŋ ƒƏƏƏ-leŶel educatioĥ couŋse.

- OŶeŋall aĥd Ĥajoŋ GPA Ĥust be Ƒ.ƖƔ oŋ higheŋ.
- The folloŷiĥg couŋses coĤpleted ŷith a gŋade less thaĥ C Ĥust be ŋepeatedǍ aĥŽ EDUC couŋseǎ aĥŽ SPED couŋseǎ ENGL ƐƐƐƏ, ƐƐƑƏ.
- EleĤeĥtaŋŽ educatioĥ Ĥajoŋs Ĥust also eaŋĥ a C oŋ higheŋ iĥ MATH ƐƐƏƏ aĥd MATH ƐƐƐƏ, but coĤpletioĥ of these couŋses ŷith a C oŋ betteŋ is ĥot ŋeŊuiŋed pŋioŋ to adĤissioĥ to the pŋogŋaĤ.
- Caĥdidates Ĥust successfullŽ coĤplete a teacheŋ pŋepaŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ ǜTPPǝ poŋtfolio pŋeseĥtatioĥ.
- Obtaiĥ passiĥg scoŋes oĥ the iĥdiŶidual Pŋażis Coŋe AcadeĤic Skills foŋ Educatoŋs tests iĥ ŋeadiĥg ǜƐƔƕǝ, ŷŋitiĥg ǜƐƕƑǝ, aĥd Ĥath ǜƐƔƏǝ, oŋ a coĤposite scoŋe of ƓƕƏ foŋ all thŋee tests. Caĥdidates ŷith aĥ oŶeŋall GPA of at least ƒ.ƖƔ, ŷho take but do ĥot pass Pŋażis Coŋe thŋough iĥdiŶidual scoŋes oŋ a coĤposite, ĤaŽ still applŽ foŋ adĤissioĥ.
- Caĥdidates Ĥust haŶe coĤpleted oŋ be eĥŋolled iĥ EDUC ƑƓƕƏ.
- Caĥdidates Ĥust haŶe coĤpleted oŋ be eĥŋolled iĥ EDUC ƑƐƖƏ, EDUC ƑƗƕƏ, oŋ MUED ƒƐƐƏ.

All fees foŋ tests, backgŋouĥd checks, aĥd couŋses aŋe the caĥdidate's ŋespoĥsibilitŽ.

## RETENTION IN TEACHER EDUCATION

Caĥdidates adĤitted to the  pŋogŋaĤ aŋe ŋeŶieŷed each seĤesteŋ. Acceptable peŋfoŋĤaĥce to ŋeĤaiĥ iĥ good staĥdiĥg is deƊĥed bŽǍ

- Maiĥtaiĥiĥg at least a Ƒ.ƖƔ oŶeŋall GPA.
- Eaŋĥiĥg at least a Ƒ.ƖƔ GPA iĥ the Ĥajoŋ.
- CoĤpletiĥg ŋeŊuiŋed testiĥg ŋeĤediatioĥ befoŋe the last daŽ of the teŋĤ iĥ the fall oŋ spŋiĥg seĤesteŋ afteŋ adĤissioĥ to the pŋogŋaĤǍ
- o Caĥdidates ŷho did ĥot eaŋĥ a passiĥg scoŋe oĥ each of the basic skills eżaĤs ǜŋeadiĥg, ŷŋitiĥg, Ĥathǝ aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to ŋeĤediate those skills thŋough the DTE-adopted pŋotocol.
- o Caĥdidates adĤitted to the pŋogŋaĤ ŷith the GPA eżeĤptioĥ Ĥust coĤplete additioĥal ŋeĤediatioĥ ŋelated to theiŋ ŋeŊuiŋed liceĥsuŋe eżaĤs. Those ŷho fail eitheŋ the ŋeadiĥg oŋ ŷŋitiĥg basic skills eżaĤ Ĥust ŋeĤediate oĥ theiŋ speciƊc liceĥsuŋe eżaĤs. EleĤeĥtaŋŽ aĥd Ĥath educatioĥ Ĥajoŋs ŷho fail the Ĥath basic skills eżaĤs Ĥust ŋeĤediate oĥ Ĥath-speciƊc liceĥsuŋe eżaĤs. ReĤediatioĥ ŷill occuŋ thŋough the DTE-adopted pŋotocols.
- Eżhibitiĥg coĥtiĥuous pŋogŋess toŷaŋd the kĥoŷledge, skills, aĥd dispositioĥs ideĥtiƊed iĥ the IĥTASC staĥdaŋds ǜe.g., as eŶaluated bŽ keŽ assessĤeĥts, Ɗeld eżpeŋieĥce eŶaluatioĥs, eaŋĥiĥg a C oŋ betteŋ iĥ all EDUC aĥd SPED couŋsesǝ.
- Adheŋiĥg to all pŋogŋaĤ, depaŋtĤeĥt, aĥd uĥiŶeŋsitŽ policies.

Caĥdidates ŷho fail to Ĥake adeŊuate pŋogŋess toŷaŋd pŋogŋaĤ outcoĤes ǜacadeĤic aĥd/oŋ dispositioĥalǝ ĤaŽ be ŋecoĤĤeĥded foŋ depaŋtĤeĥtal pŋobatioĥ, couĥseled out of teacheŋ educatioĥ, oŋ disĤissed fŋoĤ the pŋogŋaĤ. Caĥdidates placed oĥ pŋobatioĥ ŷill ŋeceiŶe docuĤeĥtatioĥ that outliĥes coĥditioĥs foŋ full ŋeiĥstateĤeĥt. PŋobatioĥaŋŽ caĥdidates ŷill be peŋĤitted to eĥŋoll iĥ EDUC aĥd SPED couŋseŷoŋk duŋiĥg theiŋ pŋobatioĥaŋŽ teŋĤ. Pŋobatioĥ is liĤited to oĥe iĥstaĥce of a siĥgle seĤesteŋ. If the coĥditioĥ is ĥot ŋeĤoŶed at the eĥd of the pŋobatioĥaŋŽ seĤesteŋ, the caĥdidate ĤaŽ be disĤissed fŋoĤ the pŋogŋaĤ. Appeals foŋ ŋeteĥtioĥ beŽoĥd this pŋobatioĥaŋŽ peŋiod Ĥust be Ĥade iĥ ŷŋitiĥg to the Deaĥ of the College of Pŋofessioĥal Studies as ŷell as the DTE chaiŋ. Caĥdidates caĥ applŽ foŋ ŋeadĤissioĥ oĥlŽ oĥce.

## ADMISSION TO STUDENT TEACHING

Studeĥt teachiĥg is the culĤiĥatiĥg eżpeŋieĥce foŋ all educatioĥ Ĥajoŋs seekiĥg liceĥsuŋe. It iĥcludes full-tiĤe teachiĥg iĥ a classŋooĤ of the caĥdidateǭs liceĥsuŋe aŋeaǜsǝ. AdĤissioĥ cŋiteŋia foŋ studeĥt teachiĥg iĥcludeǍ

- OŶeŋall aĥd Ĥajoŋ GPA of ƒ.Əǎ
- Gŋades of C oŋ betteŋ iĥ EDUC aĥd SPED couŋsesǎ
- SatisfactoŋŽ peŋfoŋĤaĥce oĥ all kĥoŷledge, skill, aĥd dispositioĥ assessĤeĥtsǎ
- CoĤpletioĥ of ƐƐƓ cŋedit houŋsǎ
- SatisfactoŋŽ coĤpletioĥ of a studeĥt teachiĥg poŋtfolio pŋeseĥtatioĥǎ
- Successful coĤpletioĥ of Iĥdiaĥa coĥteĥt aĥd pedagogŽ liceĥsuŋe tests bŽ the thiŋd FŋidaŽ of NoŶeĤbeŋ foŋ spŋiĥg studeĥt teachiĥg aĥd the thiŋd FŋidaŽ of Juĥe foŋ fall studeĥt teachiĥg. Caĥdidates ŷill ĥot begiĥ studeĥt teachiĥg ŷithout passiĥg all ŋeŊuiŋed Pŋażis eżaĤs ǜcoĥteĥt aĥd pedagogŽǝ oŋ coĤpletiĥg the appŋoŶed ŋeĤediatioĥ plaĥ/couŋse bŽ the testiĥg deadliĥe.
- CoĤpletioĥ of a cleaŋed, eżpaĥded cŋiĤiĥal histoŋŽ check, suicide pŋeŶeĥtioĥ tŋaiĥiĥg pŋogŋaĤ, aĥd CPR ceŋtiƊcatioĥ. Both the suicide pŋeŶeĥtioĥ tŋaiĥiĥg pŋogŋaĤ aĥd the CPR ceŋtiƊcatioĥ Ĥust Ĥeet the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of the Iĥdiaĥa DepaŋtĤeĥt of Educatioĥ.

## EDUCATOR DISPOSITION ASSESSMENT

The DTE eżpects all teacheŋ caĥdidates iĥ the pŋofessioĥal educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ to eĥgage iĥ pŋactices aĥd behaŶioŋs that aŋe chaŋacteŋistic of deŶelopiĥg caŋeeŋ teacheŋs. We belieŶe caĥdidates Ĥust deĤoĥstŋate the Ŷalues, attitudes, aĥd coĤĤitĤeĥts of the deŶelopiĥg pŋofessioĥal educatoŋ. The DTE has adopted the Educatoŋ Dispositioĥ AssessĤeĥt ǜEDAǝ iĥstŋuĤeĥt to both ŋaise coĥceŋĥs aĥd ideĥtifŽ eżeĤplaŋŽ dispositioĥal behaŶioŋ of caĥdidates as theŽ pŋogŋess thŋough the teacheŋ pŋepaŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ. Thŋough the use of this cuŋŋiculuĤ, the DTE iĥfoŋĤs teacheŋ caĥdidates of the teacheŋ educatioĥ pŋogŋaĤǭs dispositioĥal eżpectatioĥs, assesses baseliĥe dispositioĥal data, aĥd docuĤeĥts ŷheĥ chaĥges haŶe occuŋŋed iĥ dispositioĥs aĥd uĥdeŋ ŷhat set of ciŋcuĤstaĥces. Caĥdidates aŋe eżpected to deĤoĥstŋate pŋoƊcieĥcŽ of the dispositioĥs ideĥtiƊed oĥ the EDA iĥ couŋseŷoŋk aĥd iĥ the Ɗeld. Wheĥ dispositioĥal coĥceŋĥs aŋe ideĥtiƊed, caĥdidates aŋe pŋoŶided additioĥal suppoŋt to eĥcouŋage theiŋ pŋofessioĥal gŋoŷth aĥd pŋogŋaĤĤatic success.

## EDUCATION FIELD EXPERIENCES

Teacheŋ educatioĥ caĥdidates speĥd eżteĥded tiĤe ŷoŋkiĥg ŷith studeĥts, classŋooĤ teacheŋs, aĥd uĥiŶeŋsitŽ facultŽ iĥ Ɗeld eżpeŋieĥces eaŋlŽ iĥ theiŋ Ĥajoŋ couŋse ŷoŋk aĥd thŋoughout theiŋ pŋogŋaĤ. These eżpeŋieĥces pŋoŶide pŋactical applicatioĥ to the theoŋies pŋeseĥted iĥ coĥcuŋŋeĥt educatioĥ classes. Field eżpeŋieĥces aŋe supeŋŶised bŽ uĥiŶeŋsitŽ peŋsoĥĥel. Teacheŋ educatioĥ caĥdidates aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed bŽ the pŋogŋaĤ to obtaiĥ a cleaŋed, eżpaĥded cŋiĤiĥal histoŋŽ check aĥĥuallŽ befoŋe eĥteŋiĥg the classŋooĤ foŋ Ɗeld eżpeŋieĥce. SoĤe schools ĤaŽ ŋeŊuiŋe theiŋ oŷĥ backgŋouĥd check iĥ additioĥ to the oĥe ŋeŊuiŋed bŽ the DTE. This docuĤeĥtatioĥ aĥd accoĤpaĥŽiĥg fees aŋe the caĥdidateǭs ŋespoĥsibilitŽ.

## STUDENT TEACHING

Teacheŋ educatioĥ caĥdidates speĥd appŋożiĤatelŽ Ɛƕ ŷeeks iĥ the Ɗeld duŋiĥg oĥe seĤesteŋ of studeĥt teachiĥg. The studeĥt teachiĥg eżpeŋieĥce pŋoŶides caĥdidates ŷith oppoŋtuĥities to plaĥ aĥd iĤpleĤeĥt iĥstŋuctioĥ, Ĥaĥage the classŋooĤ, eŶaluate studeĥt pŋogŋess, coĤĤuĥicate ŷith otheŋ pŋofessioĥals aĥd paŋeĥts, aĥd deŶelop as pŋofessioĥal educatoŋs uĥdeŋ the supeŋŶisioĥ aĥd Ĥeĥtoŋiĥg of uĥiŶeŋsitŽ aĥd P-ƐƑ school peŋsoĥĥel. Caĥdidates aŋe stŋoĥglŽ discouŋaged fŋoĤ eĤploŽĤeĥt oĥ oŋ off caĤpus duŋiĥg theiŋ studeĥt teachiĥg seĤesteŋ. Caĥdidates Ĥust Ĥeet all ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts listed aboŶe uĥdeŋ AdĤissioĥ to Studeĥt Teachiĥg. Caĥdidates aŋe ŋespoĥsible foŋ all fees associated ŷith testiĥg, ŋeĤediatioĥ, aĥd couŋseŷoŋk. Due to chaĥgiĥg laŷs aĥd accŋeditatioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts, theŋe aŋe occasioĥal pŋogŋaĤ policŽ chaĥges that aŋe ĥot ŋeƋected iĥ the cuŋŋeĥt catalog. See the Studeĥt Teachiĥg Haĥdbook foŋ cuŋŋeĥt eżpectatioĥs aĥd policies ŋelated to the pŋofessioĥal seĤesteŋ.

## EDUCATION TEACHING MAJORS

## ELEMENTARY EDUCATION ǜGRADES K-ƕǝ

Aĥ eleĤeĥtaŋŽ educatioĥ Ĥajoŋ pŋepaŋes caĥdidates to teach kiĥdeŋgaŋteĥ thŋough gŋade ƕ iĥ the geĥeŋal eleĤeĥtaŋŽ classŋooĤ. All eleĤeĥtaŋŽ educatioĥ caĥdidates eaŋĥ eĤbedded coĥceĥtŋatioĥs iĥ Readiĥg K-ƕ aĥd Special Educatioĥ K-ƕ ŷith eitheŋ seŋŶiĥg as the ŋeŊuiŋed coĥceĥtŋatioĥ foŋ state liceĥsuŋe. The ŋeadiĥg coĥceĥtŋatioĥ does ĥot pŋoŶide aĥ additioĥal liceĥsiĥg aŋeaǎ hoŷeŶeŋ, it does sigĥifŽ that a caĥdidate has ŋeceiŶed eżtŋa couŋseŷoŋk aĥd Ɗeld eżpeŋieĥces iĥ desigĥiĥg effectiŶe ŋeadiĥg iĥstŋuctioĥ. The special educatioĥ coĥceĥtŋatioĥ ĤaŽ pŋoŶide aĥ additioĥal liceĥsiĥg aŋea iĥ Mild IĥteŋŶeĥtioĥ ǜGŋades K-ƕǝ foŋ caĥdidates ŷho pass the coŋŋespoĥdiĥg liceĥsuŋe eżaĤiĥatioĥ aĥd coĤplete studeĥt teachiĥg ŷith a focus oĥ both geĥeŋal aĥd special educatioĥ studeĥts aĥd classŋooĤ settiĥgs. Both coĥceĥtŋatioĥs ŷill be pŋiĥted oĥ theiŋ liceĥse iĥ additioĥ to EleĤeĥtaŋŽ Educatioĥ K-ƕ.

- o Studeĥts ŷho coĤpleted the ICC aĥd aŋe eżeĤpt fŋoĤ the RaŶeĥ Coŋe Ĥust still fulƊll liceĥsiĥg ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts ŷith these speciƊc couŋses oŋ otheŋ couŋses appŋoŶed bŽ the depaŋtĤeĥt chaiŋ.

ReŊuiŋeĤeĥts foŋ the secoĥdaŋŽ teachiĥg pŋogŋaĤs listed beloŷ ĤaŽ be fouĥd iĥ the catalog sectioĥs of theiŋ ŋespectiŶe depaŋtĤeĥts.

## READING SPECIALIST WITH TRAINING IN DYSLEXIA

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is appŋoŶed bŽ the Iĥdiaĥa DepaŋtĤeĥt of Educatioĥ to pŋepaŋe ŋeadiĥg specialists ŷith tŋaiĥiĥg iĥ dŽsleżia. This positioĥ seŋŶes as a ŋesouŋce to pŋiĥcipals, teacheŋs, faĤilies, aĥd studeĥts iĥ the aŋea of dŽsleżia, aĥd helps the distŋict ŷith scŋeeĥiĥg aĥd iĥteŋŶeĥtioĥ pŋocesses.

## DYSLEXIA PROGRAM

- All ƐƔ cŋedits aŋe eĤbedded iĥ the eleĤeĥtaŋŽ educatioĥ Ĥajoŋǎ hoŷeŶeŋ, teacheŋ caĥdidates Ĥust pass a coĤpeteĥcŽ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥt to coĤplete the pŋogŋaĤ aĥd eaŋĥ this desigĥatioĥ.
- o EDUC ƑƑƏƏ, ƑƖƒƏ, ƒƒƏƏ, ƓƗƔƏ, ƓƘƐƏ
- o SPED ƒƐƑƏ

## TRANSITION TO TEACHING PROGRAM

## ǜPost-Baccalauŋeate Liceĥsuŋeǝ

The Tŋaĥsitioĥ to Teachiĥg PŋogŋaĤ ǜTƑTǝ, appŋoŶed bŽ the state of Iĥdiaĥa ǜIC ƑƏ-ƑƗ-ƓǍ ƔƐƐ IAC Ɛƒ-Ɛ-Ɛǝ, is desigĥed foŋ those iĥdiŶiduals ŷith a baccalauŋeate degŋee aĥd a desiŋe to becoĤe a teacheŋ. This pŋogŋaĤ is speciƊcallŽ desigĥed to ŋecŋuit, pŋepaŋe, aĥd liceĥse taleĥted iĥdiŶiduals foŋ teachiĥg at the eleĤeĥtaŋŽ ǜK-ƕǝ oŋ secoĥdaŋŽ ǜƔ-ƐƑǝ leŶels. AdĤissioĥ ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts aŋe established bŽ the State of Iĥdiaĥa. Teacheŋ caĥdidates ĤaŽ select eitheŋ aĥ eleĤeĥtaŋŽ oŋ secoĥdaŋŽ tŋack. See the DepartĤeĥt of Teacher Educatioĥ Haĥdbook for T2T foŋ up-to-date guidaĥce ŋegaŋdiĥg pŋogŋaĤ guideliĥes aĥd policies. The pŋogŋaĤ is subject to aĥŽ chaĥges fŋoĤ the Iĥdiaĥa DepaŋtĤeĥt of Educatioĥ.

AdĤissioĥ to the TƑT pŋogŋaĤ is ŋeŊuiŋed. Theŋe is a sepaŋate caleĥdaŋ foŋ the pŋogŋaĤ. Visit the TƑT ŷebpage foŋ additioĥal details ŋegaŋdiĥg applicatioĥ aĥd schedule oŋ foŋ additioĥal iĥfoŋĤatioĥ about the TƑT pŋogŋaĤ.

## TƑT PROGRAM DESIGN

The Tŋaĥsitioĥ to Teachiĥg PŋogŋaĤ is a ƐƑ-Ĥoĥth iĥteĥsiŶe pŋogŋaĤ of educatioĥal couŋseŷoŋk, Ɗeld eżpeŋieĥces, aĥd a seĤesteŋ of cliĥical pŋactice ǜstudeĥt teachiĥgǝ, ŷhich, ŷheĥ successfullŽ coĤpleted, leads to a ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥ foŋ aĥ Iĥdiaĥa teachiĥg liceĥse. Couŋseŷoŋk coĥsists pŋiĤaŋilŽ of asŽĥchŋoĥous oĥliĥe iĥstŋuctioĥ. Teacheŋ caĥdidates Ĥust be aŶailable duŋiĥg the school daŽ foŋ ƐƏ-Ɛƕ ŷeeks foŋ full-tiĤe studŽ duŋiĥg studeĥt teachiĥg, ŷhich ĤaŽ be peŋĤitted to occuŋ as a paŋt of a caĥdidateǭs eĤploŽĤeĥt iĥ a K-ƐƑ settiĥg. Couŋseŷoŋk is coĤpŋessed iĥto Ĥodules thŋoughout the pŋogŋaĤ.

All couŋses aŋe iĥ aligĥĤeĥt ŷith Iĥdiaĥa Educatoŋ Staĥdaŋds ǜREPA ƒ deŶelopĤeĥtal aĥd coĥteĥt staĥdaŋdsǝ, Couĥcil foŋ the Accŋeditatioĥ of Educatoŋ Pŋepaŋatioĥ ǜCAEPǝ Staĥdaŋds, the Iĥteŋstate Neŷ Teacheŋ AssessĤeĥt aĥd Suppoŋt CoĥsoŋtiuĤ ǜIĥTASCǝ Pŋiĥciples, the Iĥteŋĥatioĥal SocietŽ foŋ TechĥologŽ iĥ Educatioĥ ǜISTEǝ Staĥdaŋds, aĥd the Iĥdiaĥa OfƊce of Educatoŋ Liceĥsiĥg.

## ƒƒƏƏ Reseaŋch-Based Readiĥg Methods: Iĥstŋuctioĥ, IĥteŋŶeĥtioĥ, &amp; AssessĤeĥt

AssessĤeĥts aligĥed ŷith ŋeadiĥg scieĥce, iĥcludiĥg oŋal ŋeadiĥg ƋueĥcŽ aĥd ĥoĥseĥse ŷoŋd ŋeadiĥg Ĥeasuŋes, aŋe adĤiĥisteŋed aĥd iĥteŋpŋeted to iĥfoŋĤ iĥitial aĥd oĥgoiĥg iĥstŋuctioĥ. Teacheŋ caĥdidates leaŋĥ a scieĥtiƊcallŽ based oĥe-oĥ-oĥe iĥteŋŶeĥtioĥ foŋ pŋiĤaŋŽ-gŋade studeĥts eżpeŋieĥciĥg difƊcultŽ leaŋĥiĥg to ŋead. The iĥteŋŶeĥtioĥ addŋesses all ƊŶe esseĥtial aŋeas of ŋeadiĥg iĥstŋuctioĥ. Caĥdidates coĥtiĥue studŽiĥg ŋeadiĥg scieĥce, iĥcludiĥg eżplicit iĥstŋuctioĥ iĥ coĤpŋeheĥsioĥ, aĥalŽsis of laĥguage aĥd teżt stŋuctuŋes, aĥd iĥstŋuctioĥal coĥteżts foŋ buildiĥg kĥoŷledge aĥd ŶocabulaŋŽ. Pŋepaŋes caĥdidates foŋ the IDOE-ŋeŊuiŋed scieĥce of ŋeadiĥg liteŋacŽ eĥdoŋseĤeĥt ǜpassiĥg scoŋe oĥ additioĥal Pŋażis eżaĤ ŋeŊuiŋedǝ. CoĤpletioĥ ŷith a gŋade of C oŋ betteŋ ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ all eleĤeĥtaŋŽ educatioĥ Ĥajoŋs. EXPECTATION Ǎ AdĤissioĥ to teacheŋ pŋepaŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ ǜTPPǝ ŋeŊuiŋed. PREREQUISITE Ǎ Ƒ.ƖƔ oŶeŋall GPAǎ EDUC ƑƑƏƏ. ## ƒƔƔƏ Iĥteŋcultuŋal Educatioĥ

ƒ hŋs. ǜƒ, Ɛǝ

Iĥtŋoduces theoŋŽ aĥd pŋactice of iĥteŋcultuŋal coĤĤuĥicatioĥ, cŋoss-cultuŋal aĥd iĥteŋĥatioĥal eżpeŋieĥces, aĥd teachiĥg ŷith a global peŋspectiŶe. Ruĥs coĥcuŋŋeĥt ŷith EDUC TRI-S paŋticipatioĥ ŷheŋe ŷoŋkiĥg ŷith childŋeĥ aĥd educatoŋs is the pŋiĤaŋŽ focus. ## ƓƘƐƏ Readiĥg Reseaŋch SeĤiĥaŋ

Ɛ hŋ. ǜƐ, Əǝ

Teacheŋ caĥdidates coĤplete oĥliĥe couŋseŷoŋk iĥ dŽsleżia scŋeeĥiĥg, ideĥtiƊcatioĥ, aĥd iĥteŋŶeĥtioĥ aĥd ŷŋite a case studŽ to deteŋĤiĥe if a studeĥt's ŋeadiĥg skills aŋe coĥsisteĥt ŷith a dŽsleżic pŋoƊle. CoĤpletioĥ ŷith a gŋade of C oŋ betteŋ ŋeŊuiŋed foŋ all eleĤeĥtaŋŽ educatioĥ Ĥajoŋs. No Ɗeld eżpeŋieĥce ŋeŊuiŋed. EXPECTATION Ǎ AdĤissioĥ to teacheŋ pŋepaŋatioĥ pŋogŋaĤ ǜTPPǝ ŋeŊuiŋed. ## ƓƑƏƏ The Pŋofessioĥ of Teachiĥg

ƒ hŋs. ǜaŋŋaĥgedǝ

Thŋough couŋseŷoŋk, teacheŋ caĥdidates ŷill deŶelop iĥsights to the cultuŋe aĥd ĥatuŋe of iĥstŋuctioĥ iĥ K-ƐƑ classŋooĤs, as ŷell as aĥ uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of hoŷ to establish a coĤĤuĥitŽ of leaŋĥeŋs thŋough gŋoup ĥoŋĤs, self-ideĥtiƊcatioĥ, aĥd discussioĥ of the ƊŶe aŋeas of holistic behaŶioŋs foŋ optiĤal pŋoductiŶitŽ. TheŽ ŷill also deŶelop aĥ uĥdeŋstaĥdiĥg of the pŋiĥciples of leaŋĥiĥg aĥd studeĥt deŶelopĤeĥt as ŋelated to plaĥĥiĥg cuŋŋiculuĤ, leaŋĥiĥg actiŶities, Ĥodes of deliŶeŋŽ, aĥd iĥstŋuctioĥal paciĥg to Ĥeet the ĥeeds of each leaŋĥeŋ. ## ASPIRE ADVISING PROGRAM

AcadeĤic adŶisiĥg at Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ is iĥtegŋal to Ǫeducatiĥg foŋ a life of faith aĥd seŋŶice iĥ the chuŋch aĥd societŽ,ǫ so the adŶisiĥg pŋogŋaĤ is about Ĥoŋe thaĥ ĤeŋelŽ selectiĥg classes foŋ aĥ upcoĤiĥg seĤesteŋ ǥ it also Ĥust help studeĥts uĥdeŋstaĥd aĥd begiĥ to puŋsue theiŋ bŋoadeŋ life puŋpose.

The heaŋt of AUǭs adŶisiĥg pŋogŋaĤ isĥǭt a checklist oŋ catalog. Itǭs the ŋelatioĥship betŷeeĥ the studeĥt aĥd his oŋ heŋ adŶisoŋ. This is a paŋtĥeŋship iĥ ŷhich both studeĥt aĥd adŶisoŋ haŶe iĤpoŋtaĥt ŋespoĥsibilities. AdŶisoŋs caĥ help guide a studeĥtǭs steps, but studeĥt success ultiĤatelŽ ŋeŊuiŋes theiŋ caŋeful thought aĥd eĥgageĤeĥt.

The Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ adŶisiĥg pŋogŋaĤ has beeĥ desigĥed to eĥcouŋage aĥd eĤpoŷeŋ studeĥts toǍ

- deŶelop aŷaŋeĥess of oppoŋtuĥities foŋ acadeĤic, peŋsoĥal aĥd pŋofessioĥal gŋoŷthǎ
- desigĥ a Ĥulti-Žeaŋ stŋategic plaĥ foŋ selectiĥg classes aĥd coĤpleĤeĥtaŋŽ oĥ- aĥd off-caĤpus actiŶities aĥd afƊliatioĥs that eĥhaĥce theiŋ leaŋĥiĥg eżpeŋieĥceǎ
- iĤpleĤeĥt theiŋ acadeĤic pŋogŋaĤ aĥd effectiŶelŽ Ĥaĥage the bŋoadeŋ aŋea of peŋsoĥal aĥd pŋofessioĥal deŶelopĤeĥtǎ aĥd
- coĥtiĥuallŽ ŋeƋect oĥ aĥd eŶaluate the appŋopŋiateĥess of theiŋ cuŋŋeĥt acadeĤic aĥd pŋofessioĥaldeŶelopĤeĥt plaĥ, aĥd ĤodifŽ the plaĥ as goals ĤaŽ chaĥge aĥd ciŋcuĤstaĥces ŋeŊuiŋe.

## Studeĥt's Role iĥ the AdŶisiĥg Pŋocess:

To get the best ŋesults, studeĥts should take aĥ actiŶe ŋole iĥ the pŋocess, keepiĥg the folloŷiĥg iĥfoŋĤatioĥ iĥ Ĥiĥd ŷheĥ doiĥg scheduliĥg oŋ otheŋ pŋogŋessioĥ plaĥĥiĥgǍ  Accept ŋespoĥsibilitŽ foŋ theiŋ acadeĤic peŋfoŋĤaĥceǎ pŋepaŋe foŋ each appoiĥtĤeĥt bŽ ŋeŶieŷiĥg pŋogŋess Ĥade, pŋepaŋiĥg the schedule theŽ thiĥk theŽǭll ĥeed, aĥd coĤpiliĥg a list of aĥŽ Ŋuestioĥs theŽ Ĥight haŶeǎ aĥd toǍ

- Accept ŋespoĥsibilitŽ foŋ decidiĥg ŷhich classes to put oĥ theiŋ scheduleǎ
- Be atteĥtiŶe to couŋse pŋeŋeŊuisites, aĥd be aŷaŋe of hoŷ theiŋ plaĥĥiĥg could be affected bŽ classes that aŋe scheduled oĥ aĥ eŶeŋŽ-otheŋ-Žeaŋ basisǎ
- Be faĤiliaŋ ŷith uĥiŶeŋsitŽ due dates, policies, aĥd pŋoceduŋes so theŽ caĥ eĥŋoll iĥ the couŋses theŽ ŷaĥt aĥd caĥ Ĥake aĥŽ chaĥges befoŋe the deadliĥes foŋ addiĥg oŋ dŋoppiĥg couŋsesǎ
- Talk ŷith theiŋ adŶisoŋ about eżtŋacuŋŋiculaŋ actiŶities, iĥteŋĥships, job pŋospects, etc., aĥd deŶelop a list of speciƊc oppoŋtuĥities theŽ Ĥight like to puŋsueǎ aĥd
- DocuĤeĥt coĤpletioĥ of pŋofessioĥal deŶelopĤeĥt eżpeŋieĥces thŋough theiŋ adŶisoŋǭs CaĥŶas adŶisiĥg page.

## AdŶisoŋ's Role iĥ the Pŋocess:

Studeĥts ĤaŽ eżpect theiŋ adŶisoŋ ǥ as theiŋ paŋtĥeŋ iĥ the adŶisiĥg pŋocess ǥ toǍ

- Be appŋoachable, listeĥ caŋefullŽ to the studeĥtǭs Ŋuestioĥs aĥd coĥceŋĥs, aĥd be ŋespoĥsiŶe to ŋeŊuests foŋ Ĥeetiĥgs aĥd assistaĥceǎ
- Uĥdeŋstaĥd aĥd eżplaiĥ hoŷ the uĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs cuŋŋiculuĤ, ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts, policies aĥd pŋoceduŋes applŽ to the studeĥtǭs acadeĤic pŋogŋaĤǎ
- PŋoŶide hoĥest guidaĥce aĥd peŋspectiŶe iĥ the deŶelopĤeĥt of attaiĥable educatioĥal aĥd pŋofessioĥal goalsǎ
- Assist iĥ eżploŋiĥg Ĥajoŋ aĥd caŋeeŋ optioĥs that aŋe iĥ keepiĥg ŷith the studeĥtǭs aptitudes, Ŷalues aĥd aŋeas of iĥteŋestǎ
- Help tŋack studeĥt pŋogŋess iĥ Ĥeetiĥg the ŋeŊuiŋeĤeĥts of theiŋ pŋogŋaĤ of studŽǎ
- Assist iĥ ideĥtifŽiĥg oppoŋtuĥities foŋ peŋsoĥal gŋoŷth, iĥcludiĥg iĥŶolŶeĤeĥt iĥ studeĥt oŋgaĥizatioĥs, iĥteŋĥships aĥd off-caĤpus pŋogŋaĤs aĥd associatioĥsǎ

- Maiĥtaiĥ stŋict coĥƊdeĥtialitŽ puŋsuaĥt to FERPA ŋegulatioĥs.

## ACADEMIC STUDENT SUCCESS COACHING

AcadeĤic coaches  ŷithiĥ the OfƊce of Educatioĥal Suppoŋt SeŋŶices ŷoŋk ŷith studeĥts aĥd studeĥt athletes ŷho aŋe eitheŋ at-ŋisk acadeĤicallŽ oŋ haŶe fouĥd theĤselŶes oĥ ǪAcadeĤic Noticeǫ puŋsuaĥt to the uĥiŶeŋsitŽǭs acadeĤic staĥdaŋds. ## ALPHA PROGRAM

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ belieŶes that all studeĥts eĥteŋiĥg the iĥstitutioĥ deseŋŶe a faiŋ chaĥce to succeed. Iĥ tuŋĥ, success depeĥds oĥ studeĥts beiĥg adeŊuatelŽ pŋepaŋed to Ĥeet the ŋigoŋs of college-leŶel studŽ. The Alpha PŋogŋaĤ is desigĥed to suppoŋt studeĥts ŷho haŶe the poteĥtial to succeed but haŶe ĥot fullŽ deŶeloped the skills ĥecessaŋŽ foŋ collegiate success.

Iĥ coĥsideŋiĥg ĥeŷ studeĥt applicatioĥs, the coĤĤittee foŋ adĤissioĥ caŋefullŽ ŋeŶieŷs seŶeŋal souŋces that seŋŶe as iĥdicatoŋs of collegiate success. Based oĥ these acadeĤic ŋecoŋds aĥd ŋecoĤĤeĥdatioĥs, the adĤissioĥ coĤĤittee ĤaŽ accept studeĥts coĥditioĥallŽ foŋ paŋticipatioĥ iĥ the Alpha pŋogŋaĤ. As paŋt of the pŋogŋaĤ, studeĥts aŋe eżpected to paŋticipate iĥ a pŋe-collegiate oŋieĥtatioĥ desigĥed to accliĤate studeĥts to caĤpus befoŋe the begiĥĥiĥg of classes. Duŋiĥg the fall seĤesteŋ, paŋticipaĥts aŋe liĤited to eĥŋolliĥg iĥ a ĤażiĤuĤ of ƐƑ-ƐƔ houŋs ǜdepeĥdiĥg oĥ the Ĥajoŋǝ. Iĥ additioĥ, Alpha studeĥts aŋe ŋeŊuiŋed to eĥŋoll iĥ LART ƐƏƐƏ ǜStŋategies foŋ AcadeĤic Successǝ, a thŋee-cŋedit-houŋ couŋse focusiĥg oĥ acadeĤic, studŽ, aĥd life skills ǜiĥcludiĥg EĤotioĥal Iĥtelligeĥce skills deŶelopĤeĥtǝ ĥecessaŋŽ foŋ success iĥ college.

## STUDENT ACCESSIBILITY SERVICES ǜSASǝ

Aĥdeŋsoĥ UĥiŶeŋsitŽ offeŋs leaŋĥiĥg-suppoŋt seŋŶices foŋ all studeĥts ŷho ŊualifŽ uĥdeŋ the AĤeŋicaĥs ŷith Disabilities Act as aĤeĥded aĥd/oŋ Sectioĥ ƔƏƓ of the Rehabilitatioĥ Act of ƐƘƖƒ. Ceŋtaiĥ accoĤĤodatioĥs aĥd aużiliaŋŽ aids/seŋŶices ĤaŽ ŋeŊuiŋe adŶaĥce ĥotice to the diŋectoŋ foŋ studeĥt accessibilitŽ seŋŶices.

The iĥstitutioĥ Ĥust be giŶeĥ a ŋeasoĥable oppoŋtuĥitŽ to eŶaluate ŋeŊuests. ReŊuests aŋe coĥsideŋed based oĥ iĥdiŶidual ĥeed. AccoĤĤodatioĥs aĥd/oŋ aużiliaŋŽ aids/seŋŶices ĤaŽ be deĥied iĥ cases that cause aĥ uĥdue buŋdeĥ to the iĥstitutioĥ oŋ that fuĥdaĤeĥtallŽ alteŋ the ĥatuŋe of the pŋogŋaĤ.

Studeĥts ŋeŊuestiĥg ŋeasoĥable accoĤĤodatioĥs aĥd/oŋ aużiliaŋŽ aids/seŋŶices should coĥtact Teŋesa Copliĥ, diŋectoŋ foŋ Studeĥt AccessibilitŽ SerŶices , Kissiĥger AcadeĤic Ceĥter for Eżcelleĥce , at ǜƖƕƔǝ ƕƓƐ-ƓƑƑƒ oŋ tjcopliĥ@aĥdersoĥ.edu .

## TRI-S GLOBAL AND STUDY-AWAY

The TRI-S aĥd StudŽ-AŷaŽ staff Ĥaiĥtaiĥ aĥd diŋect a ŷide ŋaĥge of seĤesteŋ aĥd suĤĤeŋ pŋogŋaĤs focused oĥ deŶelopiĥg iĥteŋcultuŋal coĤpeteĥce aĥd assistiĥg studeĥts iĥ iĥtegŋatiĥg aĥ iĥteŋĥatioĥal oŋ iĥteŋcultuŋal studŽ eżpeŋieĥce ŷith theiŋ degŋee pŋogŋaĤ. TheŽ also adŶise studeĥts ŋegaŋdiĥg the Ŷaŋious aspects of iĥteŋĥatioĥal aĥd iĥteŋcultuŋal studŽ, iĥcludiĥg pŋogŋaĤ selectioĥ, Ŷisas aĥd tŋaŶel docuĤeĥts, Ɗĥaĥcial aid, safetŽ aĥd secuŋitŽ issues, aĥd the tŋaĥsfeŋ of acadeĤic cŋedit. Studeĥts aŋe eĥcouŋaged to coĥtact the TRI-S aĥd StudŽ-AŷaŽ OfƊce eaŋlŽ iĥ theiŋ degŋee pŋogŋaĤ ŷheĥ coĥsideŋiĥg iĥteŋĥatioĥal oŋ iĥteŋcultuŋal studŽ oppoŋtuĥities.

TRI-S shoŋt-teŋĤ studŽ-aŷaŽ oppoŋtuĥities, seeks to eżpaĥd the college caĤpus iĥto the ŷoŋld aĥd opeĥ challeĥgiĥg aĥd stiĤulatiĥg cŋoss-cultuŋal eĥcouĥteŋs thŋough iĥteŋĥatioĥal aĥd iĥteŋcultuŋal leaŋĥiĥg aĥd seŋŶice oppoŋtuĥities. NeaŋlŽ ƒƏƏ iĥdiŶiduals aĥĥuallŽ Ŷoluĥteeŋ to build, ŋepaiŋ, paiĥt, teach, couĥsel, ŋeseaŋch, siĥg, oŋ pŋoŶide ĥuŋsiĥg seŋŶices iĥ Afŋica, Austŋalia, Asia, Euŋope, Latiĥ AĤeŋica, the Caŋibbeaĥ, aĥd the Uĥited States. These eżpeŋieĥces aŋe iĥteĥsiƊed as studeĥts ŷoŋk aĥd/oŋ liŶe ŷith iĥdiŶiduals of diffeŋeĥt cultuŋes. TRI-S pŋogŋaĤs aŋe offeŋed iĥ the suĤĤeŋ, duŋiĥg the iĥteŋĥatioĥal oppoŋtuĥitŽ betŷeeĥ seĤesteŋs, oŋ duŋiĥg spŋiĥg bŋeak ŷeek.

Additioĥal iĥfoŋĤatioĥ is aŶailable oĥ the TRI-S ŷebpage aĥd also the StudŽ AŷaŽ ŷebpage .
